- **EN.** A sequence of data points collected at successive, often equally spaced, time intervals, used to analyze temporal patterns such as crop growth.
- **ES.** Una secuencia de puntos de datos recopilados en intervalos de tiempo sucesivos, a menudo igualmente espaciados, utilizados para analizar patrones temporales como el crecimiento de cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Images](#images) — A satellite image time series combines multiple images of the same location taken at different times.
    - [Time](#time) — A time series is a sequence of data points collected at successive, often equally spaced, times.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Time series

<a id='yield'></a>
### Yield — Rendimiento
*metric* · sources: introduction · cy_poland
- **EN.** The amount of agricultural product harvested per unit area, typically expressed in kilograms per hectare or bushels per acre.
- **ES.** La cantidad de producto agrícola cosechado por unidad de área, típicamente expresada en kilogramos por hectárea o bushels por acre.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Yield is the amount of harvested crop product per unit area, typically for a specific crop.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Crop → Yield


## Level 2

<a id='accuracy'></a>
### Accuracy — Exactitud
*metric* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** A metric of how correctly a classification or estimation matches reality, typically quantified as overall accuracy and per-class user's and producer's accuracy.
- **ES.** Métrica de cuán correctamente una clasificación o estimación coincide con la realidad, típicamente cuantificada como precisión general y precisión del usuario y productor por clase.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Accuracy is computed by comparing predicted labels to known sample labels.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy

<a id='agricultural-statistics'></a>
### Agricultural Statistics — Estadísticas agrícolas
*statistic* · sources: introduction
- **EN.** Quantitative data on agricultural production, including crop area, yield, and land use, used for policy and food security monitoring.
- **ES.** Datos cuantitativos sobre la producción agrícola, incluyendo área de cultivo, rendimiento y uso del suelo, utilizados para el monitoreo de políticas y seguridad alimentaria.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Agricultural statistics quantify crop production, area, and yield using data from surveys and remote sensing.
    - [Area](#area) — Agricultural statistics include area estimates of crop cultivation derived from satellite and ground data.
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Agricultural statistics apply statistical methods to produce quantitative measures of agricultural variables.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Agricultural Statistics

<a id='agricultural-surveys'></a>
### Agricultural surveys — Encuestas agrícolas
*method* · sources: th_alignment · th_design_frames
- **EN.** Systematic data collection programs conducted by national statistical offices to gather information on crop areas, yields, and farming practices. They provide the ground-truth observations needed to train and validate remote sensing models.
- **ES.** Programas sistemáticos de recopilación de datos realizados por las oficinas nacionales de estadística para recabar información sobre áreas de cultivo, rendimientos y prácticas agrícolas. Proporcionan las observaciones de verdad terreno necesarias para entrenar y validar modelos de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Agricultural surveys provide the raw data from which official agricultural statistics are derived through statistical estimation.
    - [Survey](#survey) — Agricultural surveys are systematic survey programs that gather crop area and yield data, extending the general survey method to a specific agricultural context.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Agricultural surveys

<a id='agriculture'></a>
### Agriculture — Agricultura
*phenomenon* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The practice of cultivating land, raising crops, and livestock for food, fiber, and other products.
- **ES.** La práctica de cultivar la tierra, criar cultivos y ganado para la obtención de alimentos, fibras y otros productos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Agriculture is the practice of cultivating crops and raising livestock for food and fiber.
    - [Land](#land) — Agriculture uses land as a resource for cultivation and livestock production.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Agriculture

<a id='analysis'></a>
### Analysis — Análisis
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** The systematic examination of data to extract information, such as classifying images or estimating crop area and yield using statistical or machine-learning methods.
- **ES.** Examen sistemático de datos para extraer información, como clasificar imágenes o estimar área de cultivo y rendimiento usando métodos de aprendizaje automático.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Analysis involves systematic examination of data to extract meaningful information.
    - [Results](#results) — Results are the outputs of analysis, such as classified maps or accuracy metrics.
    - [Methods](#methods) — Analysis applies defined methods to transform data into results.
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Statistics are quantitative measures derived from data analysis, such as crop area and yield.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Analysis

<a id='analysis-ready-data'></a>
### Analysis Ready Data — Datos Listos para Análisis
*data* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** Satellite data processed to meet CEOS standards, including geometric, radiometric, and atmospheric corrections, with cloud and shadow masks, and surface reflectance values for optical sensors or GammaNought backscatter for SAR.
- **ES.** Datos satelitales procesados para cumplir con los estándares de CEOS, incluyendo correcciones geométricas, radiométricas y atmosféricas, con máscaras de nubes y sombras, y valores de reflectancia superficial para sensores ópticos o retrodispersión GammaNought para SAR.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Images](#images) — Analysis Ready Data (ARD) are satellite images that have been processed to a consistent, analysis-ready state.
    - [Processing](#processing) — ARD is produced by applying geometric, radiometric, and atmospheric corrections to raw satellite imagery.
    - [ARD image collections](#ard-image-collections) — ARD image collections are sets of satellite images processed to Analysis Ready Data standards.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Processing → Analysis Ready Data

<a id='applications'></a>
### Applications — Aplicaciones
*primitive* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** Practical uses of remote sensing data, such as crop monitoring, yield forecasting, and disaster assessment.
- **ES.** Usos prácticos de los datos de teledetección, como el monitoreo de cultivos, el pronóstico de rendimiento y la evaluación de desastres.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Methods](#methods) — Applications implement methods to solve real-world problems in agriculture and land management.
    - [Use](#use) — Applications are the practical uses of remote sensing data for specific purposes like crop monitoring.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Applications

<a id='approach'></a>
### Approach — Enfoque
*primitive* · sources: th_data_cubes#time-first-space-later
- **EN.** A methodology or strategy used to achieve a goal, such as 'time-first, space-later' or object-based image analysis.
- **ES.** Una metodología o estrategia utilizada para lograr un objetivo, como 'primero el tiempo, luego el espacio' o el análisis de imágenes basado en objetos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Methods](#methods) — An approach is a methodology or strategy used to achieve a goal within a set of methods.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Approach

<a id='area-statistics'></a>
### Area statistics — Estadísticas de área
*statistic* · sources: th_validation · crop_statistics_area
- **EN.** Quantitative measures of the spatial extent of land cover or land use categories, often derived from classified maps and used for agricultural analysis.
- **ES.** Medidas cuantitativas de la extensión espacial de categorías de cobertura o uso del suelo, a menudo derivadas de mapas clasificados y utilizadas para el análisis agrícola.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Area](#area) — Area statistics quantify the spatial extent of land cover classes from maps.
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — They use statistical methods to derive unbiased area estimates and confidence intervals.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Area statistics

<a id='big-data'></a>
### Big Data — Macrodatos
*data* · sources: introduction · introduction
- **EN.** Datasets so large or complex that traditional processing methods are insufficient. In the handbook, it refers to petabyte-scale Earth Observation archives and cloud-based services that require novel computational and statistical approaches.
- **ES.** Conjuntos de datos tan grandes o complejos que los métodos de procesamiento tradicionales son insuficientes. En el manual, se refiere a archivos de observación de la Tierra a escala de petabytes y servicios basados en la nube que requieren enfoques computacionales y estadísticos novedosos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Big data are extremely large datasets that exceed traditional processing capabilities, requiring specialized methods.
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Satellite missions generate petabytes of imagery, creating big data challenges for storage and analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Big Data

<a id='chart'></a>
### Chart — Gráfico
*primitive* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** A graphical representation of data, such as a bar chart, line plot, or confusion matrix, used to visualize results like accuracy metrics or area estimates.
- **ES.** Una representación gráfica de datos, como un gráfico de barras, un gráfico de líneas o una matriz de confusión, utilizada para visualizar resultados como métricas de precisión o estimaciones de área.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — It displays data in a graphical format, such as bar charts or line plots.
    - [Figure](#figure) — A chart is a visual element that graphically represents data trends or comparisons.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Results → Figure → Chart

<a id='classification'></a>
### Classification — Clasificación
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** The process of assigning a class label to each pixel or object in satellite imagery based on spectral, temporal, or spatial characteristics using algorithms.
- **ES.** Proceso de asignar una etiqueta de clase a cada píxel u objeto en imágenes satelitales basado en características espectrales, temporales o espaciales mediante algoritmos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — A trained classification model maps input data to class labels.
    - [Classes](#classes) — Classification assigns one of the predefined classes to each pixel or object in imagery.
    - [Samples](#samples) — Labeled samples train the classification model to recognize class patterns.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification

<a id='cloud-collections'></a>
### Cloud collections — Colecciones en la nube
*data* · sources: th_data_sources#ard-image-collections
- **EN.** Organized sets of satellite images stored on cloud platforms, often as Analysis-Ready Data (ARD), accessible via STAC protocols and services like AWS, MPC, or CDSE.
- **ES.** Conjuntos organizados de imágenes satelitales almacenados en plataformas en la nube, a menudo como datos listos para análisis, accesibles a través de protocolos STAC y servicios como AWS, MPC o CDSE.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Cloud](#cloud) — Cloud computing enables storage and retrieval of large satellite image collections as cloud collections.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Cloud collections

<a id='cloud-masking'></a>
### Cloud Masking — Enmascaramiento de nubes
*method* · sources: th_data_sources#ard-image-collections
- **EN.** Cloud masking is the process of identifying and removing pixels affected by clouds or cloud shadows in satellite imagery, often using spectral tests or pre-computed quality bands, to ensure clear observations.
- **ES.** El enmascaramiento de nubes es el proceso de identificar y eliminar píxeles afectados por nubes o sombras de nubes en imágenes satelitales, a menudo usando pruebas espectrales o bandas de calidad precalculadas, para garantizar observaciones claras.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Images](#images) — Cloud masking identifies and removes cloudy pixels in satellite images to ensure clear observations.
    - [Cloud](#cloud) — Cloud masking uses cloud detection algorithms to remove cloud-affected pixels from satellite imagery.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Cloud Masking

<a id='collection'></a>
### Collection — Colección
*method* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** A set of satellite images or other data items sharing a common source, format, and theme, often organized for access.
- **ES.** Un conjunto de imágenes satelitales u otros datos que comparten una fuente, formato y tema común, a menudo organizados para su acceso.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — A collection is a set of datasets or satellite images sharing a common source, format, and theme.
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — A collection organizes satellite images from specific missions into usable groups.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Dataset → Collection

<a id='copernicus-data-space-ecosystem'></a>
### Copernicus Data Space Ecosystem — Ecosistema del Espacio de Datos Copernicus
*organization* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** A cloud-based platform providing access to Earth observation data from the Copernicus Sentinel missions, including analysis-ready imagery and tools.
- **ES.** Una plataforma basada en la nube que proporciona acceso a datos de Observación de la Tierra de las misiones Sentinel de Copernicus, incluyendo imágenes listas para análisis y herramientas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Cloud](#cloud) — It is a cloud-based platform for storing and analyzing Earth observation data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Copernicus Data Space Ecosystem

<a id='cover'></a>
### Cover — Cobertura
*primitive* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** The observed biophysical material on Earth's surface, such as forest, water, or bare soil, measurable by satellite sensors independent of human activity.
- **ES.** El material biofísico observado en la superficie de la Tierra, como bosque, agua o suelo desnudo, medible por sensores satelitales independientemente de la actividad humana.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land](#land) — Land cover is the observed biophysical material on the Earth's surface.
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Satellite sensors measure the reflected electromagnetic radiation determining surface cover.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cover

<a id='crop-development-stage'></a>
### Crop development stage — Etapa de desarrollo del cultivo
*phenomenon* · sources: cy_colombia
- **EN.** A distinct phase in the growth cycle of a crop, from sowing to harvest, characterized by specific physiological changes.
- **ES.** Una fase distinta en el ciclo de crecimiento de un cultivo, desde la siembra hasta la cosecha, caracterizada por cambios fisiológicos específicos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Growth](#growth) — A crop development stage marks a specific period in the continuous growth of a crop.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Crop → Growth → Crop development stage

<a id='crop-types'></a>
### Crop types — Tipos de cultivos
*data* · sources: ct_poland
- **EN.** Crop types are the specific kinds of plants cultivated on agricultural land, such as maize, wheat, rice, or soybean, which are identified through remote sensing classification or field surveys.
- **ES.** Los tipos de cultivos son las especies específicas de plantas cultivadas en tierras agrícolas, como maíz, trigo, arroz o soya, que se identifican mediante clasificación por teledetección o encuestas de campo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Crop types are the specific kinds of cultivated plants, such as maize or wheat, that define the output of agricultural mapping.
    - [Type](#type) — A type is a category; crop types divide agricultural production into distinct classes for classification.
    - [Maize](#maize) — Maize is one of the main crop types studied in agricultural remote sensing.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Crop → Maize → Crop types

<a id='cropland'></a>
### Cropland — Tierras de cultivo
*phenomenon* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** Cropland is land used for cultivating crops, including both actively farmed fields and temporarily fallow areas. It is a fundamental land cover class in agricultural monitoring and crop type mapping.
- **ES.** Las tierras de cultivo son tierras utilizadas para el cultivo de cultivos, incluyendo tanto campos cultivados activamente como áreas temporalmente en barbecho. Es una clase fundamental de cobertura del suelo en el monitoreo agrícola y el mapeo de tipos de cultivo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land](#land) — Cropland is land that is used for growing crops, distinguishing it from other land cover types.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cropland

<a id='csi-image-driver'></a>
### CSI Image Driver — Controlador de imágenes CSI
*software* · sources: howto
- **EN.** A Kubernetes CSI driver that mounts OCI container images as read-only volumes. It enables fast, stateless data access by treating data artifacts like compute images, with node-level caching.
- **ES.** Un controlador CSI de Kubernetes que monta imágenes de contenedor OCI como volúmenes de solo lectura. Permite un acceso rápido y sin estado a los datos al tratar los artefactos de datos como imágenes de computación, con almacenamiento en caché a nivel de nodo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data image](#data-image) — The CSI Image Driver mounts OCI container images as read-only volumes for fast, stateless data access.
    - [Kubernetes](#kubernetes) — In a Kubernetes cluster, the CSI Image Driver exposes container images as storage volumes to pods.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Data image → CSI Image Driver

<a id='data-processing'></a>
### Data processing — Procesamiento de datos
*method* · sources: th_data_cubes · ct_poland
- **EN.** The conversion of raw satellite data into usable information through steps like geometric correction, cloud masking, and temporal compositing.
- **ES.** La conversión de datos satelitales brutos en información utilizable mediante etapas como corrección geométrica, enmascaramiento de nubes y composición temporal.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Processing](#processing) — Data processing is the generic term for the steps applied to any data, including raw satellite data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Processing → Data processing

<a id='database'></a>
### Database — Base de datos
*software* · sources: ct_poland
- **EN.** A structured collection of data, such as satellite images or ground observations, organized for efficient storage, retrieval, and analysis.
- **ES.** Colección estructurada de datos, como imágenes satelitales u observaciones de campo, organizada para el almacenamiento, recuperación y análisis eficientes.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — A database is a structured collection of datasets designed for efficient storage and retrieval.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Dataset → Database

<a id='development'></a>
### Development — Desarrollo
*primitive* · sources: crop_statistics_calibration · th_design_frames
- **EN.** The process of creating or improving methods, tools, or systems, such as developing a new crop mapping algorithm or statistical framework.
- **ES.** El proceso de crear o mejorar métodos, herramientas o sistemas, como desarrollar un nuevo algoritmo de mapeo de cultivos o marco estadístico.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Methods](#methods) — Development is the process of creating or improving analytical methods or tools.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Development

<a id='digital-elevation-model'></a>
### Digital Elevation Model — Modelo Digital de Elevación
*data* · sources: th_data_sources#copernicus-digital-elevation-model
- **EN.** A Digital Elevation Model (DEM) is a raster representation of the Earth's topographic surface, providing elevation values for each pixel, used for terrain correction and as an auxiliary feature in classification.
- **ES.** Un Modelo Digital de Elevación (MDE) es una representación ráster de la superficie topográfica de la Tierra que proporciona valores de elevación para cada píxel, utilizado para corrección del terreno y como atributo auxiliar en clasificación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Pixels](#pixels) — Digital elevation models store elevation values in each pixel, allowing slope and aspect calculations.
    - [Terrain](#terrain) — A digital elevation model is a raster representation of terrain elevation, used for topographic analysis.
    - [Topographic information](#topographic-information) — Topographic information is derived from a Digital Elevation Model, which provides elevation data for the terrain.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Digital Elevation Model

<a id='dimensional-dataset'></a>
### Dimensional dataset — Conjunto de datos dimensional
*data* · sources: th_data_cubes
- **EN.** A dimensional dataset is an Earth observation data cube organized along spatial, temporal, and spectral dimensions, providing regular grids for consistent time series analysis and machine learning classification.
- **ES.** Un conjunto de datos dimensional es un cubo de datos de observación de la Tierra organizado a lo largo de dimensiones espacial, temporal y espectral, que proporciona cuadrículas regulares para análisis consistente de series temporales y clasificación con aprendizaje automático.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Cube](#cube) — A dimensional dataset organizes Earth observation data into a multi-dimensional array called a data cube.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cube → Dimensional dataset

<a id='earth'></a>
### Earth — Tierra
*phenomenon* · sources: th_remote_sensing · introduction
- **EN.** The planet itself, often referred to in this handbook as the object of observation via satellite imagery, including its land, water, and atmosphere.
- **ES.** El planeta mismo, a menudo referido en este manual como el objeto de observación mediante imágenes satelitales, incluyendo su tierra, agua y atmósfera.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land](#land) — Earth is the planet, including its land cover and surface, as observed by satellite imagery.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Earth

<a id='earthdata'></a>
### EarthData — EarthData
*data* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** NASA's platform for discovering and accessing Earth observation data. Users must register and log in via a .netrc file to access certain collections such as Harmonized Landsat Sentinel (HLS).
- **ES.** La plataforma de la NASA para descubrir y acceder a datos de observación de la Tierra. Los usuarios deben registrarse e iniciar sesión mediante un archivo .netrc para acceder a ciertas colecciones como Landsat Sentinel Armonizado (HLS).
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Earthdatalogin](#earthdatalogin) — earthdatalogin is an R package that helps users set up credentials to access NASA Earthdata.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** .netrc file → Earthdatalogin → EarthData

<a id='entire-dataset'></a>
### Entire dataset — Conjunto de datos completo
*data* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** The complete collection of available data points used for analysis, as opposed to a subset or sample, often used for training machine learning models.
- **ES.** La colección completa de puntos de datos disponibles para el análisis, en lugar de un subconjunto o muestra, utilizada a menudo para entrenar modelos de aprendizaje automático.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — An entire dataset refers to the complete collection of all available data points.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Dataset → Entire dataset

<a id='environment'></a>
### Environment — Medio ambiente
*primitive* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The natural surroundings of Earth's surface, including land, water, and atmosphere, as observed and monitored by remote sensing satellites.
- **ES.** El entorno natural de la superficie de la Tierra, que incluye tierra, agua y atmósfera, observado y monitoreado por satélites de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land](#land) — Land is a key component of the environment monitored through satellite imagery.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Environment

<a id='estimates'></a>
### Estimates — Estimaciones
*statistic* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** Numerical approximations of population quantities, such as crop area or yield, derived from sample data and often corrected using remote sensing maps.
- **ES.** Aproximaciones numéricas de cantidades poblacionales, como el área de cultivo o el rendimiento, derivadas de datos de muestra y a menudo corregidas mediante mapas de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Statistics provides the framework for producing reliable estimates from sample data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates

<a id='example'></a>
### Example — Ejemplo
*primitive* · sources: ct_poland#introduction
- **EN.** An instance illustrating a method or result, often presented as a case study in the handbook.
- **ES.** Una instancia que ilustra un método o resultado, a menudo presentada como un estudio de caso en el manual.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Figure](#figure) — A figure is a visual element, like a diagram or map, used to illustrate concepts or results.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Results → Figure → Example

<a id='experimental-area'></a>
### Experimental Area — Área experimental
*data* · sources: ct_china#experimental-area-and-data
- **EN.** A specific geographic region selected for conducting a remote sensing study, often characterized by particular crops, climates, and agro-ecological conditions.
- **ES.** Región geográfica específica seleccionada para realizar un estudio de teledetección, a menudo caracterizada por cultivos, climas y condiciones agroecológicas particulares.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Study](#study) — This area serves as the spatial domain for a case study or pilot investigation.
    - [Study area](#study-area) — An experimental area is a specific geographic region selected for conducting a remote sensing experiment.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Study → Experimental Area

<a id='field'></a>
### Field — Campo
*phenomenon* · sources: th_parcel_extraction
- **EN.** An area of land cultivated with a single crop or managed as a unit, typically delineated as a polygon in geospatial data for analysis.
- **ES.** Un área de tierra cultivada con un solo cultivo o gestionada como una unidad, típicamente delimitada como un polígono en datos geoespaciales para análisis.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land](#land) — A field is an area of land cultivated with a single crop or managed as a unit.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field

<a id='field-surveys'></a>
### Field surveys — Encuestas de campo
*method* · sources: th_design_frames
- **EN.** Field surveys are ground-based data collection campaigns that record crop types, phenology, and other attributes at sampled locations, used to train and validate remote sensing models and produce official statistics.
- **ES.** Las encuestas de campo son campañas de recopilación de datos sobre el terreno que registran tipos de cultivo, fenología y otros atributos en ubicaciones muestreadas, utilizadas para entrenar y validar modelos de teledetección y producir estadísticas oficiales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Survey](#survey) — Field surveys are on-the-ground surveys that collect detailed crop information for training and validation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Survey → Field surveys

<a id='geometric-correction'></a>
### Geometric Correction — Corrección geométrica
*method* · sources: th_data_sources#ard-image-collections
- **EN.** Geometric correction is the process of aligning satellite imagery to a known coordinate system by removing distortions caused by sensor geometry, terrain, and Earth's rotation, ensuring accurate spatial positioning.
- **ES.** La corrección geométrica es el proceso de alinear imágenes satelitales a un sistema de coordenadas conocido eliminando distorsiones causadas por la geometría del sensor, el terreno y la rotación de la Tierra, asegurando un posicionamiento espacial preciso.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Images](#images) — Raw images from satellites often have distortions; geometric correction removes these to produce a georeferenced image.
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Geometric correction adjusts the raw coordinates of satellite imagery to align with a reference coordinate system.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Geometric Correction

<a id='georeferenced-information'></a>
### Georeferenced information — Información georreferenciada
*data* · sources: th_alignment
- **EN.** Data that has been assigned a location on the Earth's surface using a coordinate reference system, enabling spatial analysis and mapping.
- **ES.** Datos que han sido asignados a una ubicación en la superficie de la Tierra mediante un sistema de referencia de coordenadas, lo que permite el análisis espacial y la cartografía.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Information](#information) — Georeferenced information is data linked to a specific location on Earth's surface.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Information → Georeferenced information

<a id='gps'></a>
### GPS — GPS
*sensor* · sources: th_alignment
- **EN.** Global Positioning System, a satellite-based navigation system that provides precise geographic coordinates for ground control points, field sample locations, and survey points.
- **ES.** Sistema de Posicionamiento Global, un sistema de navegación basado en satélites que proporciona coordenadas geográficas precisas para puntos de control terrestre, ubicaciones de muestras de campo y puntos de encuesta.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — GPS uses a constellation of satellites to provide precise geographic coordinates for ground locations.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → GPS

<a id='grid'></a>
### Grid — Cuadrícula
*data* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** A spatial partition system, such as MGRS or WRS-2, that divides the Earth's surface into regular cells for organizing satellite imagery into analysis-ready tiles.
- **ES.** Sistema de partición espacial, como MGRS o WRS-2, que divide la superficie terrestre en celdas regulares para organizar imágenes satelitales en teselas listas para análisis.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [System](#system) — A grid is a spatial system of regular cells used to partition and index Earth observation data.
    - [Tiles](#tiles) — Tiles are the individual cells within a grid that partition satellite imagery into manageable spatial units.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Tiles → Grid

<a id='ground-survey-estimators'></a>
### Ground survey estimators — Estimadores de encuesta sobre el terreno
*statistic* · sources: crop_statistics_calibration · crop_statistics_regression
- **EN.** Statistical estimators that use data collected from ground-based surveys to produce unbiased estimates of population parameters, such as crop area.
- **ES.** Estimadores estadísticos que utilizan datos recolectados de encuestas de campo para producir estimaciones insesgadas de parámetros poblacionales, como el área de cultivo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Survey](#survey) — Ground survey estimators use data from field surveys to produce unbiased population estimates.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Survey → Ground survey estimators

<a id='handbook'></a>
### Handbook — Manual
*primitive* · sources: index · introduction
- **EN.** A practical guide that provides methodologies, case studies, and reproducible code for using remote sensing in agricultural statistics, aimed at national statistical offices and practitioners.
- **ES.** Guía práctica que proporciona metodologías, estudios de caso y código reproducible para el uso de la teledetección en estadísticas agrícolas, dirigida a oficinas nacionales de estadística y profesionales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Methods](#methods) — A handbook is a practical guide that compiles methods, case studies, and reproducible code for users.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Handbook

<a id='image-segmentation'></a>
### Image segmentation — Segmentación de imágenes
*method* · sources: th_parcel_extraction
- **EN.** The process of partitioning an image into multiple segments (sets of pixels), often used to delineate objects like agricultural field parcels by grouping spectrally similar pixels into homogeneous regions.
- **ES.** Proceso de dividir una imagen en múltiples segmentos (conjuntos de píxeles), a menudo utilizado para delinear objetos como parcelas agrícolas agrupando píxeles espectralmente similares en regiones homogéneas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Pixels](#pixels) — Image segmentation partitions an image into meaningful groups of adjacent pixels (segments).
    - [Segment Model](#segment-model) — It is designed specifically for the task of image segmentation, often using architectures like SAM.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Image segmentation

<a id='infrastructure'></a>
### Infrastructure — Infraestructura
*primitive* · sources: howto · th_data_sources
- **EN.** The underlying systems and resources needed to process and analyze Earth observation data, including cloud computing platforms, high-performance computing, data storage, and software tools.
- **ES.** Sistemas y recursos subyacentes necesarios para procesar y analizar datos de observación de la Tierra, incluyendo plataformas de computación en la nube, computación de alto rendimiento, almacenamiento de datos y herramientas de software.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Cloud](#cloud) — Infrastructure comprises cloud computing and storage systems needed to process and analyze large Earth observation data.
    - [Resources](#resources) — Resources include the infrastructure needed for processing Earth observation data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Infrastructure

<a id='instances'></a>
### Instances — Instancias
*primitive* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** Individual data points or objects in a dataset, such as a single training sample in machine learning or a single field parcel in object-based image analysis.
- **ES.** Puntos de datos u objetos individuales en un conjunto de datos, como una muestra de entrenamiento única en aprendizaje automático o una parcela de campo individual en clasificación basada en objetos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Instances are individual training or validation data points, such as a single pixel's time series.
    - [Observation](#observation) — An instance can be an observation; a collection of instances forms a dataset for machine learning.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Instances

<a id='label'></a>
### Label — Etiqueta
*data* · sources: th_quality_control · th_machine_learning
- **EN.** A categorical descriptor assigned to a sample or pixel in supervised classification, representing the land cover or crop type it belongs to.
- **ES.** Un descriptor categórico asignado a una muestra o píxel en clasificación supervisada, que representa la cobertura del suelo o el tipo de cultivo al que pertenece.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classes](#classes) — A label is the specific class assignment for a pixel or sample, using the set of classes.
    - [Samples](#samples) — Labels are assigned to each sample in the training set, providing known categories for classification.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Label

<a id='land-cover-classes'></a>
### Land cover classes — Clases de cobertura terrestre
*data* · sources: th_lucc · ct_chile
- **EN.** Categories describing the observed biophysical material on the Earth's surface, such as forest, water, or cropland. They are derived from satellite imagery and organized in hierarchical classification schemas.
- **ES.** Categorías que describen el material biofísico observado en la superficie de la Tierra, como bosque, agua o tierras de cultivo. Se derivan de imágenes satelitales y se organizan en esquemas de clasificación jerárquicos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classes](#classes) — Land cover classes are a specific set of classes that describe the observed biophysical material on Earth's surface.
    - [Land](#land) — Land cover classes categorize the Earth's surface, such as forest, water, or crop, based on satellite observations.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Land cover classes

<a id='landsat'></a>
### Landsat — Landsat
*platform* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** A series of Earth-observing satellite missions jointly managed by NASA and USGS, providing free multispectral imagery since 1972. Landsat-9 is the latest, carrying OLI-2 and TIRS-2 sensors with 30 m resolution.
- **ES.** Una serie de misiones satelitales de observación de la Tierra gestionadas conjuntamente por la NASA y el USGS, que proporcionan imágenes multiespectrales gratuitas desde 1972. Landsat-9 es el más reciente, con sensores OLI-2 y TIRS-2 y una resolución de 30 m.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Images](#images) — Landsat satellites capture images that are used for land cover and crop type mapping.
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Landsat is a series of Earth-observing satellite missions providing free multispectral imagery for land monitoring.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Landsat

<a id='landscapes'></a>
### Landscapes — Paisajes
*phenomenon* · sources: th_lucc · ct_chile
- **EN.** Geographic areas with distinctive patterns of land cover, such as agricultural fields, forests, or urban zones, which influence the spectral-temporal signatures captured by satellites.
- **ES.** Áreas geográficas con patrones distintivos de cobertura del suelo, como campos agrícolas, bosques o zonas urbanas, que influyen en las firmas espectro-temporales capturadas por satélites.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land](#land) — Landscapes are geographic areas composed of diverse land cover types such as farm fields and forests.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Landscapes

<a id='masking'></a>
### Masking — Enmascaramiento
*method* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** The process of setting certain pixels to no-data values based on criteria such as cloud cover, shadow, or non-agricultural land, to exclude them from analysis.
- **ES.** Proceso de asignar valores sin datos a ciertos píxeles basándose en criterios como cobertura de nubes, sombra o tierra no agrícola, para excluirlos del análisis.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Images](#images) — Masking removes unwanted pixels from images, such as those affected by clouds or shadows.
    - [Cloud](#cloud) — Cloud masking identifies and removes cloud-covered pixels to obtain clear observations.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Masking

<a id='methodology'></a>
### Methodology — Metodología
*method* · sources: introduction · th_validation
- **EN.** A systematic set of principles, procedures, and techniques used to conduct a study or produce statistics, ensuring reproducibility and rigor, such as the workflow for crop classification from satellite imagery.
- **ES.** Conjunto sistemático de principios, procedimientos y técnicas utilizados para realizar un estudio o producir estadísticas, garantizando reproducibilidad y rigor, como el flujo de trabajo para la clasificación de cultivos a partir de imágenes satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Methods](#methods) — Methodology is a systematic set of procedures, extending individual methods to ensure consistent and reproducible analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Methodology

<a id='monitoring'></a>
### Monitoring — Monitoreo
*method* · sources: introduction · uav_crop_growth
- **EN.** The systematic and repeated observation of a phenomenon over time to detect changes, trends, or anomalies.
- **ES.** La observación sistemática y repetida de un fenómeno a lo largo del tiempo para detectar cambios, tendencias o anomalías.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time](#time) — Monitoring involves systematic, repeated observation over time to detect changes or trends.
    - [Observation](#observation) — Monitoring relies on a series of observations at regular intervals to track conditions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Observation → Monitoring

<a id='national-datasets'></a>
### National datasets — Conjuntos de datos nacionales
*data* · sources: ct_zimbabwe
- **EN.** National datasets are collections of geospatial or statistical data covering an entire country, such as crop type maps, land cover classifications, or agricultural survey results, often produced by National Statistical Offices.
- **ES.** Los conjuntos de datos nacionales son colecciones de datos geoespaciales o estadísticos que cubren un país entero, como mapas de tipos de cultivo, clasificaciones de cobertura del suelo o resultados de encuestas agrícolas, a menudo producidos por las Oficinas Nacionales de Estadística.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — National datasets are datasets covering an entire country, so they build from the general dataset concept.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Dataset → National datasets

<a id='number'></a>
### Number — Número
*primitive* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** A mathematical object used for counting, measuring, and labeling, fundamental to statistical analysis.
- **ES.** Un objeto matemático utilizado para contar, medir y etiquetar, fundamental para el análisis estadístico.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — A number is a mathematical object fundamental to statistical analysis and quantitative measurement.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Number

<a id='oci-artifact'></a>
### OCI artifact — artefacto OCI
*phenomenon* · sources: howto · howto
- **EN.** A versioned, immutable snapshot of a chapter's data, packaged as a container image and stored in a registry. It is referenced by a content hash (SHA256) for exact reproducibility and mounted as a read-only volume in a Kubernetes session.
- **ES.** Una instantánea versionada e inmutable de los datos de un capítulo, empaquetada como imagen de contenedor y almacenada en un registro. Se referencia mediante un hash de contenido (SHA256) para garantizar la reproducibilidad exacta y se monta como un volumen de solo lectura en una sesión de Kubernetes.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Stateless data](#stateless-data) — Stateless data is managed as OCI artifacts mounted as read-only volumes, requiring no persistent storage.
    - [Container image](#container-image) — An OCI artifact is a container image packaging chapter-specific data to ensure immutability and reproducibility.
    - [Content hash](#content-hash) — OCI artifacts are identified by a content hash, enabling versioned, data integrity verification.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Container image → Stateless data → OCI artifact

<a id='patterns'></a>
### Patterns — Patrones
*primitive* · sources: ct_chile
- **EN.** Idealized approximations of the time series associated with each land cover class, derived from training data. They summarize typical temporal dynamics across spectral bands for a given class.
- **ES.** Aproximaciones idealizadas de las series temporales asociadas a cada clase de cobertura del suelo, derivadas de datos de entrenamiento. Resumen las dinámicas temporales típicas en todas las bandas espectrales para una clase determinada.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classes](#classes) — For each class, we extract a typical pattern from its training samples to represent the class signature.
    - [Time series](#time-series) — A time series reveals seasonal patterns, which we can generalize into idealized patterns for each land cover class.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Time series → Patterns

<a id='platforms'></a>
### Platforms — Plataformas
*platform* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** Cloud-based services providing access to Earth observation data and processing capabilities, such as Amazon Web Services, Microsoft Planetary Computer, and Digital Earth Africa.
- **ES.** Servicios basados en la nube que proporcionan acceso a datos de observación de la Tierra y capacidades de procesamiento, como Amazon Web Services, Microsoft Planetary Computer y Digital Earth Africa.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [System](#system) — Platforms are systems that integrate data, compute, and tools for Earth observation workflows.
    - [Cloud](#cloud) — Platforms like cloud services provide the infrastructure to access and process satellite imagery.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Platforms

<a id='plp-framework'></a>
### PLP Framework — marco PLP
*method* · sources: ad_learning
- **EN.** A digital infrastructure linking user profiles, knowledge areas, learning modules, and a course catalogue to create personalized training programs for Earth observation and agricultural statistics.
- **ES.** Infraestructura digital que vincula perfiles de usuario, áreas de conocimiento, módulos de aprendizaje y un catálogo de cursos para crear programas de capacitación personalizados en observación de la Tierra y estadísticas agrícolas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Framework](#framework) — The PLP Framework extends a structured framework by linking user profiles and learning modules to customize education.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Framework → PLP Framework

<a id='predictors'></a>
### Predictors — Predictores
*data* · sources: cy_poland
- **EN.** Variables used in a model to predict an outcome. In yield forecasting, predictors include satellite-derived vegetation indices, temperature, precipitation, and soil moisture data.
- **ES.** Variables utilizadas en un modelo para predecir un resultado. En la predicción del rendimiento, los predictores incluyen índices de vegetación derivados de satélites, datos de temperatura, precipitación y humedad del suelo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — In a model, predictors are the input variables that help forecast the outcome.
    - [Feature](#feature) — Predictors are features such as spectral bands, vegetation indices, or time series used in a model.
    - [Input](#input) — Input variables serve as predictors for a model to estimate an outcome.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Feature → Predictors

<a id='project'></a>
### Project — Proyecto
*primitive* · sources: ct_zimbabwe · ad_world_cereal
- **EN.** A planned undertaking with specific objectives, such as a national crop mapping initiative or a pilot study, often involving collaboration between statistical offices, research institutions, and international organizations.
- **ES.** Emprendimiento planificado con objetivos específicos, como una iniciativa nacional de mapeo de cultivos o un estudio piloto, que a menudo implica la colaboración entre oficinas de estadística, instituciones de investigación y organizaciones internacionales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Study](#study) — A project is a planned undertaking with specific objectives, larger than a study, often involving multiple steps.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Study → Project

<a id='quality-flags'></a>
### Quality Flags — Banderas de calidad
*data* · sources: cy_poland#modis-data
- **EN.** Quality flags are ancillary data layers in satellite products that indicate the reliability of each pixel, such as cloud cover, shadow, snow, or processing errors, used to filter out low-quality observations.
- **ES.** Las banderas de calidad son capas de datos auxiliares en productos satelitales que indican la fiabilidad de cada píxel, como cobertura de nubes, sombra, nieve o errores de procesamiento, utilizadas para filtrar observaciones de baja calidad.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Images](#images) — Satellite images often include quality bands that flag problematic pixels like clouds or shadows.
    - [Pixels](#pixels) — Quality flags are per-pixel indicators of data reliability, such as cloud or shadow presence.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Quality Flags

<a id='reference'></a>
### Reference — Referencia
*primitive* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** Reference data are ground-truth observations used to train and validate classification models. They include field surveys, photo-interpreted samples, or administrative records that provide accurate labels for land cover or crop types.
- **ES.** Los datos de referencia son observaciones de verdad terreno utilizadas para entrenar y validar modelos de clasificación. Incluyen encuestas de campo, muestras fotointerpretadas o registros administrativos que proporcionan etiquetas precisas para la cobertura del suelo o tipos de cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Labeled samples from the field form the reference dataset for training and validation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Reference

<a id='reference-datasets'></a>
### Reference datasets — Conjuntos de datos de referencia
*data* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** Collections of ground-truth observations used for training and validating classification models. They must be collected independently of the classification process and accurately labeled.
- **ES.** Colecciones de observaciones de verdad terreno utilizadas para entrenar y validar modelos de clasificación. Deben recolectarse independientemente del proceso de clasificación y etiquetarse con precisión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — They are curated datasets containing labeled samples for the study area.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Dataset → Reference datasets

<a id='remote-sensing'></a>
### Remote sensing — Teledetección
*method* · sources: th_remote_sensing · introduction
- **EN.** The science of obtaining information about objects or areas from a distance, typically from satellites or aircraft, using electromagnetic radiation.
- **ES.** La ciencia de obtener información sobre objetos o áreas a distancia, típicamente desde satélites o aeronaves, utilizando radiación electromagnética.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Remote sensing obtains information about Earth's surface from a distance, often using satellites.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing

<a id='reproducible-analysis-system'></a>
### Reproducible analysis system — Sistema de análisis reproducible
*method* · sources: howto#reproducible-analysis-system
- **EN.** A system that allows readers to launch a chapter's analysis in a one-click, pre-configured JupyterLab environment with all code, data, and dependencies ready.
- **ES.** Un sistema que permite a los lectores iniciar el análisis de un capítulo en un entorno JupyterLab preconfigurado con un solo clic, con todo el código, los datos y las dependencias listos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Chapter](#chapter) — Each chapter's analysis is delivered as a self-contained reproducible analysis system with one-click execution.
    - [Component](#component) — A component is a modular software element within the reproducible analysis system that performs a specific task.
    - [Function](#function) — A function in the system is a Dagger SDK unit that encapsulates a single build-time operation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Component → Reproducible analysis system

<a id='research'></a>
### Research — Investigación
*primitive* · sources: introduction
- **EN.** Research refers to scientific investigation conducted by academic and institutional experts to develop, test, and advance remote sensing methods for agricultural statistics, distinguishing methodological innovation from operational implementation.
- **ES.** La investigación se refiere a la investigación científica realizada por expertos académicos e institucionales para desarrollar, probar y avanzar en métodos de teledetección para estadísticas agrícolas, distinguiendo la innovación metodológica de la implementación operativa.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Study](#study) — Research advances knowledge by conducting systematic studies and experiments to develop or refine methods.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Study → Research

<a id='research-areas'></a>
### Research areas — Áreas de investigación
*data* · sources: ct_china
- **EN.** Geographic regions or thematic topics where field experiments or case studies are conducted, such as specific provinces or crop types investigated in the handbook.
- **ES.** Regiones geográficas o temas temáticos donde se realizan experimentos de campo o estudios de caso, como provincias específicas o tipos de cultivos investigados en el manual.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Area](#area) — Research areas define the spatial extent of interest for a remote sensing investigation.
    - [Study](#study) — Research areas are specific geographic or thematic domains where a study or field experiment is conducted.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Study → Research areas

<a id='resolution'></a>
### Resolution — Resolución
*metric* · sources: th_remote_sensing · uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** The level of detail in a remote sensing image, often described by the size of the ground area represented by a single pixel (spatial resolution).
- **ES.** El nivel de detalle en una imagen de teledetección, a menudo descrito por el tamaño del área terrestre representada por un solo píxel (resolución espacial).
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Pixels](#pixels) — Resolution is the level of detail in an image, often described by the ground area each pixel covers.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Resolution

<a id='satellite-image-time-series'></a>
### Satellite image time series — Series temporales de imágenes satelitales
*data* · sources: index · th_data_cubes
- **EN.** A sequence of satellite images of the same location acquired at regular intervals over time. SITS capture continuous spectral signals, enabling monitoring of ecosystem dynamics and crop phenology.
- **ES.** Secuencia de imágenes satelitales de la misma ubicación adquiridas a intervalos regulares a lo largo del tiempo. Las series temporales de imágenes satelitales capturan señales espectrales continuas, lo que permite monitorear la dinámica de los ecosistemas y la fenología de los cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Satellite image time series are sequences of satellite images of the same location acquired at regular intervals over time.
    - [Time series](#time-series) — A satellite image time series is a specific type of time series where each observation is an image capturing land surface conditions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Satellite image time series

<a id='segmentation'></a>
### Segmentation — Segmentación
*method* · sources: th_parcel_extraction · ct_mexico
- **EN.** The process of partitioning an image into meaningful regions (segments) that correspond to real-world objects, such as agricultural fields, often as a precursor to object-based classification.
- **ES.** El proceso de dividir una imagen en regiones significativas (segmentos) que corresponden a objetos del mundo real, como campos agrícolas, a menudo como precursor de la clasificación basada en objetos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Pixels](#pixels) — Segmentation partitions an image into meaningful regions by grouping adjacent pixels with similar properties.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Segmentation

<a id='source'></a>
### Source — Fuente
*primitive* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** The origin of data, such as a satellite mission (e.g., Sentinel-2) or a cloud platform (e.g., AWS).
- **ES.** El origen de los datos, como una misión satelital (p. ej., Sentinel-2) o una plataforma en la nube (p. ej., AWS).
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — A source is the origin of data, such as a satellite mission or cloud platform providing imagery.
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — A source can be a satellite sensor that acquires images for Earth observation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Source

<a id='source-datasets'></a>
### Source datasets — Conjuntos de datos fuente
*data* · sources: howto
- **EN.** Source datasets are the primary input data for remote sensing analyses, including satellite image collections, reference samples, and auxiliary geospatial layers such as elevation or land cover masks.
- **ES.** Los conjuntos de datos fuente son los datos de entrada principales para análisis de teledetección, incluyendo colecciones de imágenes satelitales, muestras de referencia y capas geoespaciales auxiliares como elevación o máscaras de cobertura del suelo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — Source datasets are the original datasets used as inputs, such as satellite imagery or survey data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Dataset → Source datasets

<a id='statistical-survey'></a>
### Statistical survey — Encuesta estadística
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_regression · th_alignment
- **EN.** A systematic method for collecting data from a sample of a population to estimate characteristics of the whole population, such as crop area or yield.
- **ES.** Un método sistemático para recopilar datos de una muestra de una población con el fin de estimar características de toda la población, como el área de cultivo o el rendimiento.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Survey](#survey) — A statistical survey is a systematic survey designed to produce quantitative estimates with known error.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Survey → Statistical survey

<a id='statisticians'></a>
### Statisticians — Estadísticos
*other* · sources: introduction
- **EN.** Professionals specialized in the theory and application of statistical methods. In the context of this handbook, they work in National Statistical Offices to produce official agricultural statistics.
- **ES.** Profesionales especializados en la teoría y aplicación de métodos estadísticos. En el contexto de este manual, trabajan en oficinas nacionales de estadística para producir estadísticas agrícolas oficiales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Statisticians are professionals who apply statistical theory to design surveys and analyze agricultural data.
    - [Experts](#experts) — They are experts who ensure that estimation methods are design-consistent and provide valid confidence intervals.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Statisticians

<a id='step'></a>
### Step — Etapa
*primitive* · sources: ct_poland
- **EN.** A single operation within a larger process, such as data acquisition, preprocessing, or classification.
- **ES.** Una operación individual dentro de un proceso más grande, como la adquisición de datos, el preprocesamiento o la clasificación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Methods](#methods) — A step is a specific procedure within a method that is executed to achieve a sub-goal.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Step

<a id='survey-records'></a>
### Survey records — Registros de encuestas
*data* · sources: th_alignment
- **EN.** Data entries collected from field surveys or administrative sources, containing information about land use, crop type, and agricultural practices at sampled locations.
- **ES.** Entradas de datos recopilados de encuestas de campo o fuentes administrativas, que contienen información sobre el uso del suelo, el tipo de cultivo y las prácticas agrícolas en ubicaciones muestreadas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Data from field questionnaires or observations are stored as survey records for analysis.
    - [Survey](#survey) — Survey records are the individual data entries collected during a systematic field survey.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Survey → Survey records

<a id='temporal-resolution'></a>
### Temporal resolution — Resolución temporal
*metric*
- **EN.** The frequency with which a satellite sensor revisits the same location on Earth, determining how often imagery is acquired for a given area over time.
- **ES.** Frecuencia con la que un sensor satelital revisita la misma ubicación en la Tierra, determinando con qué frecuencia se adquieren imágenes para un área determinada a lo largo del tiempo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time](#time) — Temporal resolution describes how frequently a satellite revisits the same location, i.e., the time between successive images.
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Temporal resolution of a satellite mission is determined by its orbit and swath, affecting the revisit frequency.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Temporal resolution

<a id='terrain-correction'></a>
### Terrain correction — Corrección del terreno
*method* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** A processing step for SAR images that corrects geometric distortions (foreshortening, layover, shadow) and radiometric variations using a digital elevation model, producing analysis-ready data.
- **ES.** Etapa de procesamiento para imágenes SAR que corrige distorsiones geométricas (acortamiento, solapamiento, sombra) y variaciones radiométricas mediante un Modelo Digital de Elevación, produciendo datos listos para análisis.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Terrain](#terrain) — Terrain correction adjusts SAR imagery for geometric distortions caused by elevation and slope.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Elevation → Terrain → Terrain correction

<a id='tools'></a>
### Tools — Herramientas
*primitive* · sources: introduction
- **EN.** Software systems, platforms, and libraries used for processing, analyzing, and classifying Earth observation data. Examples include SITS, Sen4Stat, Google Earth Engine, and Python packages.
- **ES.** Sistemas de software, plataformas y bibliotecas utilizadas para procesar, analizar y clasificar datos de observación de la Tierra. Los ejemplos incluyen SITS, Sen4Stat, Google Earth Engine y paquetes de Python.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Methods](#methods) — They operationalize methods into usable workflows for crop mapping and monitoring.
    - [Package](#package) — A package is a set of tools organized into a distributable unit for ease of use.
    - [Software](#software) — Tools are software systems that implement methods for processing and analyzing Earth observation data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Tools

<a id='training'></a>
### Training — Entrenamiento
*method* · sources: th_quality_control#outline
- **EN.** The process of fitting a machine learning model to labeled samples so it can learn to classify new data.
- **ES.** El proceso de ajustar un modelo de aprendizaje automático a muestras etiquetadas para que pueda aprender a clasificar nuevos datos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — A model is created through training on labeled data to perform tasks like classification.
    - [Samples](#samples) — Training fits a model to labeled samples so it learns to classify new data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training

<a id='values'></a>
### Values — Valores
*primitive* · sources: th_remote_sensing#introduction-to-remote-sensing-imagery
- **EN.** Numerical measurements recorded at each pixel, such as spectral reflectance or vegetation index values.
- **ES.** Mediciones numéricas registradas en cada píxel, como reflectancia espectral o valores de índices de vegetación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Pixels](#pixels) — Values are numerical measurements recorded at each pixel, such as spectral reflectance.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values

<a id='yield-forecasting'></a>
### Yield forecasting — Pronóstico de rendimiento
*method* · sources: cy_finland#introduction · cy_poland#introduction
- **EN.** The process of predicting crop yield (mass per unit area) before harvest, using satellite imagery, weather data, and/or crop models. It supports food security planning and policy decisions.
- **ES.** Proceso de predicción del rendimiento de cultivos (masa por unidad de área) antes de la cosecha, utilizando imágenes satelitales, datos meteorológicos y/o modelos de cultivo. Apoya la planificación de la seguridad alimentaria y las decisiones políticas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time series](#time-series) — Satellite image time series capture temporal crop growth patterns essential for yield forecasting models.
    - [Yield](#yield) — Yield forecasting predicts future crop yield per unit area, using historical yield data and satellite observations.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Time series → Yield forecasting


## Level 3

<a id='agricultural'></a>
### Agricultural — Agrícola
*primitive* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** Relating to the practice of farming, including cultivation of crops and rearing of animals for food and other products.
- **ES.** Relativo a la práctica de la agricultura, incluyendo el cultivo de cultivos y la cría de animales para alimento y otros productos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Agricultural Statistics](#agricultural-statistics) — Agricultural refers to the domain of farming and crop production that these statistics describe.
    - [Agriculture](#agriculture) — Agricultural is the adjective form of agriculture, the practice of cultivating land for crops.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Agricultural Statistics → Agricultural

<a id='agricultural-environmental-statistics'></a>
### Agricultural environmental statistics — Estadísticas agroambientales
*statistic* · sources: index · introduction
- **EN.** Official statistics on crop area, yield, and production, often combined with environmental data. They support food security monitoring, policy making, and sustainable development goals.
- **ES.** Estadísticas oficiales sobre área de cultivo, rendimiento y producción, a menudo combinadas con datos ambientales. Apoyan el monitoreo de la seguridad alimentaria, la formulación de políticas y los objetivos de desarrollo sostenible.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Agricultural Statistics](#agricultural-statistics) — Agricultural environmental statistics combine crop area and yield data with environmental variables for sustainability assessment.
    - [Environment](#environment) — They integrate agricultural statistics with environmental monitoring to support policy and decision-making.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Agricultural Statistics → Agricultural environmental statistics

<a id='agricultural-land-areas'></a>
### Agricultural land areas — Áreas de tierras agrícolas
*data* · sources: ct_chile
- **EN.** Portions of the Earth's surface used for crop cultivation, including arable land, pastures, and permanent crops, which are the focus of agricultural area statistics.
- **ES.** Porciones de la superficie terrestre utilizadas para el cultivo, incluyendo tierras de cultivo, pastizales y cultivos permanentes, que son el foco de las estadísticas de área agrícola.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land](#land) — Land areas dedicated to farming are agricultural land areas, classified by use and cover.
    - [Agriculture](#agriculture) — Agricultural land areas are portions of the Earth's surface used for crop cultivation and livestock.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Agriculture → Agricultural land areas

<a id='agricultural-landscapes'></a>
### Agricultural landscapes — Paisajes agrícolas
*phenomenon* · sources: th_lucc#specific-challenges-in-agricultural-classification
- **EN.** Geographic areas dominated by farming activities, characterized by a mosaic of fields with various crops, fallow land, pastures, and associated infrastructure.
- **ES.** Áreas geográficas dominadas por actividades agrícolas, caracterizadas por un mosaico de campos con diversos cultivos, barbecho, pastizales e infraestructura asociada.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Agriculture](#agriculture) — Agricultural landscapes are geographic areas dominated by farming activities and field mosaics.
    - [Landscapes](#landscapes) — These landscapes consist of patterns of agricultural fields, fallow land, and associated features.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Agriculture → Agricultural landscapes

<a id='agricultural-monitoring'></a>
### Agricultural monitoring — Monitoreo agrícola
*method* · sources: ct_poland
- **EN.** Agricultural monitoring is the systematic observation of crop growth, health, and extent over time using remote sensing and field data, supporting yield forecasting, area estimation, and early food security warning.
- **ES.** El monitoreo agrícola es la observación sistemática del crecimiento, salud y extensión de los cultivos a lo largo del tiempo mediante teledetección y datos de campo, apoyando el pronóstico de rendimiento, la estimación de área y la alerta temprana de seguridad alimentaria.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Monitoring](#monitoring) — Agricultural monitoring applies systematic observation methods to track crop conditions and changes over the growing season.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Observation → Monitoring → Agricultural monitoring

<a id='ard'></a>
### ARD — ARD
*data* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** Analysis Ready Data: satellite data processed to meet standards defined by CEOS, including geometric, radiometric, and atmospheric corrections, so that images are consistent across sensors, times, and locations, with cloud and shadow masking included; prepared for direct use in analysis without further preprocessing.
- **ES.** Datos Listos para Análisis: datos satelitales procesados para cumplir con los estándares definidos por CEOS, que incluyen correcciones geométricas, radiométricas y atmosféricas, de modo que las imágenes sean consistentes entre sensores, tiempos y ubicaciones, con enmascaramiento de nubes y sombras incluido; preparados para uso directo en análisis sin preprocesamiento adicional.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Cloud collections](#cloud-collections) — Cloud collections often consist of Analysis Ready Data (ARD) to simplify downstream processing.
    - [Radiometric corrections](#radiometric-corrections) — ARD processing includes radiometric corrections to produce consistent surface reflectance products.
    - [Analysis Ready Data](#analysis-ready-data) — ARD stands for Analysis Ready Data, which has been geometrically and radiometrically corrected.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Cloud collections → ARD

<a id='better-analytical-tools'></a>
### Better analytical tools — Mejores herramientas analíticas
*software* · sources: ct_poland · cy_poland
- **EN.** Software designed to support experts in analyzing agricultural data more effectively, improving crop classification and yield forecasting.
- **ES.** Herramientas diseñadas para ayudar a los expertos a analizar datos agrícolas de manera más efectiva, mejorando la clasificación de cultivos y el pronóstico de rendimiento.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Tools](#tools) — Better analytical tools are software systems that improve upon existing tools by adding new capabilities or efficiency.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Tools → Better analytical tools

<a id='big-data-sources'></a>
### Big Data sources — Fuentes de macrodatos
*other* · sources: introduction
- **EN.** Large and complex datasets, such as satellite imagery archives, that require specialized processing methods for analysis.
- **ES.** Conjuntos de datos grandes y complejos, como archivos de imágenes satelitales, que requieren métodos de procesamiento especializados para su análisis.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Source](#source) — Big data sources include satellite archives and public datasets that provide petabyte-scale imagery.
    - [Big Data](#big-data) — Big data sources are origins of large-scale datasets that require specialized processing methods.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Source → Big Data sources

<a id='case-studies'></a>
### Case studies — Estudios de caso
*other* · sources: introduction#purpose-of-this-handbook
- **EN.** Detailed, real-world examples of applying remote sensing methods for agricultural statistics, covering diverse regions, crops, and data sources, presented within the handbook.
- **ES.** Estudios de caso detallados y del mundo real sobre la aplicación de métodos de teledetección para estadísticas agrícolas, que cubren diversas regiones, cultivos y fuentes de datos, presentados en el manual.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Example](#example) — A case study provides a concrete instance that demonstrates the application of a methodology.
    - [Study](#study) — Case studies are detailed investigations of specific examples, illustrating methods and results.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Results → Figure → Example → Case studies

<a id='case-study'></a>
### Case study — Estudio de caso
*other*
- **EN.** A detailed examination of a specific instance or application, often used to illustrate a methodology or demonstrate practical implementation in a real-world context.
- **ES.** Un examen detallado de una instancia o aplicación específica, a menudo utilizado para ilustrar una metodología o demostrar la implementación práctica en un contexto real.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Example](#example) — A case study serves as a concrete example that illustrates how methods are applied in practice.
    - [Study](#study) — A case study is a detailed investigation of a specific instance or application within the larger study.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Results → Figure → Example → Case study

<a id='classification-accuracy'></a>
### Classification accuracy — Precisión de clasificación
*metric* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** Classification accuracy quantifies the degree to which a classification map matches reference data, measured by metrics such as overall accuracy, user's accuracy, producer's accuracy, and F1-score from a confusion matrix.
- **ES.** La precisión de clasificación cuantifica el grado en que un mapa de clasificación coincide con los datos de referencia, medido mediante métricas como la precisión general, la precisión del usuario, la precisión del productor y la puntuación F1 a partir de una matriz de confusión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Classification accuracy measures how well a classification map agrees with reference data, extending the concept of accuracy to classification tasks.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Classification accuracy

<a id='classification-map'></a>
### Classification map — Mapa de clasificación
*product* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** A classification map is a thematic raster product that assigns each pixel a land cover or land use label based on supervised or unsupervised analysis of satellite imagery.
- **ES.** Un mapa de clasificación es un producto ráster temático que asigna a cada píxel una etiqueta de cobertura del suelo o uso del suelo basada en análisis supervisado o no supervisado de imágenes satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — A classification map is a thematic map produced by applying a classification algorithm to satellite imagery.
    - [Crop type map](#crop-type-map) — A crop-type map is a classification map that focuses on differentiating crop types using spectral-temporal signatures.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Classification map

<a id='classification-systems'></a>
### Classification Systems — Sistemas de clasificación
*method* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** Structured frameworks (e.g., FAO LCCS) with rules and hierarchies for assigning semantic labels to land cover or land use. They bridge remote sensing observations and thematic information for agricultural statistics.
- **ES.** Marcos estructurados (por ejemplo, el Sistema de Clasificación de la Cobertura del Suelo de la FAO) con reglas y jerarquías para asignar etiquetas semánticas a la cobertura del suelo o al uso del suelo. Vinculan las observaciones de teledetección con la información temática para las estadísticas agrícolas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land cover classes](#land-cover-classes) — Classification systems define organized sets of land cover classes with clear boundaries and relationships.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Land cover classes → Classification Systems

<a id='classification-task'></a>
### Classification task — Tarea de clasificación
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** A specific problem in remote sensing where the goal is to assign a label, such as crop type or land cover class, to each pixel or image object.
- **ES.** Un problema específico en teledetección cuyo objetivo es asignar una etiqueta, como tipo de cultivo o clase de cobertura del suelo, a cada píxel u objeto de la imagen.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — A classification task is a specific problem where a classifier assigns labels to data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Classification task

<a id='classified-map'></a>
### Classified map — Mapa clasificado
*product* · sources: th_validation · ct_chile
- **EN.** A thematic map produced by assigning each pixel or object to a land cover or crop type class using a classification algorithm, often validated with reference data to assess accuracy.
- **ES.** Mapa temático producido al asignar cada píxel u objeto a una clase de cobertura del suelo o tipo de cultivo mediante un algoritmo de clasificación, a menudo validado con datos de referencia para evaluar la exactitud.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — A classified map is produced by assigning each pixel or object to a land cover class via classification.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Classified map

<a id='cloud-computing'></a>
### Cloud computing — Computación en la nube
*method* · sources: th_data_sources#cloud-platforms-providing-ard-data
- **EN.** A paradigm for delivering on-demand computing resources—processing, storage, and software—over the internet, enabling scalable analysis of large Earth observation datasets without local infrastructure.
