- **ES.** Un paradigma para proporcionar recursos informáticos bajo demanda—procesamiento, almacenamiento y software—a través de internet, permitiendo el análisis escalable de grandes conjuntos de datos de observación de la Tierra sin infraestructura local.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Infrastructure](#infrastructure) — Cloud computing is a type of infrastructure that delivers on-demand computing resources over the internet.
    - [Big Data](#big-data) — Cloud computing provides the scalable infrastructure needed to process and store big Earth observation data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Infrastructure → Cloud computing

<a id='cloud-shadow'></a>
### Cloud shadow — Sombra de nube
*phenomenon* · sources: th_data_sources · th_data_cubes
- **EN.** A dark area on the ground caused by a cloud blocking sunlight, which can obscure satellite imagery and must be masked during data processing.
- **ES.** Área oscura en el suelo causada por una nube que bloquea la luz solar, que puede oscurecer las imágenes satelitales y debe enmascararse durante el procesamiento de datos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Cloud](#cloud) — Cloud shadow is the dark area on the ground caused by a cloud blocking sunlight, requiring masking.
    - [Masking](#masking) — Cloud shadow is identified and removed by masking algorithms that detect adjacent dark pixels.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Masking → Cloud shadow

<a id='cloud-based-services'></a>
### Cloud-based services — Servicios basados en la nube
*software* · sources: index
- **EN.** Online platforms providing access to large petabyte-scale Earth observation data archives and computational resources for processing, analysis, and storage.
- **ES.** Plataformas en línea que proporcionan acceso a grandes archivos de datos de observación de la Tierra (a escala de petabytes) y recursos computacionales para procesamiento, análisis y almacenamiento.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Cloud](#cloud) — Cloud‑based services deliver on‑demand access to satellite data archives and computational resources via the internet.
    - [Infrastructure](#infrastructure) — Cloud‑based services provide scalable infrastructure for storing and analyzing large Earth observation datasets.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Infrastructure → Cloud-based services

<a id='continuous-monitoring'></a>
### Continuous monitoring — Monitoreo continuo
*method* · sources: th_lucc#the-key-role-of-time-series
- **EN.** The repeated, systematic observation of land surface changes over time using satellite image time series, enabling detection of events like deforestation or crop cycles.
- **ES.** Observación repetida y sistemática de los cambios en la superficie terrestre a lo largo del tiempo utilizando series temporales de imágenes satelitales, permitiendo la detección de eventos como la deforestación o los ciclos de cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time series](#time-series) — It relies on dense time series to detect subtle temporal changes over the entire season.
    - [Monitoring](#monitoring) — Continuous monitoring systematically observes land surface changes at each satellite revisit.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Observation → Monitoring → Continuous monitoring

<a id='crop-assessment'></a>
### Crop Assessment — Evaluación de cultivos
*method* · sources: ad_world_cereal#demonstration
- **EN.** The evaluation of crop condition, area, or yield, often using remote sensing, field surveys, and models, to inform agricultural decisions and food security monitoring.
- **ES.** La evaluación de la condición, área o rendimiento de los cultivos, a menudo utilizando teledetección, encuestas de campo y modelos, para informar decisiones agrícolas y el monitoreo de la seguridad alimentaria.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Crop assessment evaluates the condition, area, and yield of cultivated plants using multiple data sources.
    - [Remote sensing](#remote-sensing) — Remote sensing provides spectral and temporal data essential for crop assessment over large areas.
    - [Field surveys](#field-surveys) — Field surveys supply ground-truth measurements that validate and calibrate crop assessment models.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Crop Assessment

<a id='crop-classification'></a>
### Crop classification — Clasificación de cultivos
*method* · sources: ct_chile
- **EN.** Crop classification is the process of assigning crop type labels to satellite image pixels or field parcels using machine learning algorithms trained on reference data, enabling production of crop-type maps for agricultural statistics.
- **ES.** La clasificación de cultivos es el proceso de asignar etiquetas de tipos de cultivo a píxeles de imágenes satelitales o parcelas de campo utilizando algoritmos de aprendizaje automático entrenados con datos de referencia, lo que permite la producción de mapas de tipos de cultivo para estadísticas agrícolas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Crop classification is a type of classification that specifically assigns crop type labels using satellite imagery.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Crop classification

<a id='crop-identification'></a>
### Crop identification — Identificación de cultivos
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_area
- **EN.** The task of recognizing and labeling specific crop types from remote sensing data, often using time series of vegetation indices or radar backscatter.
- **ES.** La tarea de reconocer y etiquetar tipos de cultivos específicos a partir de datos de teledetección, a menudo utilizando series temporales de índices de vegetación o retrodispersión SAR.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Crop identification is the task of recognizing specific crop types from satellite imagery.
    - [Classification](#classification) — It uses classification methods to label pixels or fields with crop types.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Crop identification

<a id='crop-type-mapping'></a>
### Crop type mapping — Mapeo de tipos de cultivo
*method* · sources: ct_mexico
- **EN.** The process of identifying and delineating the spatial distribution of different crop types from satellite imagery.
- **ES.** El proceso de identificar y delinear la distribución espacial de diferentes tipos de cultivos a partir de imágenes satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Crop type mapping aims to delineate the spatial distribution of different crop types.
    - [Classification](#classification) — Crop type mapping is a specific classification task that identifies crop types from satellite imagery.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Crop type mapping

<a id='data-analysis'></a>
### Data Analysis — Análisis de datos
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** Data analysis involves examining, cleaning, transforming, and modeling data to discover useful information and support decision-making. In this handbook, it refers to statistical and machine learning techniques applied to satellite time series.
- **ES.** El análisis de datos implica examinar, limpiar, transformar y modelar datos para descubrir información útil y apoyar la toma de decisiones. En este manual, se refiere a técnicas estadísticas y de aprendizaje automático aplicadas a series temporales satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Data analysis systematically examines data to extract information, starting from raw factual information.
    - [Analysis](#analysis) — Data analysis is the systematic examination of data, extending the general concept of analysis to data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Analysis → Data Analysis

<a id='data-approach'></a>
### Data approach — Enfoque de datos
*method* · sources: th_data_cubes · crop_statistics_calibration
- **EN.** A strategy for handling data in analysis, such as using satellite image time series (time-first) versus single-date imagery, or combining ground surveys with remote sensing for improved estimates.
- **ES.** Estrategia para el manejo de datos en el análisis, como el uso de series temporales de imágenes satelitales (primero tiempo) frente a imágenes de una sola fecha, o la combinación de encuestas de campo con teledetección para mejorar las estimaciones.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite image time series](#satellite-image-time-series) — A data approach like 'time-first, space-later' leverages satellite image time series for classification.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Satellite image time series → Data approach

<a id='data-organization-patterns'></a>
### Data Organization Patterns — Patrones de organización de datos
*method* · sources: howto
- **EN.** Standard ways to store chapter-specific and shared data within a project. Chapter-specific data is placed in `data/<chapter>/` directories, while shared teaching artifacts are in an `etc/` directory.
- **ES.** Formas estándar de almacenar datos específicos del capítulo y compartidos dentro de un proyecto. Los datos específicos del capítulo se colocan en directorios `data/<chapter>/`, mientras que los recursos didácticos compartidos se encuentran en un directorio `etc/`.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Project](#project) — In a project, these patterns separate chapter-specific and shared data to ensure reproducibility.
    - [Database](#database) — Data organization patterns define standard ways to structure data within a database for a project.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Study → Project → Data Organization Patterns

<a id='data-scarce-regions'></a>
### Data scarce regions — Regiones con escasez de datos
*phenomenon* · sources: ad_world_cereal
- **EN.** Geographic areas with limited available reference data from field surveys, censuses, or other sources, making it difficult to train accurate machine learning models for crop mapping.
- **ES.** Áreas geográficas con datos de referencia limitados disponibles de encuestas de campo, censos u otras fuentes, lo que dificulta entrenar modelos precisos de aprendizaje automático para el mapeo de cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Regions](#regions) — Data-scarce regions are geographic areas where limited reference data from field surveys are available.
    - [Reference](#reference) — In data-scarce regions, reference data are sparse, making it difficult to train robust classification models.
    - [Field surveys](#field-surveys) — Field surveys are often insufficient in number or coverage in data-scarce regions, limiting ground truth data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Reference → Data scarce regions

<a id='design'></a>
### Design — Diseño
*method* · sources: th_design_frames
- **EN.** Design refers to the planning of sampling strategies, classification schemes, and data collection protocols to ensure statistically valid and operationally feasible agricultural statistics from Earth Observation data.
- **ES.** El diseño se refiere a la planificación de estrategias de muestreo, esquemas de clasificación y protocolos de recolección de datos para garantizar estadísticas agrícolas estadísticamente válidas y operativamente factibles a partir de datos de observación de la Tierra.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — It also outlines the classification scheme and validation protocols for a study.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design

<a id='earth-observation'></a>
### Earth Observation — observación de la Tierra
*phenomenon* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The collection of data about the Earth's surface and atmosphere using satellite-mounted sensors, enabling large-scale monitoring of land cover, vegetation, and environmental change.
- **ES.** La recolección de datos sobre la superficie y atmósfera terrestres mediante sensores montados en satélites, permitiendo el monitoreo a gran escala de la cobertura del suelo, la vegetación y el cambio ambiental.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Remote sensing](#remote-sensing) — Earth Observation is the application of remote sensing to monitor and study the planet's surface.
    - [Earth](#earth) — Earth Observation focuses on collecting data about Earth using satellite-mounted sensors.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Earth Observation

<a id='environmental-monitoring'></a>
### Environmental monitoring — Monitoreo ambiental
*method* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** The systematic observation of environmental variables such as deforestation, crop condition, and water resources using remote sensing time series to detect change over time.
- **ES.** La observación sistemática de variables ambientales como la deforestación, la condición del cultivo y los recursos hídricos mediante series temporales de teledetección para detectar cambios a lo largo del tiempo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Monitoring](#monitoring) — Environmental monitoring uses satellite time series to track changes in vegetation, water, and soil.
    - [Environment](#environment) — Environmental monitoring systematically observes natural surroundings, including land and atmosphere.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Observation → Monitoring → Environmental monitoring

<a id='errors'></a>
### Errors — Errores
*metric* · sources: th_validation · th_uncertainty
- **EN.** Mistakes in classification where pixels are either missed (omission) or incorrectly included (commission), leading to biased area estimates.
- **ES.** Errores en la clasificación donde los píxeles se omiten (omisión) o se incluyen incorrectamente (comisión), lo que lleva a estimaciones de área sesgadas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Errors in classification are the mismatches between assigned labels and true ground labels.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Errors

<a id='estimation'></a>
### Estimation — Estimación
*method* · sources: th_validation · crop_statistics_area
- **EN.** The process of inferring the value of an unknown quantity, such as crop yield or area, using statistical or machine learning methods.
- **ES.** El proceso de inferir el valor de una cantidad desconocida, como el rendimiento de cultivos o el área, utilizando métodos estadísticos o de aprendizaje automático.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Estimation uses statistical methods to infer unknown quantities like crop area from sample data.
    - [Estimates](#estimates) — Estimation is the process of deriving numerical approximations for unknown population quantities.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation

<a id='fallow'></a>
### Fallow — Barbecho
*phenomenon* · sources: th_lucc#specific-challenges-in-agricultural-classification · ct_chile#classification-scheme
- **EN.** A temporary state of agricultural land where no crop is grown, usually to allow the soil to recover moisture or nutrients. In remote sensing, fallow is a temporal phase rather than a static land cover class.
- **ES.** Estado temporal de la tierra agrícola donde no se cultiva ningún cultivo, generalmente para permitir que el suelo recupere humedad o nutrientes. En teledetección, el barbecho es una fase temporal más que una clase de cobertura del suelo estática.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Fallow land is temporarily without a crop, but remains part of agricultural land use.
    - [Cropland](#cropland) — Fallow is a state of cropland where no crop is grown, usually to allow soil recovery before the next planting season.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cropland → Fallow

<a id='food-security'></a>
### Food security — Seguridad alimentaria
*other* · sources: introduction#background · ct_china#introduction
- **EN.** The state of having reliable access to a sufficient quantity of nutritious food. Satellite-derived agricultural statistics support food security monitoring by enabling timely crop production estimates.
- **ES.** El estado de tener acceso fiable a una cantidad suficiente de alimentos nutritivos. Las estadísticas agrícolas derivadas de satélites apoyan el monitoreo de la seguridad alimentaria al permitir estimaciones oportunas de la producción de cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Satellite-based crop monitoring provides timely data to detect food shortages and support food security planning.
    - [Agricultural Statistics](#agricultural-statistics) — Agricultural statistics on crop area and yield serve as key indicators for assessing food security at regional and national levels.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Agricultural Statistics → Food security

<a id='geographic-data'></a>
### Geographic data — Datos geográficos
*data* · sources: th_design_frames#technical-suitability-of-in-situ-data
- **EN.** Data that is associated with a specific location on the Earth's surface, including satellite imagery, vector boundaries, and GPS field observations, often managed in a GIS.
- **ES.** Datos que están asociados a una ubicación específica en la superficie de la Tierra, incluyendo imágenes satelitales, límites vectoriales y observaciones de campo con GPS, a menudo gestionados en un GIS.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Geographic data is information associated with locations on the Earth's surface.
    - [Georeferenced information](#georeferenced-information) — Geographic data is essentially georeferenced information, tied to coordinates.
    - [Coordinates](#coordinates) — Geographic data often uses coordinates to define positions of features.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Information → Georeferenced information → Geographic data

<a id='geoinformatics'></a>
### Geoinformatics — Geoinformática
*other* · sources: about
- **EN.** The science and technology of acquiring, processing, analyzing, and managing geographic information, often using tools like GIS and remote sensing.
- **ES.** La ciencia y tecnología de adquirir, procesar, analizar y gestionar información geográfica, a menudo utilizando herramientas como SIG y teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Remote sensing](#remote-sensing) — It integrates remote sensing data with spatial analysis methods for Earth observation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Geoinformatics

<a id='geospatial-analysis'></a>
### Geospatial analysis — Análisis geoespacial
*method* · sources: th_design_frames
- **EN.** The process of examining, modeling, and interpreting geographic data to understand spatial patterns and relationships.
- **ES.** El proceso de examinar, modelar e interpretar datos geográficos para comprender patrones y relaciones espaciales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Georeferenced information](#georeferenced-information) — Geospatial analysis examines georeferenced information to extract patterns and relationships.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Information → Georeferenced information → Geospatial analysis

<a id='ground'></a>
### Ground — Terreno
*phenomenon* · sources: th_design_frames
- **EN.** Ground refers to in-situ observations or measurements collected on the Earth's surface, such as crop type and yield, used as reference data for calibrating and validating satellite-based products.
- **ES.** El terreno se refiere a observaciones o mediciones in situ recopiladas en la superficie de la Tierra, como tipo de cultivo y rendimiento, utilizadas como datos de referencia para calibrar y validar productos basados en satélite.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Observation](#observation) — Ground observations are measurements taken directly on the Earth's surface, such as crop type and yield data.
    - [Reference](#reference) — Reference data consists of ground observations used to label satellite image samples.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Reference → Ground

<a id='ground-surveys'></a>
### Ground surveys — Encuestas de campo
*method* · sources: th_alignment
- **EN.** Field-based data collection activities, such as measuring crop yield or recording land cover, used to train and validate remote sensing models.
- **ES.** Actividades de recolección de datos en campo, como medir el rendimiento de cultivos o registrar la cobertura del suelo, utilizadas para entrenar y validar modelos de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Field](#field) — Ground surveys visit agricultural fields to record crop types, phenology, and other attributes.
    - [Survey](#survey) — Ground surveys are field-based data collection campaigns that provide ground truth for remote sensing.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Ground surveys

<a id='harmonized-landsat-sentinel'></a>
### Harmonized Landsat Sentinel — Landsat Sentinel Armonizado
*data* · sources: th_data_sources#harmonized-landsat-sentinel
- **EN.** A NASA data product that processes and aligns Landsat 8 and Sentinel-2 imagery into a consistent, analysis-ready surface reflectance dataset.
- **ES.** Producto de datos de la NASA que procesa y alinea imágenes de Landsat 8 y Sentinel-2 en un conjunto de datos de reflectancia superficial consistente y listo para análisis.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Landsat](#landsat) — Harmonized Landsat Sentinel aligns Landsat 8 and Sentinel-2 imagery into a consistent product.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Landsat → Harmonized Landsat Sentinel

<a id='high-performance-computing'></a>
### High-performance computing — Computación de alto rendimiento
*software* · sources: cy_finland
- **EN.** Powerful computing resources (e.g., supercomputers, GPU clusters) required to process large Earth observation data volumes and run complex machine learning models efficiently.
- **ES.** Recursos informáticos potentes (por ejemplo, supercomputadoras, clústeres GPU) necesarios para procesar grandes volúmenes de datos de observación de la Tierra y ejecutar modelos de aprendizaje automático complejos de manera eficiente.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Processing](#processing) — HPC uses parallel processing and specialized hardware (e.g., GPUs) to accelerate Earth observation workflows.
    - [Big Data](#big-data) — High‑performance computing (HPC) provides the processing power needed to handle big data and complex models.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Big Data → High-performance computing

<a id='higher-classification-accuracy'></a>
### Higher classification accuracy — Mayor precisión de clasificación
*metric* · sources: th_quality_control · th_machine_learning
- **EN.** A relative measure indicating that a classification method produces fewer errors than a baseline. Practical improvements include using better training data, feature engineering, or advanced models like deep learning.
- **ES.** Medida relativa que indica que un método de clasificación produce menos errores que una línea base. Las mejoras prácticas incluyen el uso de mejores datos de entrenamiento, ingeniería de atributos o modelos avanzados como el aprendizaje profundo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Improving classification methods can yield higher classification accuracy compared to simpler models.
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Higher classification accuracy means a classification method achieves fewer errors than a baseline, often measured by overall accuracy.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Higher classification accuracy

<a id='identification'></a>
### Identification — Identificación
*method* · sources: uav_field_parcels#introduction
- **EN.** The process of recognizing and assigning a label (e.g., crop type) or detecting a feature (e.g., field parcel) from remotely sensed data, often through manual interpretation or automated algorithms.
- **ES.** El proceso de reconocer y asignar una etiqueta (por ejemplo, tipo de cultivo) o detectar una característica (por ejemplo, parcela de campo) a partir de datos de teledetección, a menudo mediante interpretación manual o algoritmos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Identification is a classification task that recognizes specific entities like crop types from satellite data.
    - [Feature](#feature) — Identification recognizes features such as crop types by analyzing their spectral or temporal patterns.
    - [Label](#label) — Identification assigns a known label to a pixel or object after analyzing its characteristics.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Identification

<a id='implementation'></a>
### Implementation — Implementación
*primitive* · sources: howto#implementation-roadmap · cy_finland#solution-architecture
- **EN.** The process of deploying a method, system, or algorithm into operational use. Implementation covers setup, execution, and integration of software and hardware components.
- **ES.** Proceso de poner en uso operativo un método, sistema o algoritmo. La implementación abarca la configuración, ejecución e integración de componentes de software y hardware.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Methods](#methods) — Implementation puts a method into practice within a specific operational context.
    - [Development](#development) — Implementation follows the development phase to deploy a system for routine use.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Development → Implementation

<a id='jupyterlab'></a>
### JupyterLab — JupyterLab
*software* · sources: howto
- **EN.** A web-based interactive development environment for Jupyter notebooks, code, and data. It enables reproducible analysis by providing a pre-configured environment with all dependencies and data ready to run.
- **ES.** Entorno de desarrollo interactivo basado en web para Jupyter Notebooks, código y datos. Permite análisis reproducible al proporcionar un entorno preconfigurado con todas las dependencias y datos listos para ejecutar.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Reproducible analysis sessions](#reproducible-analysis-sessions) — Reproducible analysis sessions are one-click JupyterLab environments pre-configured with code, data, and dependencies.
    - [Reproducible analysis system](#reproducible-analysis-system) — JupyterLab provides the interactive web-based interface for launching the reproducible analysis system.
    - [Software](#software) — JupyterLab provides a platform for interactive code development, data analysis, and visualization.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Component → Reproducible analysis system → JupyterLab

<a id='land-classes'></a>
### Land classes — Clases de tierra
*data* · sources: th_lucc · th_validation
- **EN.** The set of categories used to label areas of the Earth's surface in a classification system, such as 'Forest', 'Cropland', or 'Water'.
- **ES.** El conjunto de categorías utilizadas para etiquetar áreas de la superficie de la Tierra en un sistema de clasificación, tales como "Bosque", "Tierras de cultivo" o "Agua".
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classes](#classes) — Land classes are the set of discrete categories, such as forest or cropland, assigned to geographic areas.
    - [Land](#land) — Land classes partition the Earth's surface into categories based on its cover or use.
    - [Land cover classes](#land-cover-classes) — Land classes extend land cover classes by including land use and other classification criteria.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Land cover classes → Land classes

<a id='land-cover-mapping'></a>
### Land cover mapping — Cartografía de cobertura terrestre
*method* · sources: th_design_frames
- **EN.** The process of creating spatial datasets that depict the biophysical cover of the Earth's surface, such as forest, water, or cropland, typically using satellite imagery.
- **ES.** El proceso de crear conjuntos de datos espaciales que representan la cobertura biofísica de la superficie terrestre, como bosque, agua o tierras de cultivo, utilizando típicamente imágenes satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — It applies classification algorithms to satellite imagery to label land cover classes.
    - [LULC mapping](#land-cover-land-use-mapping) — LULC mapping extends land cover mapping by also classifying the socioeconomic function of the land.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Land cover mapping

<a id='land-preparation'></a>
### Land preparation — Preparación del terreno
*phenomenon* · sources: cy_indonesia · cy_colombia
- **EN.** The stage in crop cultivation where soil is tilled, fertilized, and otherwise prepared before sowing, typically involving plowing and leveling.
- **ES.** Etapa del cultivo en la que el suelo se labra, fertiliza y prepara antes de la siembra, que generalmente incluye arado y nivelación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Agriculture](#agriculture) — Land preparation is a key initial practice in agriculture, involving soil tillage before sowing.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Agriculture → Land preparation

<a id='land-use'></a>
### Land use — Uso del suelo
*data* · sources: th_lucc · th_lucc
- **EN.** The socioeconomic function for which land is managed, such as agriculture, forestry, or urban development. It is inferred from land cover but requires context beyond spectral signatures.
- **ES.** La función socioeconómica para la cual se gestiona la tierra, como la agricultura, la silvicultura o el desarrollo urbano. Se infiere a partir de la cobertura del suelo, pero requiere contexto más allá de las firmas espectrales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Land use mapping classifies land according to its human activities, requiring classification of land cover as a basis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Land use

<a id='large-scale-agricultural-monitoring'></a>
### Large scale agricultural monitoring — Monitoreo agrícola a gran escala
*method* · sources: introduction
- **EN.** Large-scale agricultural monitoring uses satellite imagery and automated methods to track crop conditions, planted areas, and yields across extensive regions, often at national or continental scales, supporting food security and policy decisions.
- **ES.** El monitoreo agrícola a gran escala utiliza imágenes satelitales y métodos automatizados para rastrear las condiciones de cultivos, áreas sembradas y rendimientos en regiones extensas, a menudo a escala nacional o continental, apoyando la seguridad alimentaria y las decisiones políticas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — It focuses on tracking crop conditions and extent across large agricultural areas.
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Satellites provide frequent, broad-area imagery essential for large-scale monitoring.
    - [Monitoring](#monitoring) — Large-scale agricultural monitoring extends systematic observation to regional or national levels.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Observation → Monitoring → Large scale agricultural monitoring

<a id='machine-learning'></a>
### Machine learning — Aprendizaje automático
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning · introduction
- **EN.** A branch of artificial intelligence that uses algorithms to learn patterns from data and make predictions or decisions without explicit programming for each task.
- **ES.** Una rama de la inteligencia artificial que utiliza algoritmos para aprender patrones a partir de datos y hacer predicciones o decisiones sin programación explícita para cada tarea.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Machine learning uses algorithms to learn patterns from data and make predictions or decisions.
    - [Training](#training) — Training uses machine learning algorithms to learn patterns from data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning

<a id='map'></a>
### Map — Mapa
*product* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** A thematic spatial representation, such as a crop type or land cover map, produced by classifying satellite imagery to show geographic distribution.
- **ES.** Representación espacial temática, como un mapa de tipos de cultivo o cobertura del suelo, producida clasificando imágenes satelitales para mostrar distribución geográfica.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Area](#area) — Area can be estimated by counting pixels in a classified map or summing polygon extents.
    - [Classification](#classification) — A map is the thematic output of classification, showing spatial distribution of classes.
    - [Images](#images) — A map is produced by classifying satellite images into thematic categories.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map

<a id='map-sf'></a>
### Map SF — Mapa SF
*product* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** A classified data cube that has been labeled by assigning each pixel the land cover class with the highest probability. It represents the final thematic map output.
- **ES.** Un cubo de datos clasificado que ha sido etiquetado asignando a cada píxel la clase de cobertura del suelo con mayor probabilidad. Representa el producto cartográfico temático final.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — After classification, each pixel of the cube receives a class label.
    - [Cube](#cube) — A classified data cube is labeled by selecting for each pixel the class with highest probability.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map SF

<a id='methodological-improvement'></a>
### Methodological improvement — Mejora metodológica
*method* · sources: introduction
- **EN.** Refinements to existing methods that enhance accuracy, efficiency, or applicability in agricultural statistics, such as improved sampling strategies or classification techniques.
- **ES.** Refinamientos a los métodos existentes que mejoran la exactitud, eficiencia o aplicabilidad en las estadísticas agrícolas, como estrategias de muestreo mejoradas o técnicas de clasificación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — A methodological improvement targets higher accuracy, reducing errors in classification or estimation.
    - [Methods](#methods) — A methodological improvement refines an existing method to enhance accuracy, efficiency, or applicability.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Methodological improvement

<a id='metrics'></a>
### Metrics — Métricas
*metric* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** Quantitative measures used to evaluate classification or model performance. Common examples include overall accuracy, F1-score, precision, recall, and kappa coefficient.
- **ES.** Medidas cuantitativas utilizadas para evaluar el rendimiento de la clasificación o del modelo. Los ejemplos comunes incluyen la precisión general, la puntuación F1, la precisión, la exhaustividad y el coeficiente Kappa.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Metrics are quantitative measures, such as accuracy, used to evaluate classification performance.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Metrics

<a id='military-grid-reference-system'></a>
### Military Grid Reference System — Sistema de Referencia de Cuadrícula Militar
*data* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** A global tiling system dividing the world into 60 UTM zones of 8° longitude, each split into 6° latitude blocks and further into 110×110 km tiles with 10 km overlap. Used by Sentinel-2.
- **ES.** Un sistema global de teselas que divide el mundo en 60 zonas UTM de 8° de longitud, cada una dividida en bloques de 6° de latitud y luego en teselas de 110×110 km con superposición de 10 km. Utilizado por Sentinel-2.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Grid](#grid) — MGRS is a global tiling system that divides the Earth into 60 UTM zones, each further divided into grid cells.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Tiles → Grid → Military Grid Reference System

<a id='model-accuracy'></a>
### Model accuracy — Precisión del modelo
*metric* · sources: th_validation · th_quality_control
- **EN.** A measure of how often a classification model correctly predicts the true class, often reported as overall accuracy or per-class user's and producer's accuracies.
- **ES.** Una medida de la frecuencia con la que un modelo de clasificación predice correctamente la clase verdadera, a menudo reportada como precisión general o precisiones de usuario y productor por clase.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Model accuracy is the accuracy metric applied specifically to a classification model's predictions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Model accuracy

<a id='model-training'></a>
### Model training — Entrenamiento del modelo
*method*
- **EN.** The process of fitting a machine learning algorithm to labeled data by adjusting its parameters to minimize prediction error. It requires a representative dataset and produces a model for classification or regression.
- **ES.** El proceso de ajustar un algoritmo de aprendizaje automático a datos etiquetados modificando sus parámetros para minimizar el error de predicción. Requiere un conjunto de datos representativo y produce un modelo para clasificación o regresión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — During model training, the algorithm learns to map input features to output classes using labeled samples.
    - [Training](#training) — Model training is the process of fitting a machine learning algorithm to labeled data by adjusting its parameters.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Model training

<a id='modeling'></a>
### Modeling — Modelado
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning#common-interface-to-machine-learning-and-deep-learning-models
- **EN.** The process of constructing a mathematical or computational representation, often a machine learning model, to predict a target variable from input features.
- **ES.** Proceso de construir una representación matemática o computacional, a menudo un modelo de aprendizaje automático, para predecir una variable objetivo a partir de atributos de entrada.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — Modeling is the process of constructing a mathematical or computational representation from data.
    - [Training](#training) — Modeling involves training a model on labeled samples to learn patterns.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Modeling

<a id='nasa'></a>
### NASA — NASA
*organization* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The National Aeronautics and Space Administration, the United States space agency that jointly manages the Landsat program with USGS and provides the Harmonized Landsat-Sentinel (HLS) products.
- **ES.** La Administración Nacional de Aeronáutica y el Espacio, la agencia espacial de Estados Unidos que gestiona conjuntamente el programa Landsat con el USGS y proporciona los productos Landsat Sentinel Armonizado (HLS).
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — NASA is the U.S. space agency that jointly manages Earth-observing satellite missions like Landsat.
    - [EarthData](#earthdata) — EarthData is NASA's platform for discovering and accessing Earth observation data from various missions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** .netrc file → Earthdatalogin → EarthData → NASA

<a id='near-real-time'></a>
### Near real-time — Tiempo casi real
*metric*
- **EN.** Describes data or processing that is delivered with minimal delay after acquisition, enabling timely monitoring, such as satellite imagery available within hours of acquisition.
- **ES.** Describe datos o procesamiento que se entregan con un retraso mínimo después de la adquisición, permitiendo un monitoreo oportuno, como imágenes satelitales disponibles horas después de la captura.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time](#time) — Near real‑time processing delivers data or results within a short delay after acquisition, enabling timely monitoring.
    - [Monitoring](#monitoring) — Near real‑time capability is essential for operational monitoring of crop conditions as the growing season progresses.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Observation → Monitoring → Near real-time

<a id='object-based-classification'></a>
### Object-based classification — Clasificación basada en objetos
*method* · sources: ct_mexico
- **EN.** A classification approach that analyzes image objects (segments) rather than individual pixels. Objects are created by aggregating pixels into homogeneous regions, often corresponding to real-world features like agricultural parcels.
- **ES.** Enfoque de clasificación que analiza objetos de imagen (segmentos) en lugar de píxeles individuales. Los objetos se crean agregando píxeles en regiones homogéneas, a menudo correspondientes a características del mundo real como parcelas agrícolas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Object-based classification improves upon pixel-based classification by using image objects as the unit of analysis.
    - [Segmentation](#segmentation) — Object-based classification first segments an image into objects (groups of pixels) and then classifies each object.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Object-based classification

<a id='official-agricultural-statistics'></a>
### Official agricultural statistics — Estadísticas agrícolas oficiales
*statistic* · sources: ct_chile#introduction
- **EN.** Statistical data on agricultural production, area, and yield produced and disseminated by national statistical offices, adhering to standards for timeliness, accuracy, and reliability.
- **ES.** Datos estadísticos sobre producción, área y rendimiento agrícola producidos y difundidos por las Oficinas Nacionales de Estadística, cumpliendo con estándares de puntualidad, exactitud y fiabilidad.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Official statistics ensure consistency and enable policy decisions based on rigorous statistical methods.
    - [Agricultural Statistics](#agricultural-statistics) — Official agricultural statistics are the authoritative quantitative data on farming produced by government agencies.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Agricultural Statistics → Official agricultural statistics

<a id='operational-crop-monitoring'></a>
### Operational crop monitoring — Monitoreo operativo de cultivos
*method* · sources: cy_finland · cy_poland
- **EN.** The routine, systematic use of satellite data and models to track crop conditions, area, and yield in near real-time, supporting timely agricultural statistics and food security decisions.
- **ES.** Uso rutinario y sistemático de datos satelitales y modelos para monitorear las condiciones, el área y el rendimiento de los cultivos en tiempo casi real, apoyando estadísticas agrícolas oportunas y decisiones de seguridad alimentaria.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Monitoring](#monitoring) — Operational crop monitoring applies systematic satellite observation and models routinely to track crops.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Observation → Monitoring → Operational crop monitoring

<a id='overall-accuracy'></a>
### Overall accuracy — Precisión general
*metric* · sources: th_validation · th_validation
- **EN.** The proportion of correctly classified pixels or samples out of the total, calculated as (TP + TN) / (TP + TN + FP + FN). It is a global performance metric but may be misleading for imbalanced classes.
- **ES.** La proporción de píxeles o muestras correctamente clasificados sobre el total, calculada como (VP + VN) / (VP + VN + FP + FN). Es una métrica de rendimiento global pero puede ser engañosa para clases desbalanceadas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Overall accuracy is the proportion of correctly classified pixels or samples out of the total number.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Overall accuracy

<a id='parcels'></a>
### Parcels — Parcelas
*data* · sources: ct_poland
- **EN.** Individual agricultural fields or plots, the fundamental spatial units for crop mapping and area estimation.
- **ES.** Campos o parcelas agrícolas individuales, las unidades espaciales fundamentales para el mapeo de cultivos y la estimación de área.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Field](#field) — Parcels are individual agricultural fields or plots, the fundamental spatial units for crop mapping.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Parcels

<a id='performance'></a>
### Performance — Rendimiento
*metric* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** The accuracy and reliability of a classification or estimation model, often measured by metrics like overall accuracy and F1-score.
- **ES.** La exactitud y fiabilidad de un modelo de clasificación o estimación, a menudo medida mediante la precisión general y la puntuación F1.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — Performance evaluates how well a model achieves its task using metrics like accuracy.
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Performance measures the accuracy and reliability of a classification or estimation model.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Performance

<a id='phenology'></a>
### Phenology — Fenología
*phenomenon* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** The study of recurring biological events in plant life cycles, such as emergence, flowering, and senescence, often monitored via satellite time series to track crop development.
- **ES.** Estudio de eventos biológicos recurrentes en los ciclos de vida de las plantas, como la emergencia, la floración y la senescencia, a menudo monitoreado mediante series temporales de satélite para rastrear el desarrollo del cultivo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Phenology studies the timing of recurring biological events in crop life cycles, such as flowering.
    - [Time](#time) — By observing vegetation over time, phenology tracks seasonal changes in plant development stages.
    - [Crop development stage](#crop-development-stage) — A crop development stage is a distinct phenological phase in a crop's growth cycle.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Crop → Growth → Crop development stage → Phenology

<a id='pixel-classification'></a>
### Pixel classification — Clasificación de píxeles
*method* · sources: th_data_cubes
- **EN.** Assigning a class label to each individual pixel in an image based on its spectral or temporal characteristics.
- **ES.** Asignación de una etiqueta de clase a cada píxel individual de una imagen basada en sus características espectrales o temporales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Pixel classification applies classification to each individual pixel rather than objects.
    - [Pixels](#pixels) — Pixel classification assigns a class label to every pixel based on its spectral values.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Pixel classification

<a id='precision'></a>
### Precision — Precisión
*metric* · sources: th_validation#accuracy-assessment-of-classified-images
- **EN.** In classification, the fraction of pixels predicted as a given class that actually belong to that class in the reference data.
- **ES.** En clasificación, la fracción de píxeles predichos como una clase dada que realmente pertenecen a esa clase en los datos de referencia.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Precision (user's accuracy) measures how many of the pixels predicted as a class truly belong to that class.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Precision

<a id='probability'></a>
### Probability — Probabilidad
*statistic* · sources: th_uncertainty#measuring-uncertainty
- **EN.** A numerical value between 0 and 1 representing the likelihood that a pixel belongs to a particular land cover class, as output by a classifier.
- **ES.** Un valor numérico entre 0 y 1 que representa la probabilidad de que un píxel pertenezca a una clase de cobertura terrestre particular, según la salida de un clasificador.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Values](#values) — Probability assigns a numerical value between 0 and 1 to the likelihood of an event.
    - [Set](#set) — Probability measures the chance that an element from a set belongs to a particular subset.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Probability

<a id='process'></a>
### Process — Proceso
*method* · sources: ct_poland
- **EN.** A sequence of steps designed to transform input data into a desired output, such as a crop map or yield estimate.
- **ES.** Una secuencia de etapas diseñadas para transformar datos de entrada en un resultado deseado, como un mapa de cultivos o una estimación de rendimiento.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Methods](#methods) — A process implements a method by executing its steps in a defined order.
    - [Step](#step) — A process is a sequence of steps designed to transform input data into a desired output.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Step → Process

<a id='public-datasets'></a>
### Public datasets — Conjuntos de datos públicos
*data* · sources: th_parcel_extraction
- **EN.** Data resources that are openly accessible without cost, often provided by space agencies or research organizations, such as Sentinel or Landsat imagery.
- **ES.** Recursos de datos que son de acceso abierto sin costo, a menudo proporcionados por agencias espaciales u organizaciones de investigación, como las imágenes de Sentinel o Landsat.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — Public datasets are openly available collections of satellite imagery or ground observations.
    - [Source](#source) — They come from public sources like space agencies and are free to use for research.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Source → Public datasets

<a id='quality'></a>
### Quality — Calidad
*metric* · sources: th_quality_control#outline
- **EN.** The degree to which data meet requirements for accuracy, precision, and reliability, especially for training and validation.
- **ES.** El grado en que los datos cumplen con los requisitos de exactitud, precisión y fiabilidad, especialmente para entrenamiento y validación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Quality refers to how well data meet requirements for accuracy, precision, and reliability.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Quality

<a id='quality-band'></a>
### Quality band — Banda de calidad
*data* · sources: th_data_sources · ct_china
- **EN.** A raster layer that provides per-pixel quality information (e.g., cloud presence, shadow, and sensor conditions) from satellite image products.
- **ES.** Capa ráster que proporciona información de calidad por píxel (por ejemplo, presencia de nubes, sombra y condiciones del sensor) a partir de productos de imágenes satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Quality Flags](#quality-flags) — Quality bands encode quality flags that indicate cloud, shadow, or sensor conditions per pixel.
    - [Per-pixel quality](#per-pixel-quality) — A quality band is a raster layer providing per-pixel quality information for satellite imagery.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Quality Flags → Quality band

<a id='raster'></a>
### Raster — Ráster
*data* · sources: th_parcel_extraction
- **EN.** A data structure consisting of a grid of cells (pixels) where each cell holds a value representing a measurement, such as spectral reflectance.
- **ES.** Una estructura de datos que consiste en una cuadrícula de celdas (píxeles) donde cada celda contiene un valor que representa una medición, como la reflectancia espectral.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Pixels](#pixels) — A raster is a grid of pixels where each pixel stores a value representing a measurement.
    - [Grid](#grid) — A raster organizes spatial data into a regular grid of cells (pixels) for analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Tiles → Grid → Raster

<a id='reflectance'></a>
### Reflectance — Reflectancia
*data* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The proportion of incident light that is reflected from a surface, typically expressed as a value between 0 and 1. It is a fundamental measure in remote sensing for analyzing surface properties.
- **ES.** Proporción de la luz incidente que se refleja desde una superficie, típicamente expresada como un valor entre 0 y 1. Es una medida fundamental en teledetección para analizar las propiedades de la superficie.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Values](#values) — Pixels in satellite images store digital numbers that are converted to reflectance values.
    - [Spectral reflectance](#spectral-reflectance) — Reflectance is the ratio of reflected to incident radiation, often derived from spectral reflectance.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Reflectance

<a id='reliability'></a>
### Reliability — Fiabilidad
*metric* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** The consistency and dependability of results, often assessed through accuracy, precision, and reproducibility metrics.
- **ES.** La consistencia y fiabilidad de los resultados, a menudo evaluada a través de métricas de exactitud, precisión y reproducibilidad.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Reliability extends accuracy by ensuring results are consistent and dependable over repeated applications.
    - [Consistency](#consistency) — Reliability of a method is the consistency of its results across different datasets or conditions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Reliability

<a id='remote-image-classification'></a>
### Remote image classification — Clasificación de imágenes remotas
*method* · sources: th_quality_control · th_machine_learning
- **EN.** The process of assigning semantic labels, such as crop type, to pixels in satellite imagery using algorithms trained on reference data.
- **ES.** Proceso de asignar etiquetas semánticas, como el tipo de cultivo, a píxeles en imágenes satelitales utilizando algoritmos entrenados con datos de referencia.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Remote image classification applies the general classification process to satellite imagery instead of other data.
    - [Images](#images) — Remote image classification uses satellite images as the input data to assign class labels.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Remote image classification

<a id='remote-sensing-science'></a>
### Remote Sensing Science — Ciencia de la teledetección
*other* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The scientific discipline focused on acquiring information about Earth's surface from a distance, using sensors on satellites or aircraft to measure reflected or emitted electromagnetic radiation.
- **ES.** Disciplina científica centrada en la adquisición de información sobre la superficie de la Tierra a distancia, utilizando sensores en satélites o aeronaves para medir la radiación electromagnética reflejada o emitida.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Remote sensing](#remote-sensing) — Remote sensing science is the academic discipline underlying the practice of remote sensing.
    - [Earth](#earth) — It studies Earth observation from a distance using sensors and energy interactions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Remote Sensing Science

<a id='sam'></a>
### SAM — SAM
*product* · sources: dis_china_floods
- **EN.** The Segment Anything Model, a deep learning model developed by Meta AI that can segment objects in images using prompt points, used in the TSM-SAM flood detection framework.
- **ES.** El Modelo de Segmentación de Cualquier Cosa, un modelo de aprendizaje profundo desarrollado por Meta AI que puede segmentar objetos en imágenes utilizando puntos de aviso, utilizado en el marco de detección de inundaciones TSM-SAM.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Image segmentation](#image-segmentation) — SAM (Segment Anything Model) is a deep learning model that performs image segmentation from prompts.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Image segmentation → SAM

<a id='satellite-image-classification'></a>
### Satellite image classification — Clasificación de imágenes satelitales
*method* · sources: th_lucc#problem-statement
- **EN.** The process of assigning thematic labels (e.g., crop type, land cover) to pixels or image objects based on their spectral, temporal, and spatial characteristics using algorithms.
- **ES.** El proceso de asignar etiquetas temáticas (por ejemplo, tipo de cultivo, cobertura del suelo) a píxeles u objetos de imagen basándose en sus características espectrales, temporales y espaciales mediante algoritmos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — It applies classification algorithms to satellite images to identify land cover types.
    - [Images](#images) — Satellite image classification assigns thematic labels to pixels or objects in satellite imagery.
    - [Spectral reflectance](#spectral-reflectance) — Spectral reflectance patterns from imagery are the basis for classifying satellite images.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Satellite image classification

<a id='satellite-image-collections'></a>
### Satellite image collections — Colecciones de imágenes satelitales
*data* · sources: th_data_sources#major-global-and-large-regional-cloud-providers
- **EN.** Organized archives of satellite imagery, typically provided as Analysis Ready Data (ARD) or regular data cubes, accessible via cloud platforms such as AWS, MPC, CDSE, or DEAFRICA.
- **ES.** Archivos organizados de imágenes satelitales, típicamente proporcionados como Datos Listos para Análisis (ARD) o cubos de datos regulares, accesibles a través de plataformas en la nube como AWS, MPC, CDSE o DEAFRICA.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Satellite image collections are organized archives of imagery from satellite missions.
    - [Collection](#collection) — A satellite image collection is a set of images sharing a common source, format, and theme.
    - [Cloud collections](#cloud-collections) — Cloud collections are satellite image collections stored on cloud platforms for scalable access.
    - [ARD image collections](#ard-image-collections) — Satellite image collections can be stored as ARD image collections, processed to analysis-ready standards.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Dataset → Collection → Satellite image collections

<a id='satellite-image-time-series-2'></a>
### Satellite image time series — Series temporales de imágenes satelitales
*data* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** A sequence of satellite images acquired over the same location at regular intervals, capturing spectral changes over time. SITS enables monitoring of phenology, land cover change, and crop dynamics.
- **ES.** Una secuencia de imágenes satelitales adquiridas sobre la misma ubicación en intervalos regulares, capturando cambios espectrales a lo largo del tiempo. Las SITS permiten monitorear la fenología, el cambio de cobertura del suelo y la dinámica de los cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Images](#images) — By stacking images over time, we create a satellite image time series that captures change.
    - [Satellite image time series](#satellite-image-time-series) — A satellite image time series is a sequence of satellite images of the same area acquired at regular intervals.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Satellite image time series → Satellite image time series

<a id='segment'></a>
### Segment — Segmento
*method* · sources: ct_mexico · ct_poland
- **EN.** A group of contiguous pixels representing a homogeneous area (e.g., an agricultural parcel) in object-based image analysis.
- **ES.** Un grupo de píxeles contiguos que representa un área homogénea (por ejemplo, una parcela agrícola) en el análisis de imágenes basado en objetos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Pixels](#pixels) — Segments group meaningful regions from pixels, used in object-based classification.
    - [Image segmentation](#image-segmentation) — A segment is a group of contiguous pixels produced by image segmentation, representing a homogeneous area.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Image segmentation → Segment

<a id='sensors'></a>
### Sensors — Sensores
*sensor* · sources: th_remote_sensing · th_data_sources
- **EN.** Instruments on aerial or space platforms that detect electromagnetic radiation reflected or emitted from the Earth's surface, recording it as digital imagery.
- **ES.** Instrumentos en plataformas aéreas o espaciales que detectan la radiación electromagnética reflejada o emitida desde la superficie de la Tierra, registrándola como imágenes digitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Sensors are the instruments mounted on satellites that collect imagery and other measurements.
    - [Remote sensing](#remote-sensing) — Remote sensing uses sensors on satellites or aircraft to detect electromagnetic radiation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors

<a id='soil'></a>
### Soil — Suelo
*phenomenon* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The upper layer of the earth's surface, composed of mineral particles, organic matter, water, and air, that supports plant growth.
- **ES.** La capa superior de la superficie terrestre, compuesta de partículas minerales, materia orgánica, agua y aire, que sustenta el crecimiento de las plantas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land](#land) — Soil is the upper layer of the Earth's land surface that supports plant growth.
    - [Earth](#earth) — Soil forms from the weathering of Earth's crust and organic matter decomposition.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Earth → Soil

<a id='spatial-information'></a>
### Spatial information — Información espacial
*data* · sources: th_design_frames · th_data_sources
- **EN.** Data that describes the location, shape, and relationships of features on Earth's surface, typically stored as coordinates and attributes in a GIS.
- **ES.** Datos que describen la ubicación, la forma y las relaciones de los elementos en la superficie de la Tierra, generalmente almacenados como coordenadas y atributos en un SIG.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Georeferenced information](#georeferenced-information) — Spatial information is any data referenced to locations, i.e., georeferenced information.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Information → Georeferenced information → Spatial information

<a id='strategy'></a>
### Strategy — Estrategia
*primitive* · sources: uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** A deliberate approach or set of principles guiding decisions to attain long-term objectives in agricultural statistics.
- **ES.** Un enfoque deliberado o conjunto de principios que guían las decisiones para alcanzar objetivos a largo plazo en estadísticas agrícolas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Approach](#approach) — A strategy is a high-level approach that guides decisions for achieving long-term objectives.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Approach → Strategy

<a id='temporal-compositing'></a>
### Temporal Compositing — Composición temporal
*method* · sources: th_data_cubes#generating-regular-data-cubes
- **EN.** Temporal compositing is the process of combining multiple satellite images over a specified time period into a single image by selecting the best available pixel (e.g., median, minimum cloud cover) to reduce noise and cloud interference.
- **ES.** La composición temporal es el proceso de combinar múltiples imágenes satelitales durante un período de tiempo específico en una sola imagen seleccionando el mejor píxel disponible (por ejemplo, mediana, mínima cobertura de nubes) para reducir ruido e interferencia de nubes.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time series](#time-series) — Temporal compositing merges multiple images over a time period into a single composite by selecting the best observation per pixel.
    - [Cloud Masking](#cloud-masking) — After cloud masking, temporal compositing combines clear pixels from several dates to produce a cloud-free synthesis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Cloud → Cloud Masking → Temporal Compositing

<a id='thresholding'></a>
### Thresholding — Umbralización
*method* · sources: dis_china_floods
- **EN.** A segmentation method that assigns pixels to classes based on whether their value is above or below a chosen cutoff (threshold). Multiple threshold methods can be combined for robust flood detection.
- **ES.** Un método de segmentación que asigna píxeles a clases en función de si su valor está por encima o por debajo de un umbral elegido. Se pueden combinar múltiples métodos de umbralización para una detección robusta de inundaciones.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Thresholding is a simple classification method that separates data into two groups based on a threshold value.
    - [Values](#values) — Thresholding assigns pixels to classes by comparing their values against a chosen cut‑off point.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Thresholding

<a id='time-series-analysis'></a>
### Time series analysis — Análisis de series temporales
*method* · sources: th_data_cubes#working-with-satellite-image-time-series
- **EN.** A method that examines sequential observations of the same location over time to detect temporal patterns, trends, and changes in land surface properties from satellite data.
- **ES.** Un método que examina observaciones secuenciales de la misma ubicación a lo largo del tiempo para detectar patrones temporales, tendencias y cambios en las propiedades de la superficie terrestre a partir de datos satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time](#time) — Time series analysis examines sequential data over time to detect patterns and trends.
    - [Analysis](#analysis) — Time series analysis is a systematic examination of temporal data to extract information.
    - [Time series](#time-series) — Time series analysis focuses on sequences of data points collected at successive times.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Analysis → Time series analysis

<a id='training-dataset'></a>
### Training dataset — Conjunto de datos de entrenamiento
*data* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** A training dataset is a set of labeled samples used to teach a machine learning model to recognize patterns. In remote sensing, it consists of satellite image time series with known land cover or crop type labels.
- **ES.** Un conjunto de datos de entrenamiento es un conjunto de muestras etiquetadas utilizado para enseñar a un modelo de aprendizaje automático a reconocer patrones. En teledetección, consiste en series temporales de imágenes satelitales con etiquetas conocidas de cobertura del suelo o tipo de cultivo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — A training dataset is a labeled dataset used to train models, extending the general dataset concept.
    - [Training](#training) — A training dataset is the data used during the training process of a machine learning model.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Training dataset

<a id='training-samples'></a>
### Training samples — Muestras de entrenamiento
*data* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** Labeled observations used to train machine learning models, consisting of input features and known output classes.
- **ES.** Observaciones etiquetadas utilizadas para entrenar modelos de aprendizaje automático, que consisten en atributos de entrada y clases de salida conocidas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Training samples are a subset of samples with known labels used to teach a machine learning model.
    - [Label](#label) — Training samples consist of labeled observations that guide the model during supervised learning.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Label → Training samples

<a id='validation'></a>
### Validation — Validación
*method* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** The process of assessing the accuracy of a classification or model by comparing its predictions against independent reference data.
- **ES.** El proceso de evaluar la exactitud de una clasificación o modelo comparando sus predicciones con datos de referencia independientes.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Validation assesses the accuracy of a classification by comparing its predictions against independent data.
    - [Reference](#reference) — Validation uses reference data to check if a map or model correctly reflects ground conditions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation

<a id='variability'></a>
### Variability — Variabilidad
*primitive* · sources: th_quality_control · th_uncertainty
- **EN.** The degree of variation in data, such as spectral or temporal differences within a land cover class, which affects classification accuracy and requires techniques like sample balancing.
- **ES.** Grado de variación en los datos, como diferencias espectrales o temporales dentro de una clase de cobertura del suelo, que afecta la precisión de la clasificación y requiere técnicas como el balanceo de muestra.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Values](#values) — Variability refers to the degree of spread or variation among data values, affecting classification complexity.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Variability

<a id='variance'></a>
### Variance — Varianza
*statistic* · sources: th_validation · crop_statistics_area
- **EN.** A statistical measure of the spread of a set of values around their mean. In area estimation, variance quantifies uncertainty and is used to construct confidence intervals and evaluate precision.
- **ES.** Una medida estadística de la dispersión de un conjunto de valores alrededor de su media. En la estimación de área, la varianza cuantifica la incertidumbre y se utiliza para construir intervalos de confianza y evaluar la precisión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Variance is a statistical measure of the spread of a set of values around their mean.
    - [Values](#values) — It quantifies how much individual values differ from the average of the dataset.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Variance

<a id='vegetation'></a>
### Vegetation — Vegetación
*phenomenon* · sources: th_remote_sensing#introduction-to-remote-sensing-imagery
- **EN.** Plant cover on the Earth's surface, often monitored using indices like NDVI to assess health and growth.
- **ES.** Cobertura vegetal en la superficie de la Tierra, a menudo monitoreada mediante índices como NDVI para evaluar la salud y el crecimiento.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land](#land) — Vegetation is plant cover on Earth's surface, a key land cover type monitored via remote sensing.
    - [Cover](#cover) — Vegetation is a type of cover on the Earth's surface, monitored using spectral indices.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cover → Vegetation

<a id='vegetation-monitoring'></a>
### Vegetation monitoring — Monitoreo de vegetación
*method* · sources: th_remote_sensing · cy_finland
- **EN.** The use of satellite-derived spectral indices, like NDVI, to track changes in plant health, growth, and phenology over time.
- **ES.** El uso de índices espectrales derivados de satélites, como el NDVI, para rastrear cambios en la salud de la vegetación, el crecimiento y la fenología a lo largo del tiempo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Monitoring](#monitoring) — Vegetation monitoring applies systematic repeated observation specifically to plant cover.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Observation → Monitoring → Vegetation monitoring


## Level 4

<a id='accuracy-assessment'></a>
### Accuracy assessment — Evaluación de precisión
*method* · sources: th_validation · th_validation
- **EN.** The process of evaluating the quality of a classified map by comparing it to reference data, often using metrics like overall accuracy, user's accuracy, and producer's accuracy.
- **ES.** El proceso de evaluar la calidad de un mapa clasificado comparándolo con datos de referencia, utilizando a menudo métricas como la precisión general, la precisión del usuario y la precisión del productor.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Accuracy assessment evaluates how correctly a classification assigns labels to pixels or objects.
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Accuracy assessment quantifies the overall accuracy of a classified map through comparison with reference.
    - [Validation](#validation) — Accuracy assessment uses validation data independent of training to compute error metrics.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment

<a id='agricultural-plots'></a>
### Agricultural plots — Parcelas agrícolas
*data* · sources: uav_field_parcels#introduction
- **EN.** Individual, spatially contiguous areas of land where a single crop type is grown, often the smallest unit for field data collection and analysis.
- **ES.** Áreas de tierra individuales y espacialmente contiguas donde se cultiva un solo tipo de cultivo, a menudo la unidad más pequeña para la recolección y análisis de datos de campo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Field](#field) — Agricultural plots are individual fields managed as single units for a specific crop.
    - [Parcels](#parcels) — Agricultural plots are the fundamental spatial units also known as parcels in crop mapping.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Parcels → Agricultural plots

<a id='agronomic-conditions'></a>
### Agronomic Conditions — Condiciones Agronómicas
*phenomenon* · sources: ct_chile#classification-scheme
- **EN.** Agronomic conditions refer to the set of factors affecting crop growth and management, including soil properties, climate, irrigation, fertilization, and farming practices.
- **ES.** Las Condiciones Agronómicas se refieren al conjunto de factores que afectan el crecimiento y manejo de los Cultivos, incluyendo propiedades del Suelo, Clima, riego, fertilización y prácticas agrícolas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Vegetation](#vegetation) — Agronomic conditions encompass the physical environment and plant health factors influencing crop development.
    - [Soil](#soil) — Agronomic conditions include soil properties like moisture and nutrient status that affect crop growth.
    - [Regional field experts](#regional-field-experts) — They understand agronomic conditions that influence crop growth and satellite observations.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cover → Vegetation → Agronomic Conditions

<a id='algorithm'></a>
### Algorithm — Algoritmo
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning · th_quality_control
- **EN.** A defined set of step-by-step instructions or rules designed to perform a specific task, such as classification or regression.
- **ES.** Un conjunto definido de instrucciones paso a paso o reglas diseñadas para realizar una tarea específica, como clasificación o regresión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Methods](#methods) — Methods are systematic techniques, often implemented through algorithms, for processing data.
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Machine learning involves algorithms that improve through experience with data.
    - [Step](#step) — An algorithm is a defined set of step-by-step instructions or rules designed to perform a task.
    - [Parameters](#parameters) — Parameters adjust how an algorithm runs, like the number of neighbors in a classifier.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm

<a id='anomaly-score-map'></a>
### Anomaly score map — Mapa de puntuación de anomalías
*product* · sources: dis_china_floods
- **EN.** A raster layer where each pixel represents a normalized score indicating deviation from expected patterns, used to detect unusual events like floods.
- **ES.** Una capa ráster donde cada píxel representa una puntuación normalizada que indica una desviación de los patrones esperados, utilizada para detectar eventos inusuales como inundaciones.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Map](#map) — An anomaly score map is a thematic map where each pixel shows deviation from expected patterns.
    - [Deviation](#deviation) — An anomaly score map quantifies deviation, assigning high scores to unusual observations.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Anomaly score map

<a id='area-estimation'></a>
### Area estimation — Estimación de área
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_area
- **EN.** Area estimation is a statistical method to quantify the extent of land covered by a specific crop or land use, using sample-based estimators and bias correction from confusion matrices to produce unbiased estimates with confidence intervals.
- **ES.** La estimación de área es un método estadístico para cuantificar la extensión de tierra cubierta por un cultivo o uso del suelo específico, utilizando estimadores basados en muestras y corrección de sesgo a partir de matrices de confusión para producir estimaciones insesgadas con intervalos de confianza.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Estimation](#estimation) — Area estimation applies statistical methods to estimate the spatial extent of land cover or crop types from sample data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Area estimation

<a id='basemap'></a>
### Basemap — Mapa base
*product* · sources: uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** A georeferenced image, such as an orthophoto, used as a visual reference layer on top of which other spatial data, like plot boundaries, are overlaid and digitized.
- **ES.** Una imagen georreferenciada, como una ortofoto, utilizada como capa de referencia visual sobre la cual se superponen y digitalizan otros datos espaciales, como los límites de parcelas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Map](#map) — A basemap is a georeferenced map used as a visual reference layer beneath other spatial data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Basemap

<a id='better-reference-data-series'></a>
### Better reference data series — Mejor serie de datos de referencia
*data* · sources: ct_poland
- **EN.** A set of reference data, such as field observations, that is more comprehensive, accurate, or timely than previously available, improving model training and validation.
- **ES.** Un conjunto de datos de referencia, como observaciones de campo, que es más completo, preciso u oportuno que los disponibles anteriormente, mejorando el entrenamiento y la validación del modelo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time series](#time-series) — A better reference data series may include temporal information to capture phenological patterns.
    - [Training dataset](#training-dataset) — A better reference data series serves as an improved training dataset for classification models.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Training dataset → Better reference data series

<a id='biophysical'></a>
### Biophysical — Biofísico
*phenomenon*
