- **EN.** Biophysical refers to the physical and biological properties of the Earth's surface, such as vegetation health, biomass, and leaf area index, which are measured or estimated from remote sensing data.
- **ES.** Biofísico se refiere a las propiedades físicas y biológicas de la superficie terrestre, como salud de la vegetación, biomasa e índice de área foliar, que se miden o estiman a partir de datos de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Vegetation](#vegetation) — Biophysical properties describe the physical and biological characteristics of vegetation, such as biomass and LAI.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cover → Vegetation → Biophysical

<a id='chapter-crop-classification'></a>
### Chapter Crop Classification — Capítulo Clasificación de Cultivos
*other* · sources: index
- **EN.** Any chapter in this handbook that presents a case study or methodology for identifying and mapping crop types from satellite or UAV imagery.
- **ES.** Cualquier capítulo de este manual que presente un estudio de caso o metodología para identificar y mapear tipos de cultivos a partir de imágenes satelitales o de UAV.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Chapter](#chapter) — As a handbook section, it focuses on the specific topic of crop classification.
    - [Crop classification](#crop-classification) — This chapter presents methodologies and case studies for crop classification using remote sensing.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Crop classification → Chapter Crop Classification

<a id='classification-framework'></a>
### Classification framework — Marco de clasificación
*method* · sources: th_lucc · th_lucc
- **EN.** A structured approach that defines the rules, hierarchies, and classes used to assign labels to remote sensing data based on land cover or land use.
- **ES.** Un enfoque estructurado que define las reglas, jerarquías y clases utilizadas para asignar etiquetas a datos de teledetección según la cobertura o el uso del suelo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classes](#classes) — It defines how classes are structured and related in a hierarchical system.
    - [Classification Systems](#classification-systems) — Classification systems are structured frameworks such as FAO LCCS with rules and hierarchies for assigning semantic labels to land cover.
    - [Classification scheme](#classification-scheme) — A classification framework organizes a classification scheme into rules and hierarchies.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Land cover classes → Classification Systems → Classification framework

<a id='classification-performance'></a>
### Classification performance — Rendimiento de clasificación
*metric* · sources: th_validation · th_quality_control
- **EN.** The effectiveness of a classification model, quantified by metrics such as overall accuracy and per-class user's and producer's accuracies.
- **ES.** La efectividad de un modelo de clasificación, cuantificada mediante métricas como la precisión general y las precisiones de usuario y productor por clase.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Performance](#performance) — Classification performance is the specific performance measure of a classification model or map.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Performance → Classification performance

<a id='confidence-interval'></a>
### Confidence interval — Intervalo de confianza
*statistic* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** A range of values, derived from sample data, that is likely to contain the true population parameter with a specified probability (e.g., 95%), providing a measure of estimation uncertainty.
- **ES.** Un rango de valores, derivado de datos de muestra, que probablemente contenga el verdadero parámetro de la población con una probabilidad especificada (por ejemplo, 95%), proporcionando una medida de la incertidumbre de estimación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Variance](#variance) — A confidence interval is a range around an estimate, derived from variance, that likely contains the true value.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Variance → Confidence interval

<a id='confidence-intervals'></a>
### Confidence Intervals — Intervalos de Confianza
*statistic* · sources: th_validation#accuracy-assessment-of-classified-images
- **EN.** Confidence intervals are a range of values around an estimate (e.g., area) that likely contains the true population value with a specified probability, typically 95%, reflecting sampling uncertainty.
- **ES.** Los Intervalos de Confianza son un rango de valores alrededor de una estimación (ej. área) que probablemente contiene el valor verdadero de la Población con una probabilidad especificada, típicamente 95%, reflejando la incertidumbre del muestreo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Estimates](#estimates) — Confidence intervals provide a range around an estimate that likely contains the true population value.
    - [Variance](#variance) — Confidence intervals are computed from the variance of the estimate and a chosen confidence level.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Variance → Confidence Intervals

<a id='crop-classification-models'></a>
### Crop classification models — Modelos de clasificación de cultivos
*model* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** Crop classification models are machine learning algorithms trained to identify crop types from satellite image time series. Examples include Random Forest, XGBoost, and deep learning architectures like TempCNN and ResNet.
- **ES.** Los modelos de clasificación de cultivos son algoritmos de aprendizaje automático entrenados para identificar tipos de cultivos a partir de series temporales de imágenes satelitales. Ejemplos incluyen Random Forest, XGBoost y arquitecturas de aprendizaje profundo como TempCNN y ResNet.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — These models are trained to identify specific crop types from satellite imagery.
    - [Classification](#classification) — Crop classification models are machine learning algorithms that perform classification on image data.
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Machine learning provides the algorithms that learn patterns from labeled samples.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Crop classification models

<a id='crop-yield-estimation'></a>
### Crop yield estimation — Estimación del rendimiento de cultivos
*method* · sources: cy_finland · cy_poland
- **EN.** The process of predicting the amount of crop produced per unit area, often using models that combine satellite data, weather data, and field observations.
- **ES.** El proceso de predecir la cantidad de cultivo producida por unidad de área, a menudo utilizando modelos que combinan datos satelitales, datos meteorológicos y observaciones de campo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Estimation](#estimation) — Crop yield estimation is the process of inferring yield values from satellite and ground data.
    - [Yield](#yield) — Crop yield estimation uses models to predict the amount of crop produced per unit area.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Crop yield estimation

<a id='data-division'></a>
### Data Division — División de datos
*method* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** The process of splitting a dataset into separate parts, such as training, validation, and testing sets, to develop and evaluate machine learning models.
- **ES.** El proceso de dividir un conjunto de datos en partes separadas, como conjuntos de entrenamiento, validación y prueba, para desarrollar y evaluar modelos de aprendizaje automático.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — Data division splits a dataset into training, validation, and test subsets for model development.
    - [Validation](#validation) — Data division reserves a validation set to tune model parameters and prevent overfitting.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Data Division

<a id='data-science'></a>
### Data Science — Ciencia de Datos
*primitive* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** Data science is an interdisciplinary field that uses statistical and computational methods to extract insights from data. In this handbook, it underpins machine learning and deep learning approaches for analyzing satellite image time series.
- **ES.** La Ciencia de Datos es un campo interdisciplinario que utiliza métodos estadísticos y computacionales para extraer información de los datos. En este manual, sustenta los enfoques de aprendizaje automático y aprendizaje profundo para analizar series temporales de imágenes satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Data science applies statistical and computational methods to extract insights from data.
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Data science relies on statistical principles to analyze and interpret data.
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Using machine learning algorithms, data science builds models from data for predictions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Data Science

<a id='earth-observation-integration'></a>
### Earth observation integration — integración de observación de la Tierra
*method* · sources: introduction#improving-the-use-of-eo-in-agricultural-statistics
- **EN.** The process of combining satellite-derived data with ground-based surveys and statistical methods to produce official agricultural statistics, improving accuracy and timeliness.
- **ES.** El proceso de combinar datos derivados de satélites con encuestas de campo y métodos estadísticos para producir estadísticas agrícolas oficiales, mejorando la exactitud y la oportunidad.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Earth Observation](#earth-observation) — Earth observation integration combines satellite data with other sources for comprehensive analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Earth Observation → Earth observation integration

<a id='earth-observation-classifications'></a>
### EO classifications — clasificaciones EO
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_calibration#crop-type-maps
- **EN.** Labels assigned to pixels or objects in satellite imagery based on land cover or land use, often derived from machine learning models trained on reference data.
- **ES.** Etiquetas asignadas a píxeles u objetos en imágenes satelitales basadas en la cobertura o el uso del suelo, a menudo derivadas de modelos de aprendizaje automático entrenados con datos de referencia.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — EO classifications are the labels produced by classifying satellite imagery into land cover or use categories.
    - [Earth Observation](#earth-observation) — Earth observation data are the source from which EO classifications are derived through analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Earth Observation → EO classifications

<a id='estimator'></a>
### Estimator — Estimador
*statistic* · sources: crop_statistics_area
- **EN.** A statistical rule or formula for calculating an estimate of a population parameter from sample data, such as crop area.
- **ES.** Una regla o fórmula estadística para calcular una estimación de un parámetro poblacional a partir de datos de muestra, como el área de cultivo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — An estimator uses statistical methods to infer unknown quantities like crop area or yield.
    - [Estimation](#estimation) — An estimator is a statistical rule for estimating a population parameter from sample data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator

<a id='extensive-ground-samples'></a>
### Extensive ground samples — Muestras extensivas de campo
*data* · sources: ct_china
- **EN.** Extensive ground samples refer to a large number of field observations collected across a study area to train and validate classification models, ensuring representativeness and reducing bias in crop type mapping.
- **ES.** Las muestras extensivas de campo se refieren a un gran número de observaciones de campo recolectadas en un área de estudio para entrenar y validar modelos de clasificación, asegurando representatividad y reduciendo el sesgo en el mapeo de tipos de cultivo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Extensive ground samples are a large number of labeled samples collected in the field.
    - [Ground](#ground) — Extensive ground samples are many in-situ observations, building from the ground concept of field data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Reference → Ground → Extensive ground samples

<a id='fao-land-cover-classification-system'></a>
### FAO Land Cover Classification System — Sistema de Clasificación de la Cobertura del Suelo de la FAO
*standard* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** A standardized framework by FAO for classifying land cover, using a hierarchical set of diagnostic criteria to ensure interoperability.
- **ES.** Un marco estandarizado de la FAO para clasificar la cobertura del suelo, que utiliza un conjunto jerárquico de criterios de diagnóstico para garantizar la interoperabilidad.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classes](#classes) — The FAO Land Cover Classification System defines hierarchical classes and diagnostic criteria for land cover.
    - [Land](#land) — The FAO Land Cover Classification System provides a standardized framework to classify land cover types.
    - [Classification Systems](#classification-systems) — The FAO Land Cover Classification System extends classification systems with hierarchical diagnostic criteria.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Land cover classes → Classification Systems → FAO Land Cover Classification System

<a id='fao-situ-quality-framework'></a>
### FAO situ quality framework — Marco de calidad in situ de la FAO
*organization* · sources: th_alignment
- **EN.** A framework developed by FAO to assess the compatibility of field data collected through surveys with the requirements for Earth Observation applications.
- **ES.** Un marco desarrollado por la FAO para evaluar la compatibilidad de los datos de campo recolectados mediante encuestas con los requisitos para aplicaciones de observación de la Tierra.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Ground surveys](#ground-surveys) — The FAO situ quality framework provides criteria for evaluating ground survey data quality.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Ground surveys → FAO situ quality framework

<a id='field-data-collection'></a>
### Field data collection — Recolección de datos de campo
*method* · sources: th_alignment · th_design_frames
- **EN.** The process of gathering ground observations such as crop type, GPS coordinates, and phenological stage, used for training and validating remote sensing models. Quality protocols ensure fitness for Earth observation use.
- **ES.** El proceso de recopilar observaciones de campo como tipo de cultivo, coordenadas GPS y etapa fenológica, utilizado para entrenar y validar modelos de teledetección. Los protocolos de calidad garantizan la idoneidad para el uso en observación de la Tierra.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Field](#field) — Field data collection involves gathering ground observations such as crop type and GPS coordinates from agricultural fields.
    - [Ground surveys](#ground-surveys) — It is a systematic process of recording ground surveys to provide reference data for remote sensing analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Ground surveys → Field data collection

<a id='field-samples'></a>
### Field samples — Muestras de campo
*data* · sources: th_quality_control · th_design_frames
- **EN.** Data or observations collected directly from agricultural fields, used as ground truth for training and validating remote sensing models.
- **ES.** Datos u observaciones recolectados directamente de campos agrícolas, utilizados como verdad terreno para entrenar y validar modelos de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Field samples are samples collected directly from agricultural fields during ground surveys.
    - [Field](#field) — Field samples are taken from individual fields, representing specific crop types and conditions.
    - [Ground surveys](#ground-surveys) — Field samples are the primary output of ground surveys, used for training and validation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Ground surveys → Field samples

<a id='geographic-distribution'></a>
### Geographic distribution — Distribución geográfica
*phenomenon*
- **EN.** The spatial arrangement or spread of features, such as crop types or land cover classes, across a geographic area, analyzed to identify patterns and variability.
- **ES.** La disposición espacial o extensión de características, como tipos de cultivos o clases de cobertura del suelo, a través de un área geográfica, analizada para identificar patrones y variabilidad.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Area](#area) — Geographic distribution describes how a variable's values are spread across spatial coordinates within a region.
    - [Map](#map) — A map visually displays the geographic distribution by showing where each class or measurement occurs.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Geographic distribution

<a id='geographic-information-systems'></a>
### Geographic information systems — Sistemas de información geográfica
*software* · sources: ad_learning · th_design_frames
- **EN.** Computer systems for capturing, storing, analyzing, and displaying geospatial data. NSOs use them to manage satellite imagery, field boundaries, and sampling frames for agricultural statistics.
- **ES.** Sistemas informáticos para capturar, almacenar, analizar y mostrar datos geoespaciales. Las ONE los utilizan para gestionar imágenes satelitales, límites de campos y marcos de muestreo para estadísticas agrícolas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Geographic information systems are computer systems that capture, store, analyze, and display geospatial data.
    - [Georeferenced information](#georeferenced-information) — GIS integrates georeferenced information layers such as satellite imagery, field boundaries, and survey records.
    - [Geoinformatics](#geoinformatics) — Geoinformatics encompasses GIS and other geospatial technologies for analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Geoinformatics → Geographic information systems

<a id='geoinformation'></a>
### Geoinformation — Geoinformación
*data* · sources: about
- **EN.** Information about objects or phenomena on the Earth's surface that is associated with a specific geographic location, often stored in a GIS.
- **ES.** Información sobre objetos o fenómenos en la superficie de la Tierra que está asociada a una ubicación geográfica específica, a menudo almacenada en un SIG.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Information](#information) — Geoinformation is information that has geographic location and attributes derived from Earth observation.
    - [Geoinformatics](#geoinformatics) — Geoinformation is the output produced by geoinformatics; it is geographic data with meaning.
    - [Spatial information](#spatial-information) — Geoinformation is a type of spatial information specifically focused on Earth surface features.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Geoinformatics → Geoinformation

<a id='geospatial-data'></a>
### Geospatial Data — Datos geoespaciales
*data* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** Data that contains geographic location information, such as satellite images or vector boundaries, referenced to a coordinate system and used for spatial analysis.
- **ES.** Datos que contienen información de ubicación geográfica, como imágenes satelitales o límites vectoriales, referenciados a un sistema de coordenadas y utilizados para análisis espacial.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Geospatial data is any data that includes geographic location information.
    - [Spatial information](#spatial-information) — Spatial information provides the coordinate reference for geospatial data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Information → Georeferenced information → Spatial information → Geospatial Data

<a id='ground-measurements'></a>
### Ground measurements — Mediciones de campo
*data*
- **EN.** In-situ observations collected on the Earth's surface, such as crop type, yield, or soil properties. They serve as reference data for training and validating remote sensing models.
- **ES.** Observaciones in situ recolectadas en la superficie terrestre, como tipo de cultivo, rendimiento o propiedades del suelo. Sirven como datos de referencia para entrenar y validar modelos de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Ground](#ground) — Ground measurements are in-situ observations collected on the Earth's surface, such as crop yield or type.
    - [Measure](#measure) — Ground measurements serve as reference data for calibrating and validating satellite-derived models.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Reference → Ground → Ground measurements

<a id='ground-observations'></a>
### Ground observations — Observaciones de campo
*data* · sources: th_design_frames · th_alignment
- **EN.** Data collected directly at field locations, such as crop type, phenological stage, or yield measurements, used to train or validate remote sensing models.
- **ES.** Datos recopilados directamente en ubicaciones de campo, como tipo de cultivo, etapa fenológica o mediciones de rendimiento, utilizados para entrenar o validar modelos de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Field surveys](#field-surveys) — They are collected through field surveys and represent in-situ conditions.
    - [Ground](#ground) — Ground observations are specific measurements taken on the Earth's surface, synonymous with ground data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Reference → Ground → Ground observations

<a id='ground-truth-2'></a>
### Ground truth — Verdad terreno
*data* · sources: th_alignment
- **EN.** Observations or measurements of the actual conditions on the Earth's surface, collected via field surveys or very high-resolution imagery, used to train and validate remote sensing classification models.
- **ES.** Observaciones o mediciones de las condiciones reales en la superficie de la Tierra, recopiladas mediante encuestas de campo o imágenes de muy alta resolución, utilizadas para entrenar y validar modelos de clasificación de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Ground](#ground) — Ground truth data are direct observations of actual conditions on the Earth's surface used for validation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Reference → Ground → Ground truth

<a id='indicators'></a>
### Indicators — Indicadores
*statistic* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** Quantitative measures derived from data to assess a condition, such as vegetation indices like NDVI for crop health.
- **ES.** Medidas cuantitativas derivadas de datos para evaluar una condición, como los índices de vegetación como el NDVI para la salud del cultivo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Indices](#indices) — Indicators such as NDVI are spectral indices that highlight vegetation properties.
    - [Metrics](#metrics) — Indicators are derived metrics like vegetation indices that quantify crop condition or performance.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Metrics → Indicators

<a id='labeled-samples'></a>
### Labeled samples — Muestras etiquetadas
*data* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** Data points (e.g., pixels or polygons) that have been assigned a known class label by an expert, used to train and validate supervised machine learning models.
- **ES.** Puntos de datos (por ejemplo, píxeles o polígonos) a los que un experto ha asignado una etiqueta de clase conocida, utilizados para entrenar y validar modelos de aprendizaje automático supervisado.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Labeled samples are observations that have been assigned a ground truth class by an expert.
    - [Training dataset](#training-dataset) — A training dataset consists of labeled samples that serve as ground truth for supervised learning.
    - [Reference datasets](#reference-datasets) — Each reference dataset consists of labeled samples that specify the correct class for a location.
    - [Label](#label) — A label is the correct class category attached to each sample for supervised learning.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Training dataset → Labeled samples

<a id='land-cover-map'></a>
### Land cover map — Mapa de cobertura terrestre
*product* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** A thematic map showing the spatial distribution of land cover classes, such as forest or cropland, produced by classifying satellite imagery, often validated with reference data.
- **ES.** Mapa temático que muestra la distribución espacial de clases de cobertura del suelo, como bosque o tierras de cultivo, producido mediante la clasificación de imágenes satelitales y a menudo validado con datos de referencia.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Map](#map) — Thematic maps like land cover maps represent classified satellite imagery spatially.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Land cover map

<a id='large-scale-agricultural-mapping'></a>
### Large scale agricultural mapping — Cartografía agrícola a gran escala
*method* · sources: ct_zimbabwe
- **EN.** The process of creating land cover or crop type maps over extensive areas, often using satellite imagery and automated classification.
- **ES.** El proceso de crear mapas de cobertura del suelo o tipos de cultivo en áreas extensas, a menudo utilizando imágenes satelitales y clasificación automatizada.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Large-scale agricultural mapping applies classification algorithms to satellite data for regional crop maps.
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Large-scale agricultural mapping uses satellite imagery to cover wide regions efficiently.
    - [Crop type mapping](#crop-type-mapping) — Large-scale agricultural mapping extends crop type mapping to cover extensive areas using automated methods.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Crop type mapping → Large scale agricultural mapping

<a id='machine-learning-models'></a>
### Machine learning models — Modelos de aprendizaje automático
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** Algorithms trained on data to make predictions or decisions. For satellite image classification, they learn to assign land cover labels based on spectral and temporal patterns. Examples include Random Forest and TempCNN.
- **ES.** Algoritmos entrenados con datos para realizar predicciones o tomar decisiones. Para la clasificación de imágenes satelitales, aprenden a asignar etiquetas de cobertura del suelo basándose en patrones espectrales y temporales. Los ejemplos incluyen Random Forest y TempCNN.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — A model is a representation that learns from features and labels to perform classification or regression.
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Machine learning models are algorithms trained on data to recognize patterns and make predictions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Machine learning models

<a id='map-approach'></a>
### Map approach — Enfoque cartográfico
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_ppi
- **EN.** An estimation method that uses only satellite-derived map predictions for a quantity of interest, without incorporating ground-truth survey data, and may therefore be biased.
- **ES.** Método de estimación que utiliza únicamente predicciones de mapa derivadas de satélite para una cantidad de interés, sin incorporar datos de encuesta de verdad terreno, y que por lo tanto puede estar sesgado.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Map](#map) — The Map approach uses only satellite-derived map predictions, without survey data, to estimate quantities.
    - [Approach](#approach) — An approach is a methodology; the Map approach selects the classification map as the sole estimator.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Map approach

<a id='map-product'></a>
### Map product — Producto cartográfico
*product* · sources: crop_statistics_ppi · th_validation
- **EN.** A thematic map generated from satellite imagery or other data, showing the spatial distribution of land cover, crop types, or other variables, often used as input for statistical estimation.
- **ES.** Mapa temático generado a partir de imágenes satelitales u otros datos, que muestra la distribución espacial de la cobertura del suelo, tipos de cultivo u otras variables, a menudo utilizado como insumo para la estimación estadística.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Map](#map) — A map product is the final output, typically a thematic map derived from satellite imagery.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Map product

<a id='map-validation'></a>
### Map Validation — Validación de mapas
*method* · sources: th_validation · th_validation · th_validation
- **EN.** The assessment of a classified map's accuracy by comparing it against independent, probabilistically selected reference samples, using area-weighted error matrices.
- **ES.** La evaluación de la exactitud de un mapa clasificado mediante su comparación con muestras de referencia independientes seleccionadas probabilísticamente, utilizando matrices de error ponderadas por área.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Validation](#validation) — Map validation is the process of assessing a map's accuracy by comparing it to reference data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Map Validation

<a id='mapping'></a>
### Mapping — Mapeo
*method* · sources: ct_zimbabwe#crop-classification
- **EN.** The process of producing thematic maps, such as crop type or land cover maps, from remote sensing data.
- **ES.** El proceso de producir mapas temáticos, como mapas de tipos de cultivo o de cobertura del suelo, a partir de datos de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Mapping produces thematic maps by applying classification to satellite imagery.
    - [Map](#map) — Mapping is the process of producing thematic maps from remote sensing data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Mapping

<a id='model-ability'></a>
### Model ability — Capacidad del modelo
*metric* · sources: th_parcel_extraction#evaluation-metrics
- **EN.** A general term for a model's capability to perform a task, such as generalization across new regions or discrimination between spectrally similar classes.
- **ES.** Término general para la capacidad de un modelo de realizar una tarea, como la generalización a nuevas regiones o la discriminación entre clases espectralmente similares.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — Model ability refers to the capability of a model to generalize or discriminate across tasks.
    - [Performance](#performance) — It is often measured by the model's performance on new, unseen data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Performance → Model ability

<a id='model-evaluation'></a>
### Model evaluation — Evaluación de modelos
*method* · sources: th_validation#accuracy-assessment-of-classified-images
- **EN.** The process of assessing a classification model's performance using metrics like accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score on a validation dataset.
- **ES.** El proceso de evaluar el rendimiento de un modelo de clasificación utilizando métricas como exactitud, precisión, exhaustividad y puntuación F1 en un conjunto de datos de validación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — Model evaluation assesses how well a trained model performs on unseen data.
    - [Performance](#performance) — Model evaluation measures the performance of a model using quantitative metrics.
    - [Validation](#validation) — Model evaluation uses validation datasets to compute accuracy metrics and detect overfitting.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Performance → Model evaluation

<a id='model-generalization-capabilities'></a>
### Model generalization capabilities — Capacidades de generalización del modelo
*metric* · sources: ad_world_cereal · th_parcel_extraction
- **EN.** The ability of a machine learning model to perform accurately on new, unseen data from different regions, time periods, or conditions. Strong transferability and robustness to domain shifts are key aspects.
- **ES.** La capacidad de un modelo de aprendizaje automático para desempeñarse con precisión en datos nuevos no vistos de diferentes regiones, períodos de tiempo o condiciones. La fuerte transferibilidad y robustez ante cambios de dominio son aspectos clave.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — A model's generalization capability refers to its ability to perform well on new, unseen data beyond its training set.
    - [Validation](#validation) — Generalization is assessed by validating the model on independent datasets from different regions or times.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Model generalization capabilities

<a id='multi-task-learning'></a>
### Multi-task learning — Aprendizaje multitarea
*method* · sources: uav_field_parcels
- **EN.** A machine learning approach where a model is trained simultaneously on multiple related tasks, sharing representations between tasks to improve generalization and performance, such as jointly learning parcel region and boundary segmentation.
- **ES.** Un enfoque de aprendizaje automático donde un modelo se entrena simultáneamente en múltiples tareas relacionadas, compartiendo representaciones entre tareas para mejorar la generalización y el rendimiento, como aprender conjuntamente la segmentación de región y límites de parcelas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Multi-task learning trains a single model simultaneously on multiple related tasks, improving generalization.
    - [DCP MTL model](#dcp-mtl-model) — The DCP MTL model is a multi-task learning model that simultaneously extracts field parcel boundaries and regions from UAV imagery.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Multi-task learning

<a id='national-statistical-offices'></a>
### National Statistical Offices — Oficinas Nacionales de Estadística
*organization* · sources: introduction · th_alignment
- **EN.** Government agencies responsible for producing and disseminating official statistics, including agricultural data. They are the primary audience of the handbook, which aims to help them adopt Earth Observation methods.
- **ES.** Agencias gubernamentales responsables de producir y difundir estadísticas oficiales, incluidos los datos agrícolas. Son la audiencia principal del manual, cuyo objetivo es ayudarles a adoptar métodos de observación de la Tierra.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Users](#users) — Users, especially national statistical offices, apply remote sensing methods to produce official agricultural statistics.
    - [Official agricultural statistics](#official-agricultural-statistics) — National statistical offices are responsible for compiling and disseminating official agricultural statistics.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Agricultural Statistics → Official agricultural statistics → National Statistical Offices

<a id='ndvi'></a>
### NDVI — NDVI
*index* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI) is a spectral index calculated from near-infrared and red reflectance that indicates vegetation vigor and density. It is widely used for crop monitoring and phenology analysis.
- **ES.** El Índice de Vegetación de Diferencia Normalizada (NDVI) es un índice espectral calculado a partir de la reflectancia del infrarrojo cercano y la reflectancia roja que indica el vigor y la densidad de la vegetación. Es ampliamente utilizado para el monitoreo de cultivos y el análisis de fenología.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Vegetation](#vegetation) — NDVI is a spectral index designed to highlight vegetation, building on the concept of vegetation cover.
    - [Bands](#bands) — NDVI uses the near-infrared and red bands from satellite imagery to compute its index value.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cover → Vegetation → NDVI

<a id='neural-networks'></a>
### Neural networks — Redes neuronales
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning · th_parcel_extraction
- **EN.** Computational models inspired by biological neural networks, consisting of interconnected layers of nodes (neurons) that learn patterns from data through training.
- **ES.** Modelos computacionales inspirados en redes neuronales biológicas, que consisten en capas interconectadas de nodos (neuronas) que aprenden patrones de datos a través del entrenamiento.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Neural networks are a class of machine learning algorithms inspired by biological neurons.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Neural networks

<a id='operational-application'></a>
### Operational Application — Aplicación operativa
*other* · sources: introduction
- **EN.** A methodology or system that is routinely used in production settings, as opposed to a research prototype. It requires robustness, automation, and integration into institutional workflows.
- **ES.** Una metodología o sistema que se utiliza de forma rutinaria en entornos de producción, a diferencia de un prototipo de investigación. Requiere robustez, automatización e integración en flujos de trabajo institucionales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Implementation](#implementation) — Moving from research to operational application requires robust implementation and automation of the workflow.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Development → Implementation → Operational Application

<a id='phenological-patterns'></a>
### Phenological patterns — Patrones fenológicos
*phenomenon* · sources: th_lucc#the-key-role-of-time-series · ct_chile#satellite-image-time-series
- **EN.** Repeating sequences of plant growth stages (e.g., emergence, flowering, senescence) observable as temporal changes in satellite-derived vegetation indices. They are unique to each crop and form the basis for crop type discrimination.
- **ES.** Secuencias repetitivas de etapas de crecimiento de las plantas (p. ej., emergencia, floración, senescencia) observables como cambios temporales en los índices de vegetación derivados de satélite. Son únicos para cada cultivo y forman la base para la discriminación de tipos de cultivo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time series](#time-series) — Satellite time series data reveal phenological patterns through changes in vegetation indices over the growing season.
    - [Phenology](#phenology) — Phenological patterns are the repetitive sequences of plant growth stages observed in phenology, such as leaf emergence.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Crop → Growth → Crop development stage → Phenology → Phenological patterns

<a id='pixel-counting'></a>
### Pixel counting — Conteo de píxeles
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_area
- **EN.** A method to estimate area by multiplying the number of pixels classified as a given class by the pixel area. It is biased because it integrates classifier errors and does not correct for omission or commission.
- **ES.** Un método para estimar área multiplicando el número de píxeles clasificados como una clase determinada por el área del píxel. Está sesgado porque integra errores del clasificador y no corrige omisiones ni comisiones.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Area](#area) — From a classified map, pixel counting yields the area for each land cover or crop type.
    - [Classified map](#classified-map) — Pixel counting estimates area by multiplying the number of pixels classified as a class by its spatial resolution.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Classified map → Pixel counting

<a id='polygons'></a>
### Polygons — Polígonos
*data* · sources: th_alignment#quality-control-of-gps-traces · uav_agriculture_cook_islands#agricultural-plot-delineation
- **EN.** A vector data type representing a geographic area enclosed by a boundary. In remote sensing, field parcels are often digitized as polygons for labeling, training, and area computation.
- **ES.** Un tipo de dato vectorial que representa un área geográfica encerrada por un límite. En teledetección, las parcelas de campo a menudo se digitalizan como polígonos para etiquetado, entrenamiento y cálculo de área.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Field](#field) — Polygons are vector boundaries delineating individual fields or parcels in geospatial data.
    - [Parcels](#parcels) — Parcels are often represented as polygons in geographic information systems for analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Parcels → Polygons

<a id='precision-agriculture'></a>
### Precision agriculture — Agricultura de precisión
*method* · sources: th_remote_sensing · uav_crop_growth
- **EN.** A management approach that uses detailed spatial data, including remote sensing, to optimize inputs such as water, fertilizer, and pesticides at the field level, improving efficiency and reducing environmental impact.
- **ES.** Un enfoque de gestión que utiliza datos espaciales detallados, incluida la teledetección, para optimizar insumos como agua, fertilizantes y pesticidas a nivel de campo, mejorando la eficiencia y reduciendo el impacto ambiental.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Agriculture](#agriculture) — Precision agriculture uses detailed spatial data, including remote sensing, to optimize crop management inputs.
    - [Variability](#variability) — It addresses spatial variability within fields by applying treatments tailored to specific locations.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Variability → Precision agriculture

<a id='quality-control'></a>
### Quality Control — Control de Calidad
*method* · sources: th_quality_control#outline
- **EN.** Quality control in remote sensing refers to procedures for assessing and improving the reliability of training data, classifications, and derived products, including detection of noisy samples and class imbalance correction.
- **ES.** El Control de Calidad en teledetección se refiere a procedimientos para evaluar y mejorar la fiabilidad de los datos de entrenamiento, clasificaciones y productos derivados, incluyendo la detección de Muestras ruidosas y corrección de desbalance de Clases.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Quality](#quality) — Quality control is a systematic process to ensure data meets required standards through checks and corrections.
    - [Training dataset](#training-dataset) — Quality control of training data ensures samples are accurate and representative before model training.
    - [SOM analysis](#som-analysis) — It serves as a quality control step to identify mislabeled samples before training a classifier.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Quality → Quality Control

<a id='radar'></a>
### Radar — Radar
*sensor* · sources: th_remote_sensing#introduction-to-remote-sensing-imagery
- **EN.** A remote sensing technique that emits microwave signals and analyzes the returning echoes to observe the Earth's surface, capable of penetrating clouds and operating day or night.
- **ES.** Una técnica de teledetección que emite señales de microondas y analiza los ecos de retorno para observar la superficie de la Tierra, capaz de penetrar nubes y funcionar de día o de noche.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Remote sensing](#remote-sensing) — Radar is a remote sensing technique that uses actively emitted microwave signals instead of passive solar radiation.
    - [Sensors](#sensors) — Radar sensors on satellites transmit pulses and record echoes to measure surface properties.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Radar

<a id='random-forest'></a>
### Random Forest — Random forest
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning#random-forest
- **EN.** An ensemble machine learning method that builds many decision trees on random data subsets and averages their predictions for classification or regression.
- **ES.** Método de aprendizaje automático de conjunto que construye muchos árboles de decisión sobre subconjuntos aleatorios de datos y promedia sus predicciones para clasificación o regresión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — This ensemble method reduces overfitting compared to a single decision tree.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Random Forest

<a id='reliable-statistical-analyses'></a>
### Reliable statistical analyses — Análisis estadísticos fiables
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_ppi
- **EN.** Analyses that produce unbiased estimates with valid confidence intervals, often by combining satellite map predictions with a small random sample of ground-truth data to correct for prediction errors.
- **ES.** Análisis que producen estimaciones insesgadas con intervalos de confianza válidos, a menudo combinando predicciones de mapas satelitales con una pequeña muestra aleatoria de datos de verdad terreno para corregir errores de predicción.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — They incorporate accuracy metrics to correct classification errors and provide valid confidence intervals.
    - [Estimation](#estimation) — Reliable statistical analyses combine map predictions with design-based estimators to produce unbiased estimates.
    - [Ground survey estimators](#ground-survey-estimators) — By integrating ground survey data, these analyses ensure estimates are design-consistent.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Reliable statistical analyses

<a id='remote-sensing-estimation'></a>
### Remote sensing estimation — Estimación por teledetección
*method* · sources: cy_china
- **EN.** The process of deriving agricultural parameters, such as crop yield or planted area, from satellite imagery using models that relate spectral measurements to ground conditions.
- **ES.** Proceso de derivar parámetros agrícolas, como el rendimiento de cultivos o el área sembrada, a partir de imágenes satelitales utilizando modelos que relacionan las mediciones espectrales con las condiciones del terreno.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Estimation](#estimation) — Estimation infers unknown quantities like crop area from observed data such as satellite imagery.
    - [Remote sensing](#remote-sensing) — Remote sensing provides satellite imagery from which agricultural parameters can be estimated.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Remote sensing estimation

<a id='roadmap'></a>
### Roadmap — Hoja de ruta
*primitive* · sources: howto · howto
- **EN.** A strategic plan outlining the steps and timeline for developing or deploying a system or methodology. The handbook provides an implementation roadmap for the reproducible analysis system.
- **ES.** Un plan estratégico que describe los pasos y el cronograma para desarrollar o implementar un sistema o metodología. El manual proporciona una hoja de ruta de implementación para el sistema de análisis reproducible.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Development](#development) — It guides the development and deployment of a system or methodology over time.
    - [Strategy](#strategy) — A roadmap is a strategic plan that outlines steps and milestones for achieving long-term objectives.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Approach → Strategy → Roadmap

<a id='sample-balancing'></a>
### Sample balancing — Balanceo de muestra
*method* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** Techniques to adjust an imbalanced training dataset, such as oversampling minority classes (e.g., SMOTE) or undersampling majority classes, to improve classifier performance on less frequent categories.
- **ES.** Técnicas para ajustar un conjunto de datos de entrenamiento desequilibrado, como el sobremuestreo de clases minoritarias (p. ej., SMOTE) o el submuestreo de clases mayoritarias, para mejorar el rendimiento del clasificador en categorías menos frecuentes.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Sample balancing techniques (e.g., oversampling, undersampling) create a more balanced training dataset.
    - [Training samples](#training-samples) — Sample balancing adjusts the class distribution in training samples to avoid bias toward majority classes.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Label → Training samples → Sample balancing

<a id='sampling'></a>
### Sampling — Muestreo
*method* · sources: th_validation · th_design_frames
- **EN.** A method for selecting a subset of units from a population to estimate characteristics of the whole, often using probability-based designs like stratified random sampling to ensure unbiased estimates.
- **ES.** Método para seleccionar un subconjunto de unidades de una población con el fin de estimar características del total, utilizando a menudo diseños basados en probabilidad, como el muestreo aleatorio estratificado, para garantizar estimaciones insesgadas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Design](#design) — Design specifies the sampling strategy to collect representative data for estimation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling

<a id='satellite-imagery'></a>
### Satellite imagery — Imágenes satelitales
*data* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** Satellite imagery refers to data collected by sensors mounted on satellite platforms that capture electromagnetic radiation reflected or emitted from the Earth's surface, used for observing and analyzing land cover and crop conditions.
- **ES.** Las imágenes satelitales se refieren a datos recolectados por sensores montados en plataformas satelitales que capturan la radiación electromagnética reflejada o emitida desde la superficie de la Tierra, utilizadas para observar y analizar la cobertura del suelo y las condiciones de cultivo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Satellite imagery is the data captured by satellite sensors, from the satellite platform concept.
    - [Imagery](#imagery) — Satellite imagery is imagery specifically collected by satellite sensors, hence building from the broader imagery concept.
    - [Indices](#indices) — Satellite imagery provides the spectral bands used to calculate vegetation indices.
    - [Sensors](#sensors) — Satellite imagery is produced by sensors aboard satellites that detect electromagnetic radiation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite imagery

<a id='satellite-sensors'></a>
### Satellite sensors — Sensores satelitales
*sensor* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** Instruments mounted on satellites that collect data about the Earth's surface. They include optical sensors (e.g., cameras) and radar sensors (e.g., Synthetic Aperture Radar).
- **ES.** Instrumentos montados en satélites que recopilan datos sobre la superficie de la Tierra. Incluyen sensores ópticos (por ejemplo, cámaras) y sensores de radar (por ejemplo, Radar de Apertura Sintética).
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Satellite sensors are the instruments mounted on satellites that detect electromagnetic radiation to capture images.
    - [Remote sensing](#remote-sensing) — In remote sensing, satellite sensors are the key hardware that record data from a distance.
    - [Sensors](#sensors) — Satellite sensors are specific sensors designed to operate in space and collect Earth observation data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors

<a id='segmentation-map'></a>
### Segmentation map — Mapa de segmentación
*product* · sources: th_parcel_extraction#results
- **EN.** A raster or vector product where each pixel or polygon is assigned a class label representing a land cover or land use category.
- **ES.** Un producto ráster o vectorial donde cada píxel o polígono se asigna una etiqueta de clase que representa una categoría de cobertura del suelo o uso del suelo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Map](#map) — A segmentation map is a thematic map showing homogeneous regions like fields or forest patches.
    - [Segmentation](#segmentation) — A segmentation map stores the output of an image segmentation algorithm, labeling each pixel with a segment ID.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Segmentation map

<a id='self-organizing-maps'></a>
### Self-Organizing Maps — Mapas Autoorganizados
*method* · sources: th_quality_control#quality-control-using-self-organizing-maps
- **EN.** Self-Organizing Maps (SOM) are an unsupervised neural network technique that projects high-dimensional data onto a 2D grid while preserving topological relationships, used for clustering and quality control of training samples.
- **ES.** Los Mapas Autoorganizados (SOM) son una técnica no supervisada de redes neuronales que proyecta datos de alta dimensión en una cuadrícula 2D preservando relaciones topológicas, utilizada para agrupamiento y Control de Calidad de Muestras de Entrenamiento.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Self-organizing maps use a neural network to learn a topological representation of input data without labels.
    - [SOM analysis](#som-analysis) — SOM analysis uses Self-Organizing Maps to cluster time series and detect confusions in training data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Self-Organizing Maps

<a id='sentinel-missions'></a>
### Sentinel Missions — misiones Sentinel
*platform* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The European Space Agency's constellation of Earth observation satellites, including Sentinel-1 (SAR radar), Sentinel-2 (optical), and Sentinel-3, providing open-access, high-resolution data for global monitoring.
- **ES.** La constelación de satélites de observación de la Tierra de la Agencia Espacial Europea, que incluye Sentinel-1 (radar SAR), Sentinel-2 (óptico) y Sentinel-3, que proporcionan datos de alta resolución y acceso abierto para el monitoreo global.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — The Sentinel missions are a constellation of Earth‑observing satellites developed by the European Space Agency.
    - [Copernicus Data Space Ecosystem](#copernicus-data-space-ecosystem) — The Copernicus Data Space Ecosystem provides access to Sentinel mission data and processing tools.
    - [Harmonized Landsat Sentinel](#harmonized-landsat-sentinel) — This product merges data from Landsat and Sentinel missions for seamless time series analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Landsat → Harmonized Landsat Sentinel → Sentinel Missions

<a id='sowing'></a>
### Sowing — Siembra
*phenomenon* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** The agricultural practice of planting seeds in the soil; a key phenological event in crop calendars that satellite time series can detect by monitoring changes in vegetation indices.
- **ES.** Práctica agrícola de sembrar semillas en el suelo; un evento fenológico clave en los calendarios de cultivos que las series temporales satelitales pueden detectar monitoreando cambios en los índices de vegetación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Sowing is the agricultural practice of planting crop seeds into prepared soil to initiate a growing season.
    - [Land preparation](#land-preparation) — It occurs before sowing to create a suitable seedbed.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Agriculture → Land preparation → Sowing

<a id='spatial-datasets'></a>
### Spatial datasets — Conjuntos de datos espaciales
*data* · sources: ct_digital_earth_africa
- **EN.** Spatial datasets are georeferenced collections of Earth observation data, such as satellite imagery, land cover maps, and environmental variables, organized for analysis over a defined geographic area and often provided through cloud platforms.
- **ES.** Los conjuntos de datos espaciales son colecciones georreferenciadas de datos de observación de la Tierra, como imágenes satelitales, mapas de cobertura del suelo y variables ambientales, organizadas para su análisis en un área geográfica definida y a menudo proporcionadas a través de plataformas en la nube.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — Spatial datasets are datasets that include geographic location information, such as satellite images or vector boundaries.
    - [Spatial information](#spatial-information) — It is organized in spatial datasets such as vectors and rasters.
    - [Grid](#grid) — A grid organizes spatial datasets into regular cells for systematic analysis and efficient retrieval.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Information → Georeferenced information → Spatial information → Spatial datasets

<a id='spatial-patterns'></a>
### Spatial patterns — Patrones espaciales
*phenomenon*
- **EN.** The arrangement, distribution, or structure of features across geographic space. In agricultural statistics, spatial patterns reveal variability in crop growth, land use, or environmental conditions.
- **ES.** La disposición, distribución o estructura de las características en el espacio geográfico. En las estadísticas agrícolas, los patrones espaciales revelan la variabilidad en el crecimiento de los cultivos, el uso del suelo o las condiciones ambientales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Map](#map) — By analyzing a classified map, one can identify spatial patterns of crop distribution or land cover.
    - [Variability](#variability) — Spatial patterns describe how data values vary across geographic locations within a study area.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Spatial patterns

<a id='spatial-variability'></a>
### Spatial variability — Variabilidad espacial
*phenomenon* · sources: uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** The variation in values of a property (e.g., NDVI, yield) across geographic locations within a study area, often quantified by metrics like coefficient of variation.
- **ES.** La variación en los valores de una propiedad (por ejemplo, NDVI, rendimiento) entre ubicaciones geográficas dentro de un área de estudio, a menudo cuantificada por métricas como el coeficiente de variación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Variability](#variability) — Spatial variability is the geographic variation of a property, such as NDVI, across a region.
    - [Spatial dimension](#spatial-dimension) — Spatial variability captures differences between locations within a study area.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Variability → Spatial variability

<a id='spectral-range'></a>
### Spectral Range — Rango espectral
*data* · sources: th_remote_sensing#introduction-to-remote-sensing-imagery
- **EN.** Spectral range refers to the interval of wavelengths in the electromagnetic spectrum that a satellite sensor measures, typically expressed in micrometers (µm) or nanometers (nm).
- **ES.** El rango espectral se refiere al intervalo de longitudes de onda en el espectro electromagnético que mide un sensor satelital, generalmente expresado en micrómetros (µm) o nanómetros (nm).
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Sensors](#sensors) — Spectral range defines the wavelength intervals a sensor can detect, such as visible or near-infrared.
    - [Range](#range) — Range is a shortened term often used to refer to spectral range or spatial coverage of a sensor.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Spectral Range

<a id='stages'></a>
### Stages — Etapas
*primitive* · sources: ct_poland
- **EN.** The discrete steps or phases in a process, such as data acquisition, preprocessing, classification, and validation in a remote sensing workflow.
- **ES.** Los pasos o fases discretas en un proceso, como la adquisición de datos, el preprocesamiento, la clasificación y la validación en un flujo de trabajo de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Step](#step) — Each stage represents a major phase of the workflow for agricultural statistics.
    - [Process](#process) — Stages are the discrete steps within a process, such as data acquisition and classification.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Step → Process → Stages

<a id='standardization'></a>
### Standardization — Estandarización
*method* · sources: th_lucc · ad_world_cereal
- **EN.** The process of establishing and applying uniform rules, formats, or procedures to ensure consistency and comparability of data across different sources or time periods.
- **ES.** Proceso de establecer y aplicar reglas, formatos o procedimientos uniformes para garantizar la consistencia y comparabilidad de los datos entre diferentes fuentes o períodos de tiempo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification Systems](#classification-systems) — It is applied to classification systems to enable comparability.
    - [Consistency](#consistency) — Standardization establishes uniform rules to ensure consistency across data and methods.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Land cover classes → Classification Systems → Standardization

<a id='statistical-indicators'></a>
### Statistical indicators — Indicadores estadísticos
*statistic* · sources: uav_wheat_growth#model-evaluation-metrics
- **EN.** Quantitative measures used to evaluate model performance, such as coefficient of determination, root mean square error, and mean absolute error.
- **ES.** Medidas cuantitativas utilizadas para evaluar el rendimiento del modelo, como el coeficiente de determinación, la raíz del error cuadrático medio y el error absoluto medio.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — Model performance is evaluated using statistical indicators like RMSE and R-squared.
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Statistical indicators derive from the broader field of statistics to quantify accuracy and precision.
    - [Metrics](#metrics) — Statistical indicators are quantitative metrics that assess the performance of models or analyses.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Metrics → Statistical indicators

<a id='surface-reflectance'></a>
### Surface reflectance — Reflectancia superficial
*data* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** The fraction of incident solar radiation reflected by the Earth's surface, derived from satellite imagery after atmospheric correction. It enables consistent comparison across time and locations.
- **ES.** La fracción de la radiación solar incidente reflejada por la superficie de la Tierra, derivada de imágenes satelitales después de la corrección atmosférica. Permite una comparación consistente entre ubicaciones y momentos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Reflectance](#reflectance) — Surface reflectance is the reflectance measured at the Earth's surface after removing atmospheric effects.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Reflectance → Surface reflectance

<a id='surveying'></a>
### Surveying — Topografía
*method* · sources: th_design_frames · ct_chile
- **EN.** The systematic collection of data on agricultural variables, such as crop type and area, through direct observation or interviews at sample locations, often using GPS.
- **ES.** Recopilación sistemática de datos sobre variables agrícolas, como tipo de cultivo y área, mediante observación directa o entrevistas en ubicaciones de muestra, a menudo utilizando GPS.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Survey](#survey) — Surveying is the systematic act of conducting a survey to gather data.
    - [Ground surveys](#ground-surveys) — It often involves field-based data collection, synonymous with ground surveys.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Ground surveys → Surveying

<a id='temporal-pattern'></a>
### Temporal pattern — Patrón temporal
*phenomenon* · sources: th_data_cubes
- **EN.** A recurring sequence or trend in data over time, such as the seasonal variation in vegetation indices observed in satellite image time series, used to monitor change.
- **ES.** Secuencia o tendencia recurrente en los datos a lo largo del tiempo, como la variación estacional en los índices de vegetación observada en series temporales de imágenes satelitales, utilizada para monitorear cambios.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time series](#time-series) — A temporal pattern is a recurring sequence or trend observed in a satellite image time series.
    - [Phenology](#phenology) — Crop phenology drives the temporal pattern of vegetation indices over a growing season.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Crop → Growth → Crop development stage → Phenology → Temporal pattern

<a id='thematic-map'></a>
### Thematic map — Mapa temático
*product* · sources: th_validation#introduction · ct_chile#generation-of-land-use-and-land-cover-maps-using-time-series-of-satellite-images
- **EN.** A map that displays the spatial distribution of a specific theme or class, such as land cover, crop type, or yield. Thematic maps are the primary output of satellite image classification for agricultural statistics.
- **ES.** Un mapa que muestra la distribución espacial de un tema o clase específica, como cobertura del suelo, tipo de cultivo o rendimiento. Los mapas temáticos son el resultado principal de la clasificación de imágenes satelitales para estadísticas agrícolas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Classification labels are used to create a thematic map that displays the spatial distribution of a specific theme.
    - [Map](#map) — A map that shows the distribution of classes such as land cover or crop types is called a thematic map.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Thematic map

<a id='tiling-system'></a>
### Tiling system — Sistema de teselas
*data* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** A spatial partition that divides the Earth's surface into regular, uniquely identified grid cells (tiles) used to organize satellite image collections, such as the MGRS grid for Sentinel-2 or the WRS-2 for Landsat, enabling consistent data management and processing.
- **ES.** Una partición espacial que divide la superficie de la Tierra en celdas de cuadrícula regulares e identificadas de manera única (teselas) utilizadas para organizar colecciones de imágenes satelitales, como la cuadrícula MGRS para Sentinel-2 o la WRS-2 para Landsat, permitiendo una gestión y procesamiento de datos consistentes.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Grid](#grid) — A tiling system divides the Earth into regular grid cells for managing large satellite image collections.
    - [Military Grid Reference System](#military-grid-reference-system) — The Military Grid Reference System is a standard tiling system used for global satellite data organization.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Tiles → Grid → Military Grid Reference System → Tiling system

<a id='tillering-samples'></a>
### Tillering samples — Muestras de macollamiento
*data* · sources: cy_colombia#noisy-sample-detection
- **EN.** Training data points representing the tillering phenological stage, where the crop develops side shoots; these samples may show spectral confusion with adjacent stages.
- **ES.** Puntos de datos de entrenamiento que representan la etapa fenológica de macollamiento, donde el cultivo desarrolla brotes laterales; estas muestras pueden presentar confusión espectral con etapas adyacentes.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Training samples](#training-samples) — Tillering samples are training samples that represent the specific phenological stage of tillering.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Label → Training samples → Tillering samples

<a id='time-series-classification'></a>
### Time series classification — Clasificación de series temporales
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning#common-interface-to-machine-learning-and-deep-learning-models
- **EN.** A machine learning task that assigns a land cover or crop type label to a pixel based on its complete temporal profile of spectral measurements.
- **ES.** Una tarea de aprendizaje automático que asigna una etiqueta de cobertura del suelo o tipo de cultivo a un píxel basándose en su perfil temporal completo de mediciones espectrales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — It applies classification algorithms to time series data to categorize each sequence.
    - [Satellite image time series classification](#satellite-image-time-series-classification) — Satellite image time series classification applies time series classification methods to sequences of satellite images.
    - [Satellite image time series](#satellite-image-time-series) — Satellite image time series classification uses temporal sequences of images to label land cover.
    - [Time series analysis](#time-series-analysis) — Time series classification assigns labels to entire temporal sequences based on patterns.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Analysis → Time series analysis → Time series classification

<a id='transferable-classification-system'></a>
### Transferable classification system — Sistema de clasificación transferible
*method* · sources: ad_world_cereal
- **EN.** A classification approach designed to be applied across different regions, times, or contexts without extensive retraining, often using foundation models.
- **ES.** Un enfoque de clasificación diseñado para aplicarse en diferentes regiones, tiempos o contextos sin necesidad de un reentrenamiento extenso, a menudo utilizando modelos fundacionales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification Systems](#classification-systems) — A transferable classification system is designed to be applied across different regions and times.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Land cover classes → Classification Systems → Transferable classification system

<a id='uhr-cfp-dataset'></a>
### UHR CFP dataset — conjunto de datos UHR CFP
*data* · sources: uav_field_parcels#experimental-area-and-data
- **EN.** A dataset of ultra-high resolution (0.2m) UAV images paired with labels for cultivation field parcels, used to train and evaluate models for automated parcel vectorization.
- **ES.** Un conjunto de datos de imágenes de UAV de resolución ultraalta (0,2 m) emparejadas con etiquetas para parcelas de campo de cultivo, utilizado para entrenar y evaluar modelos para la vectorización automatizada de parcelas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — The UHR CFP dataset is a labeled collection of UAV images for parcel detection and segmentation.
    - [Parcels](#parcels) — Each image in the UHR CFP dataset is paired with polygon labels of individual agricultural field parcels.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Parcels → UHR CFP dataset

<a id='usgs'></a>
### USGS — USGS
*organization* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The U.S. Geological Survey, a scientific agency that jointly manages the Landsat program with NASA and distributes Landsat imagery through platforms like Earth Explorer.
- **ES.** El Servicio Geológico de Estados Unidos, una agencia científica que gestiona conjuntamente el programa Landsat con la NASA y distribuye imágenes satelitales a través de plataformas como Earth Explorer.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [NASA](#nasa) — The USGS jointly manages the Landsat program with NASA and distributes the satellite data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** .netrc file → Earthdatalogin → EarthData → NASA → USGS

<a id='vegetation-indices'></a>
### Vegetation indices — Índices de vegetación
*index* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** Mathematical combinations of spectral bands, such as NDVI and EVI, designed to enhance vegetation signal and assess crop health, biomass, and phenological stage.
- **ES.** Combinaciones matemáticas de bandas espectrales, como NDVI y EVI, diseñadas para mejorar la señal de vegetación y evaluar la salud del cultivo, la biomasa y la etapa fenológica.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Vegetation](#vegetation) — Vegetation indices use spectral combinations to quantify green biomass and plant condition.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cover → Vegetation → Vegetation indices

<a id='workflow'></a>
### Workflow — Flujo de trabajo
*method* · sources: ct_mexico#methods
- **EN.** A sequence of processing steps for analyzing remote sensing data, such as loading imagery, classifying pixels, and validating results.
- **ES.** Una secuencia de pasos de procesamiento para analizar datos de teledetección, como cargar imágenes, clasificar píxeles y validar resultados.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Process](#process) — A workflow is a specific sequence of steps (a process) that is formally defined to analyze data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Step → Process → Workflow

<a id='worldcereal-reference-data-module'></a>
### WorldCereal Reference Data Module — Módulo de Datos de Referencia de WorldCereal
*software* · sources: ad_world_cereal · ad_world_cereal
- **EN.** A community-driven framework for collecting, harmonizing, documenting, and sharing reference data for crop mapping, integrating field surveys, parcel systems, and citizen science. It reduces the cost of training data for Earth observation applications.
- **ES.** Un marco impulsado por la comunidad para recopilar, armonizar, documentar y compartir datos de referencia para el mapeo de cultivos, integrando encuestas de campo, sistemas de parcelas y ciencia ciudadana. Reduce el costo de los datos de entrenamiento para aplicaciones de observación de la Tierra.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop type mapping](#crop-type-mapping) — It supports crop type mapping by standardizing reference data collection and documentation across projects.
    - [Reference datasets](#reference-datasets) — The WorldCereal Reference Data Module provides a framework for harmonizing and sharing reference datasets for crop mapping.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Crop type mapping → WorldCereal Reference Data Module


## Level 5

<a id='acreage-estimation'></a>
### Acreage estimation — Estimación de superficie
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_area · th_validation
- **EN.** The process of estimating the total area planted with a specific crop using remote sensing, surveys, or combined methods, often with uncertainty quantification.
- **ES.** Proceso de estimar el área total sembrada con un cultivo específico mediante teledetección, encuestas o métodos combinados, a menudo con cuantificación de incertidumbre.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Area estimation](#area-estimation) — Acreage estimation is a type of area estimation focused on crop extent.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Area estimation → Acreage estimation

<a id='agricultural-statistical-systems'></a>
### Agricultural statistical systems — Sistemas estadísticos agrícolas
*system* · sources: introduction
- **EN.** Agricultural statistical systems are the institutional frameworks and processes used by National Statistical Offices to collect, process, and disseminate official data on crop areas, yields, and production, increasingly integrating Earth Observation data.
- **ES.** Los sistemas estadísticos agrícolas son los marcos institucionales y procesos utilizados por las Oficinas Nacionales de Estadística para recopilar, procesar y difundir datos oficiales sobre áreas de cultivo, rendimientos y producción, integrando cada vez más datos de observación de la Tierra.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Agricultural Statistics](#agricultural-statistics) — Agricultural statistical systems are the institutional frameworks that produce agricultural statistics.
    - [National Statistical Offices](#national-statistical-offices) — National Statistical Offices operate agricultural statistical systems to generate official data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Agricultural Statistics → Official agricultural statistics → National Statistical Offices → Agricultural statistical systems

<a id='analytics'></a>
### Analytics — Analítica
*method* · sources: ad_world_cereal
- **EN.** The systematic computational analysis of data, often using statistical or machine learning methods, to extract insights and support decision-making.
- **ES.** El análisis computacional sistemático de datos, a menudo utilizando métodos estadísticos o de aprendizaje automático, para extraer información y apoyar la toma de decisiones.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Analysis](#analysis) — Analytics is the systematic application of computational methods to extract insights from data.
    - [Data Science](#data-science) — It uses statistical and machine learning techniques for understanding Earth observation data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Data Science → Analytics

<a id='atmospheric-correction'></a>
### Atmospheric correction — Corrección atmosférica
*method* · sources: th_data_sources · th_data_sources
- **EN.** Processing that removes atmospheric scattering and absorption effects from satellite imagery to obtain surface reflectance values.
- **ES.** Procesamiento que elimina los efectos de dispersión y absorción atmosférica de las imágenes satelitales para obtener valores de reflectancia superficial.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Cloud](#cloud) — Cloud is atmospheric water vapor that obscures satellite imagery and must be masked or composited.
    - [Processing](#processing) — Atmospheric correction is a processing step that removes scattering and absorption effects from satellite data.
    - [Radiometric corrections](#radiometric-corrections) — Radiometric corrections include atmospheric correction to convert raw digital numbers to surface reflectance.
    - [Surface reflectance](#surface-reflectance) — Atmospheric correction converts top-of-atmosphere radiance to surface reflectance for accurate analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Reflectance → Surface reflectance → Atmospheric correction

<a id='biomass'></a>
### Biomass — Biomasa
*phenomenon* · sources: cy_colombia · th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The total mass of living plant material in a given area, often estimated from vegetation indices or SAR backscatter, used to assess crop growth and yield.
- **ES.** Masa total de material vegetal vivo en un área determinada, a menudo estimada a partir de índices de vegetación o retrodispersión SAR, utilizada para evaluar el crecimiento y rendimiento de cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Vegetation](#vegetation) — Biomass is the total mass of living vegetation in a given area, estimated from spectral indices.
    - [Surface reflectance](#surface-reflectance) — Biomass can be estimated from surface reflectance via models relating spectral response to mass.
