- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Pixels → Values → Reflectance → Surface reflectance → Biomass

<a id='boundaries'></a>
### Boundaries — Límites
*data*
- **EN.** The edges or limits separating different land cover types, agricultural fields, or administrative units. In remote sensing, boundaries are often delineated through segmentation or vectorization.
- **ES.** Los bordes o límites que separan diferentes tipos de cobertura del suelo, campos agrícolas o unidades administrativas. En teledetección, los límites a menudo se delinean mediante segmentación o vectorización.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Polygons](#polygons) — Boundaries are the edges of polygons that delineate agricultural fields or land cover parcels.
    - [Segmentation](#segmentation) — Image segmentation produces boundaries that separate different land cover or crop regions.
    - [Study area](#study-area) — A study area is delineated by boundaries that define its spatial extent for remote sensing.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Parcels → Polygons → Boundaries

<a id='cgi-algorithm'></a>
### CGI algorithm — algoritmo CGI
*method* · sources: uav_crop_growth#methods
- **EN.** A method that monitors crop growth by computing multiple vegetation indices from UAV multispectral imagery, normalizing them, and extracting the first principal component to produce a continuous Crop Growth Index.
- **ES.** Un método que monitorea el crecimiento de cultivos calculando múltiples índices de vegetación a partir de imágenes multiespectrales de UAV, normalizándolos y extrayendo el primer componente principal para producir un Índice de Crecimiento de Cultivos continuo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Algorithm](#algorithm) — The CGI algorithm is a defined computational procedure for extracting crop growth indicators from images.
    - [Vegetation indices](#vegetation-indices) — By combining multiple vegetation indices, the CGI algorithm captures different aspects of crop growth.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → CGI algorithm

<a id='classification-algorithm'></a>
### Classification algorithm — Algoritmo de clasificación
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning · th_machine_learning
- **EN.** A computational method that uses labeled samples to learn patterns and then assigns class labels to new observations, such as Random Forest or neural networks.
- **ES.** Un método computacional que utiliza muestras etiquetadas para aprender patrones y luego asigna etiquetas de clase a nuevas observaciones, como Random Forest o redes neuronales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Algorithm](#algorithm) — A classification algorithm is an algorithm specifically designed to assign class labels to data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → Classification algorithm

<a id='classification-method'></a>
### Classification method — Método de clasificación
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** A machine learning or deep learning algorithm used to assign land cover labels to pixels based on their spectral-temporal features. Examples include Random Forest, XGBoost, and TempCNN.
- **ES.** Un algoritmo de aprendizaje automático o profundo utilizado para asignar etiquetas de cobertura del suelo a los píxeles basándose en sus características espectro-temporales. Los ejemplos incluyen Random Forest, XGBoost y TempCNN.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — A classification method is a machine learning algorithm that learns from samples to assign classes.
    - [Algorithm](#algorithm) — It is a specific algorithm—e.g., decision tree or random forest—that processes features to label pixels.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → Classification method

<a id='classification-process'></a>
### Classification process — Proceso de clasificación
*method* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** The set of operations, from training data preparation to model application, that assigns semantic labels to pixels or objects in satellite imagery.
- **ES.** El conjunto de operaciones, desde la preparación de datos de entrenamiento hasta la aplicación del modelo, que asigna etiquetas semánticas a píxeles u objetos en imágenes satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — The classification process is the entire workflow from data preparation to label assignment.
    - [Stages](#stages) — It includes stages like training, classification, and validation in a sequential order.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Step → Process → Stages → Classification process

<a id='classification-workflows'></a>
### Classification workflows — Flujos de trabajo de clasificación
*method* · sources: ct_digital_earth_africa
- **EN.** Sequences of steps for assigning land cover or crop type labels to satellite imagery, including data preparation, model training, and validation.
- **ES.** Secuencias de etapas para asignar etiquetas de cobertura del suelo o tipo de cultivo a las imágenes satelitales, que incluyen preparación de datos, entrenamiento del modelo y validación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Classification workflows organize the steps of classification, from data prep to map validation.
    - [Workflow](#workflow) — Classification workflows are a specific type of workflow that sequences steps for assigning labels.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Step → Process → Workflow → Classification workflows

<a id='cluster'></a>
### Cluster — Clúster
*method* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** A set of data points (e.g., satellite image time series) grouped together by a clustering algorithm because they share similar properties, used to identify patterns or separate land cover classes.
- **ES.** Conjunto de puntos de datos (por ejemplo, series temporales de imágenes satelitales) agrupados por un algoritmo de agrupamiento porque comparten propiedades similares, utilizado para identificar patrones o separar clases de cobertura del suelo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Data points are grouped by a clustering algorithm into clusters based on similarity metrics.
    - [Algorithm](#algorithm) — A clustering algorithm partitions data into clusters of similar points.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → Cluster

<a id='confusion-matrix'></a>
### Confusion matrix — Matriz de confusión
*metric* · sources: th_validation#accuracy-assessment-of-classified-images · th_quality_control#validation
- **EN.** A table that compares predicted class labels (from a map or model) against reference labels, showing the number of correct and incorrect predictions per class. It is the basis for accuracy metrics such as user's and producer's accuracy.
- **ES.** Una tabla que compara las etiquetas de clase predichas (de un mapa o modelo) con las etiquetas de referencia, mostrando el número de predicciones correctas e incorrectas por clase. Es la base para métricas de precisión como la precisión del usuario y del productor.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classes](#classes) — Each cell of the confusion matrix counts the number of samples for specific predicted versus actual class combinations.
    - [Classification](#classification) — A confusion matrix tabulates the agreement between predicted classes from a classification and actual reference classes.
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Accuracy metrics like overall accuracy are derived from the confusion matrix by comparing predictions to ground truth.
    - [Metrics](#metrics) — They are derived from a confusion matrix to compute overall accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score.
    - [Overall accuracy](#overall-accuracy) — It is calculated from the confusion matrix as the sum of true positives and true negatives divided by total.
    - [Accuracy assessment](#accuracy-assessment) — Accuracy assessment is typically based on the confusion matrix comparing predicted vs. reference labels.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix

<a id='coordinate-reference-system'></a>
### Coordinate Reference System — Sistema de referencia de coordenadas
*other* · sources: uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** A framework for defining real-world geographic coordinates, such as WGS 84 (latitude/longitude) or UTM (projected meters). Harmonizing CRS between data layers is essential for accurate spatial analysis.
- **ES.** Un marco para definir coordenadas geográficas del mundo real, como WGS 84 (latitud/longitud) o UTM (metros proyectados). Armonizar el sistema de referencia de coordenadas entre los conjuntos de datos es esencial para un análisis espacial preciso.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Geographic information systems](#geographic-information-systems) — In GIS, the CRS is essential for aligning and analyzing spatial data from different sources.
    - [Coordinates](#coordinates) — A coordinate reference system (CRS) defines how geographic coordinates map to positions on the Earth.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Geoinformatics → Geographic information systems → Coordinate Reference System

<a id='coordinate-system'></a>
### Coordinate system — Sistema de coordenadas
*other* · sources: th_data_sources
- **EN.** A reference system used to uniquely identify the location of points on the Earth's surface. It includes geographic coordinates (latitude/longitude) as well as projected coordinate systems (e.g., UTM) that convert the Earth's curved surface to a flat map, enabling area and distance calculations.
- **ES.** Un sistema de referencia utilizado para identificar de manera única la ubicación de puntos en la superficie de la Tierra. Incluye coordenadas geográficas (latitud/longitud), así como sistemas de coordenadas proyectadas (por ejemplo, UTM) que convierten la superficie curva de la Tierra a un mapa plano, permitiendo cálculos de área y distancia.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Georeferenced information](#georeferenced-information) — A coordinate system provides the reference for georeferenced information, linking data to locations.
    - [Basemap](#basemap) — A basemap is projected in a coordinate system to align with other geospatial layers.
    - [Coordinates](#coordinates) — A coordinate system defines how coordinates are assigned to points on Earth, enabling georeferencing.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Basemap → Coordinate system

<a id='crop-mapping'></a>
### Crop mapping — Mapeo de cultivos
*method* · sources: ct_zimbabwe
- **EN.** Crop mapping is the process of generating spatial maps that show the distribution of different crop types across a landscape, typically using satellite imagery and machine learning classification.
- **ES.** El mapeo de cultivos es el proceso de generar mapas espaciales que muestran la distribución de diferentes tipos de cultivos en un paisaje, típicamente utilizando imágenes satelitales y clasificación de aprendizaje automático.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Crop mapping applies mapping techniques to identify and delineate cultivated plant species, using crop knowledge.
    - [Classification](#classification) — Crop mapping relies on classification methods to assign crop type labels to pixels or parcels in satellite imagery.
    - [Mapping](#mapping) — Crop mapping is the process of producing thematic maps showing crop types, building on the general mapping concept.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Mapping → Crop mapping

<a id='cropland-extent-map'></a>
### Cropland extent map — Mapa de extensión de tierras de cultivo
*product* · sources: ct_digital_earth_africa · crop_statistics_area
- **EN.** A thematic map that delineates areas used for crop cultivation, often derived from satellite imagery and used to mask non-agricultural land for crop type mapping or area estimation.
- **ES.** Un mapa temático que delimita las áreas utilizadas para el cultivo agrícola, a menudo derivado de imágenes satelitales y utilizado para enmascarar tierras no agrícolas en el mapeo de tipos de cultivo o la estimación de área.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land cover map](#land-cover-map) — A cropland extent map is a land cover map that specifically delineates areas used for crop cultivation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Land cover map → Cropland extent map

<a id='data-cube'></a>
### Data cube — Cubo de datos
*data* · sources: th_data_cubes#regular-earth-observation-data-cubes
- **EN.** A three-dimensional array of satellite data with two spatial dimensions and one temporal dimension, where each cell has the same spatial resolution and regular time intervals, suitable for machine learning.
- **ES.** Un arreglo tridimensional de datos satelitales con dos dimensiones espaciales y una dimensión temporal, donde cada celda tiene la misma resolución espacial e intervalos de tiempo regulares, adecuado para aprendizaje automático.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time](#time) — The time dimension in a data-cube allows analysis of temporal changes across repeated satellite observations.
    - [Satellite imagery](#satellite-imagery) — A data-cube organizes satellite imagery along spatial axes and a time dimension for easy access.
    - [Raster](#raster) — A data-cube is a multi-temporal raster where each layer is a spatially aligned image at a different date.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite imagery → Data cube

<a id='decision-tree'></a>
### Decision tree — Árbol de decisión
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** A supervised machine learning model that splits data into branches based on feature values, forming a tree structure. Each leaf represents a class label. Ensembles like Random Forest combine multiple trees.
- **ES.** Un modelo de aprendizaje automático supervisado que divide los datos en ramas basadas en valores de atributos, formando una estructura de árbol. Cada hoja representa una etiqueta de clase. Los conjuntos como Random Forest combinan múltiples árboles.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — In classification, a decision tree partitions the feature space into regions assigned to classes.
    - [Feature](#feature) — A decision tree splits the data based on feature values to create a tree-like model of decisions.
    - [Random Forest](#random-forest) — Random forest extends decision trees by building many trees on random data subsets and averaging.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Random Forest → Decision tree

<a id='deep-learning'></a>
### Deep learning — Aprendizaje profundo
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** A class of machine learning algorithms using multi-layered neural networks to automatically learn hierarchical features from large datasets, widely used for image classification tasks.
- **ES.** Una clase de algoritmos de aprendizaje automático que utilizan redes neuronales multicapa para aprender automáticamente atributos jerárquicos de grandes conjuntos de datos, ampliamente utilizado para tareas de clasificación de imágenes.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Deep learning is a subset of machine learning using multi-layered neural networks to learn hierarchical features.
    - [Neural networks](#neural-networks) — It extends neural networks by adding many hidden layers that automatically extract complex patterns from data.
    - [Segment Model](#segment-model) — A Segment Model is a deep learning model that performs image segmentation by generating object masks from input images.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Neural networks → Deep learning

<a id='design-estimator'></a>
### Design estimator — Estimador de diseño
*statistic* · sources: crop_statistics_calibration#national-level-estimators
- **EN.** An estimator based on the sampling design (defined by inclusion probabilities), which is design-consistent, meaning it becomes unbiased as the sample size increases under that design.
- **ES.** Un estimador basado en el diseño muestral (definido por probabilidades de inclusión), que es consistente con el diseño, lo que significa que se vuelve insesgado a medida que aumenta el tamaño de la muestra bajo ese diseño.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Estimator](#estimator) — A design estimator extends the estimator by incorporating the sampling design's inclusion probabilities.
    - [Sampling](#sampling) — The design estimator uses the probability-based sampling scheme to produce unbiased population estimates.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator → Design estimator

<a id='detailed-mapping'></a>
### Detailed mapping — Cartografía detallada
*method* · sources: ct_mexico · th_parcel_extraction
- **EN.** Creating high-resolution spatial representations of land cover, crop types, or field boundaries, often using object-based image analysis. It supports area estimation and agricultural statistics at fine administrative levels.
- **ES.** Creación de representaciones espaciales de alta resolución de la cobertura del suelo, tipos de cultivo o límites de campos, a menudo mediante análisis de imágenes basado en objetos. Apoya la estimación de áreas y las estadísticas agrícolas a niveles administrativos detallados.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Mapping](#mapping) — Detailed mapping extends general mapping by using high-resolution imagery and object-based methods to produce fine-scale crop maps.
    - [Resolution](#resolution) — Detailed mapping requires high spatial resolution imagery to delineate individual fields and small features.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Mapping → Detailed mapping

<a id='early-season-crop-yield-mapping'></a>
### Early season crop yield mapping — Cartografía temprana del rendimiento de cultivos
*method* · sources: cy_finland
- **EN.** The practice of forecasting crop yields before harvest using satellite imagery and machine learning, enabling timely estimates for food security planning.
- **ES.** Práctica de pronosticar el rendimiento de cultivos antes de la cosecha utilizando imágenes satelitales y aprendizaje automático, permitiendo estimaciones oportunas para la planificación de la seguridad alimentaria.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Mapping](#mapping) — Mapping techniques produce spatial yield estimates from satellite imagery and models.
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Machine learning models predict early season crop yield from satellite features.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Mapping → Early season crop yield mapping

<a id='gis'></a>
### GIS — GIS
*software* · sources: th_alignment
- **EN.** Geographic Information System, a software framework for capturing, storing, analyzing, and displaying spatial data; used for tasks such as parcel digitization, map creation, and spatial analysis.
- **ES.** Sistema de Información Geográfica, un marco de software para capturar, almacenar, analizar y mostrar datos geoespaciales; utilizado para tareas como digitalización de parcelas, creación de mapas y análisis espacial.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Geospatial Data](#geospatial-data) — A GIS is a software system for capturing, storing, analyzing, and displaying geospatial data layers.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Information → Georeferenced information → Spatial information → Geospatial Data → GIS

<a id='hidden-layers'></a>
### Hidden layers — Capas ocultas
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** Intermediate layers in a neural network between the input and output layers that transform inputs through weighted connections; deeper hidden layers capture more complex features.
- **ES.** Capas intermedias en una red neuronal entre las capas de entrada y salida que transforman las entradas mediante conexiones ponderadas; las capas ocultas más profundas capturan atributos más complejos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Neural networks](#neural-networks) — Hidden layers are intermediate layers in a neural network between input and output that transform features.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Neural networks → Hidden layers

<a id='in-situ-observations'></a>
### In-situ observations — Observaciones in situ
*data* · sources: th_alignment#introduction · th_design_frames#matching-in-situ-survey-data-to-remote-sensing-analysis-needs
- **EN.** Measurements or descriptions recorded directly at a location on the Earth's surface, typically collected by field surveys. They serve as ground truth for calibrating and validating remote sensing products.
- **ES.** Mediciones o descripciones registradas directamente en una ubicación de la superficie terrestre, típicamente recopiladas mediante encuestas de campo. Sirven como verdad terreno para calibrar y validar productos de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Field](#field) — In-situ observations are collected directly in agricultural fields to record crop type, condition, and other attributes.
    - [Ground observations](#ground-observations) — In-situ observations are measurements or descriptions recorded directly at field locations, same as ground observations.
    - [FAO situ quality framework](#fao-situ-quality-framework) — The FAO situ quality framework evaluates the compatibility of in-situ observations with satellite data needs.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Reference → Ground → Ground observations → In-situ observations

<a id='individual-agricultural-plot-polygons'></a>
### Individual agricultural plot polygons — Polígonos de parcelas agrícolas individuales
*data* · sources: uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** Vector boundaries delineating individual farm fields or crop parcels, digitized from high-resolution imagery and used for area measurement and analysis.
- **ES.** Límites vectoriales que delimitan parcelas agrícolas individuales o parcelas de cultivo, digitalizados a partir de imágenes de alta resolución y utilizados para medición y análisis de área.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Field](#field) — Fields are individual cultivated areas represented as polygons in geospatial data.
    - [Polygons](#polygons) — Polygons are vector boundaries used to delineate individual agricultural plots.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Parcels → Polygons → Individual agricultural plot polygons

<a id='land-classification'></a>
### Land classification — Clasificación de tierras
*method* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** Land classification is the process of assigning semantic labels to pixels or objects in satellite imagery based on their spectral, temporal, or spatial characteristics, distinguishing land cover or land use categories.
- **ES.** La clasificación de tierras es el proceso de asignar etiquetas semánticas a píxeles u objetos en imágenes satelitales basándose en sus características espectrales, temporales o espaciales, distinguiendo categorías de cobertura del suelo o uso del suelo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classes](#classes) — It uses predefined classes, such as forest or cropland, to categorize land cover.
    - [Land](#land) — Land classification assigns labels to land cover types observed on the Earth's surface.
    - [Satellite imagery](#satellite-imagery) — Satellite imagery provides the spectral data needed for land classification.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite imagery → Land classification

<a id='land-cover'></a>
### Land cover — Cobertura del suelo
*phenomenon* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** The observed biophysical material on the Earth's surface, such as forest, water, or cropland. It is directly detectable by remote sensing sensors and distinct from land use.
- **ES.** El material biofísico observado sobre la superficie terrestre, como bosque, agua o tierras de cultivo. Es directamente detectable por sensores de teledetección y distinto del uso del suelo.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classes](#classes) — In classification, land cover is one of the classes assigned to pixels or objects.
    - [Forest](#forest) — Forest is a land cover type characterized by dense tree cover in remote sensing imagery.
    - [Land cover mapping](#land-cover-mapping) — Land cover mapping produces thematic maps showing the distribution of land cover types.
    - [Classification scheme](#classification-scheme) — Land cover classes are organized by a classification scheme into a hierarchical system.
    - [Cover](#cover) — Land cover is the observed biophysical material on the Earth's surface, such as forest or cropland.
    - [Land cover map](#land-cover-map) — A land cover map displays the spatial distribution of land cover classes.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Land cover map → Land cover

<a id='land-use-mapping'></a>
### Land use mapping — Mapeo de uso del suelo
*method* · sources: th_lucc
- **EN.** Land use mapping classifies land according to its socioeconomic function, such as agriculture, forestry, or urban areas, using satellite imagery and ancillary data. It differs from land cover mapping by inferring human activity.
- **ES.** El mapeo de uso del suelo clasifica la tierra según su función socioeconómica, como agricultura, silvicultura o áreas urbanas, utilizando imágenes satelitales y datos auxiliares. Se diferencia del mapeo de cobertura terrestre al inferir la actividad humana.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Land](#land) — Land use mapping classifies land according to its use, based on understanding the Earth's surface.
    - [Mapping](#mapping) — Land use mapping produces themes showing socioeconomic functions, building on general mapping processes.
    - [LULC mapping](#land-cover-land-use-mapping) — LULC mapping integrates both biophysical cover and human-use categories into a single thematic map.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Mapping → Land use mapping

<a id='machine-learning-algorithms'></a>
### Machine learning algorithms — Algoritmos de aprendizaje automático
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** Computational methods that learn patterns from data to make predictions or decisions without explicit programming for each task.
- **ES.** Métodos computacionales que aprenden patrones a partir de datos para hacer predicciones o tomar decisiones sin programación explícita para cada tarea.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Machine learning algorithms are specific techniques like random forest or SVM used within machine learning.
    - [Algorithm](#algorithm) — Machine learning algorithms apply an algorithm to learn patterns from data for prediction.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → Machine learning algorithms

<a id='microwave'></a>
### Microwave — Microondas
*method* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** Electromagnetic radiation with wavelengths from 1 mm to 1 m, used in remote sensing by radar satellites like Sentinel-1 and GF-3, which can penetrate clouds and operate day or night.
- **ES.** Radiación electromagnética con longitudes de onda de 1 mm a 1 m, utilizada en teledetección por satélites de Radar como Sentinel-1 y GF-3, que pueden penetrar nubes y operar de día o noche.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Radar](#radar) — Radar operates in the microwave portion of the spectrum, allowing day-and-night and all-weather imaging.
    - [Electromagnetic radiation](#electromagnetic-radiation) — Microwave radiation is electromagnetic radiation with wavelengths from 1 mm to 1 m, used by radar sensors.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Radar → Microwave

<a id='mlp-models'></a>
### MLP models — modelos MLP
*method* · sources: th_machine_learning
- **EN.** A type of feedforward artificial neural network consisting of an input layer, one or more hidden layers, and an output layer, used for classification and regression.
- **ES.** Un tipo de red neuronal artificial feedforward que consta de una capa de entrada, una o más capas ocultas y una capa de salida, utilizada para clasificación y regresión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Neural networks](#neural-networks) — MLP models are a specific type of neural network with fully connected layers.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Neural networks → MLP models

<a id='model-development'></a>
### Model Development — Desarrollo de modelos
*method* · sources: cy_indonesia
- **EN.** The process of creating, training, and tuning a computational model, such as a machine learning classifier, to perform a specific task like crop classification.
- **ES.** El proceso de crear, entrenar y ajustar un modelo computacional, como un clasificador de aprendizaje automático, para realizar una tarea específica como la clasificación de cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — Model development is the process of creating, training, and tuning a computational model.
    - [Training](#training) — Model development involves training a model on labeled data to learn patterns.
    - [Model evaluation](#model-evaluation) — Model development includes model evaluation to assess performance and guide improvements.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Performance → Model evaluation → Model Development

<a id='national-scale-mapping'></a>
### National scale mapping — Cartografía a escala nacional
*method* · sources: ct_zimbabwe
- **EN.** The production of thematic maps covering an entire country, typically using Earth observation data and automated methods to support agricultural statistics and policy.
- **ES.** Producción de mapas temáticos que cubren un país completo, utilizando típicamente datos de observación de la Tierra y métodos automatizados para apoyar las estadísticas agrícolas y las políticas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Mapping](#mapping) — National scale mapping applies mapping techniques to produce country-wide thematic maps.
    - [Satellite imagery](#satellite-imagery) — Satellite imagery covering entire countries enables national scale mapping.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Mapping → National scale mapping

<a id='optical'></a>
### Optical — Óptico
*sensor* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** A type of remote sensing sensor that measures reflected solar radiation in visible, near-infrared, and shortwave infrared wavelengths. It is passive and requires sunlight.
- **ES.** Tipo de sensor de teledetección que mide la radiación solar reflejada en longitudes de onda visibles, infrarrojo cercano e infrarrojo de onda corta. Es pasivo y requiere luz solar.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite sensors](#satellite-sensors) — Optical sensors on satellites measure reflected solar radiation in these wavelength ranges.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors → Optical

<a id='orthophoto'></a>
### Orthophoto — Ortofoto
*product* · sources: uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** A geometrically corrected aerial or satellite image where distortions due to terrain relief and camera tilt have been removed, making it usable for accurate area measurement and map creation.
- **ES.** Una imagen aérea o satelital corregida geométricamente donde se han eliminado las distorsiones debidas al relieve del terreno y la inclinación de la cámara, haciéndola utilizable para la medición precisa de áreas y la creación de mapas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Images](#images) — An orthophoto is a geometrically corrected image where distortions from terrain and camera have been removed.
    - [Basemap](#basemap) — A basemap is often an orthophoto that provides accurate geographic context for digitizing.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Basemap → Orthophoto

<a id='phenological-stage'></a>
### Phenological stage — Etapa fenológica
*phenomenon* · sources: cy_colombia
- **EN.** A distinct phase in a plant's growth cycle, such as germination, leaf development, tillering, or flowering. These stages are used to classify crop development and map agricultural dynamics.
- **ES.** Una fase distinta en el ciclo de crecimiento de una planta, como germinación, desarrollo de hojas, macollamiento o floración. Estas etapas se utilizan para clasificar el desarrollo de los cultivos y mapear la dinámica agrícola.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Crop development progresses through defined phenological stages from sowing to harvest.
    - [Tillering samples](#tillering-samples) — These samples capture the spectral signature during the tillering phase of crop development.
    - [Phenology](#phenology) — A phenological stage is a distinct phase in the growth cycle of a crop, such as flowering or maturity.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Label → Training samples → Tillering samples → Phenological stage

<a id='planet'></a>
### Planet — Planet
*platform* · sources: th_parcel_extraction
- **EN.** A commercial satellite imagery provider offering high-resolution (3–5 m) multispectral data, often used for detailed agricultural mapping and validation.
- **ES.** Proveedor comercial de imágenes satelitales que ofrece datos multiespectrales de alta resolución (3–5 m), a menudo utilizado para cartografía agrícola detallada y validación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Planet is a commercial satellite constellation that provides high-resolution multispectral imagery daily.
    - [Satellite imagery](#satellite-imagery) — Planet's satellites capture imagery similar to other missions but with higher spatial resolution.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite imagery → Planet

<a id='population'></a>
### Population — Población
*statistic* · sources: crop_statistics_calibration
- **EN.** The entire collection of statistical units (e.g., all pixels in a study area) from which a sample is drawn; in survey sampling, the target set for inference.
- **ES.** La colección completa de unidades estadísticas (ej. todos los Píxeles en un Área de Estudio) de la cual se extrae una Muestra; en encuestas por muestreo, el conjunto objetivo para la Inferencia.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Sampling](#sampling) — Sampling selects a subset of units from a population to estimate characteristics while reducing cost.
    - [Statistical unit](#statistical-unit) — The population is the complete set of statistical units (e.g., all fields) from which a sample is drawn.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling → Population

<a id='quality-framework'></a>
### Quality framework — Marco de calidad
*method* · sources: th_alignment
- **EN.** A structured set of criteria and procedures to assess the fitness-for-use of in-situ survey data for Earth observation applications, covering sampling design, response design, and EO-based post-hoc checks.
- **ES.** Un conjunto estructurado de criterios y procedimientos para evaluar la idoneidad de los datos de encuestas in situ para aplicaciones de observación de la Tierra, que abarca el diseño de muestreo, el diseño de respuesta y las verificaciones posteriores basadas en EO.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Quality](#quality) — A quality framework is a structured set of criteria to assess the fitness‑for‑use of in‑situ survey data.
    - [Framework](#framework) — The quality framework provides standardized procedures for evaluating and documenting data quality.
    - [FAO situ quality framework](#fao-situ-quality-framework) — The FAO situ quality framework is a specific quality framework for assessing field survey data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Ground surveys → FAO situ quality framework → Quality framework

<a id='radar-vegetation-index'></a>
### Radar Vegetation Index — Índice de Vegetación Radar
*index* · sources: cy_colombia#dual-polarimetric-radar-vegetation-index-dprvi
- **EN.** An index derived from radar satellite data, such as the Dual-polarimetric Radar Vegetation Index (DpRVI), designed to track vegetation growth by measuring canopy structural complexity.
- **ES.** Un índice derivado de datos satelitales de radar, como el Índice de Vegetación Radar Dual-Polarimétrico (DpRVI), diseñado para seguir el crecimiento de la vegetación midiendo la complejidad estructural del dosel.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Radar](#radar) — Radar vegetation indices use radar backscatter from different polarizations to estimate vegetation structure.
    - [Polarization](#polarization) — The radar vegetation index leverages cross- and co-polarized signals to separate vegetation from soil.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Radar → Radar Vegetation Index

<a id='random-training-testing-datasets'></a>
### Random training testing datasets — Conjuntos de datos aleatorios de entrenamiento y prueba
*data* · sources: ct_poland
- **EN.** Subsets of available samples randomly assigned to train a model and evaluate its performance, ensuring unbiased assessment.
- **ES.** Subconjuntos de muestras disponibles asignados aleatoriamente para entrenar un modelo y evaluar su rendimiento, garantizando una evaluación insesgada.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Random training-testing datasets randomly partition samples into training and testing sets.
    - [Dataset](#dataset) — Random training-testing datasets split a dataset into subsets by random assignment for evaluation.
    - [Data Division](#data-division) — Data division randomly assigns samples to training and testing sets to ensure unbiased evaluation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Data Division → Random training testing datasets

<a id='regression'></a>
### Regression — Regresión
*method* · sources: cy_poland
- **EN.** A statistical method that models the relationship between a dependent variable (e.g., crop yield) and one or more independent variables (e.g., vegetation indices), used for prediction.
- **ES.** Método estadístico que modela la relación entre una variable dependiente (por ejemplo, rendimiento del cultivo) y una o más variables independientes (por ejemplo, índices de vegetación), utilizado para la predicción.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Regression is a statistical method that models relationships between a dependent and independent variables.
    - [Values](#values) — It uses numeric values of predictors to predict a continuous outcome, such as crop yield.
    - [PLSR model](#plsr-model) — PLSR model is a multivariate regression method that handles many correlated predictors.
    - [Crop yield estimation](#crop-yield-estimation) — Crop yield estimation often employs regression models relating vegetation indices to yield.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Crop yield estimation → Regression

<a id='representativeness'></a>
### Representativeness — Representatividad
*statistic* · sources: th_design_frames#matching-in-situ-survey-data-to-remote-sensing-analysis-needs · th_quality_control#validation
- **EN.** The degree to which a sample or dataset accurately reflects the diversity of the target population (e.g., land cover classes). High representativeness ensures that model training data covers the full variability of the area of interest.
- **ES.** El grado en que una muestra o conjunto de datos refleja con precisión la diversidad de la población objetivo (por ejemplo, clases de cobertura terrestre). Una alta representatividad asegura que los datos de entrenamiento del modelo cubran toda la variabilidad del área de interés.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Representativeness ensures that the collected samples reflect the diversity of the entire population for accurate estimates.
    - [Sampling](#sampling) — Sampling designs aim to achieve representativeness so that sample statistics can be generalized to the whole area.
    - [Robust sampling frame](#robust-sampling-frame) — Robust sampling frames ensure representativeness of the target population for valid inference.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling → Representativeness

<a id='reproducible-code'></a>
### Reproducible code — Código reproducible
*software* · sources: howto
- **EN.** Analysis code (e.g., R, Python scripts) that can be executed by others to produce identical results, often packaged in a containerized environment with all dependencies and data.
- **ES.** Código de análisis (por ejemplo, scripts en R o Python) que otros pueden ejecutar para producir resultados idénticos, a menudo empaquetado en un entorno contenerizado con todas las dependencias y datos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Reproducible analysis system](#reproducible-analysis-system) — The reproducible analysis system packages the chapter's reproducible code into a pre-configured JupyterLab environment.
    - [Workflow](#workflow) — Reproducible code encapsulates the entire workflow from data loading to figure generation in a shareable script.
    - [Software](#software) — Reproducible code packages analysis scripts and dependencies so that others can rerun the same computations.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Step → Process → Workflow → Reproducible code

<a id='satellite-image-analysis'></a>
### Satellite Image Analysis — Análisis de imágenes satelitales
*method* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The use of computer algorithms to interpret data collected by satellite-mounted sensors, extracting meaningful information about Earth's surface for applications like agriculture.
- **ES.** Uso de algoritmos computacionales para interpretar datos recolectados por sensores montados en satélites, extrayendo información significativa sobre la superficie de la Tierra para aplicaciones como la agricultura.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Algorithm](#algorithm) — Algorithms interpret satellite imagery to extract meaningful patterns and information.
    - [Satellite imagery](#satellite-imagery) — Satellite imagery is the primary input for analysis using computer algorithms.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → Satellite Image Analysis

<a id='satellite-imagery-nasa-english'></a>
### Satellite Imagery NASA English — imágenes satelitales de la NASA
*data* · sources: ad_learning
- **EN.** A NASA-provided training course in English that teaches the application of satellite remote sensing to agricultural monitoring, including crop classification and vegetation indices.
- **ES.** Curso de capacitación proporcionado por la NASA en inglés que enseña la aplicación de la teledetección satelital al monitoreo agrícola, incluida la clasificación de cultivos y los índices de vegetación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite imagery](#satellite-imagery) — Satellite Imagery NASA English is a NASA training course utilizing satellite imagery for agriculture.
    - [Training program](#training-program) — It is a structured training program provided in English.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite imagery → Satellite Imagery NASA English

<a id='satellite-vegetation-indices'></a>
### Satellite vegetation indices — Índices de vegetación satelitales
*index* · sources: th_remote_sensing · th_design_frames
- **EN.** Mathematical combinations of spectral bands that highlight vegetation properties, such as NDVI (Normalized Difference Vegetation Index), used to assess crop health, biomass, and phenology.
- **ES.** Combinaciones matemáticas de bandas espectrales que resaltan propiedades de la vegetación, como el NDVI (Índice de Vegetación de Diferencia Normalizada), utilizados para evaluar la salud, biomasa y fenología de los cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Vegetation indices](#vegetation-indices) — Satellite vegetation indices are mathematical combinations of spectral bands computed from satellite sensors.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cover → Vegetation → Vegetation indices → Satellite vegetation indices

<a id='satellite-derived-models'></a>
### Satellite-derived models — Modelos derivados de satélite
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_ppi#example-yield-estimation · cy_finland#machine-learning
- **EN.** Computational models that use satellite imagery as input to predict biophysical variables (e.g., crop yield, plant area index) or classify land surface types. They are calibrated with ground observations and can be statistical or machine-learning based.
- **ES.** Modelos computacionales que utilizan imágenes satelitales como entrada para predecir variables biofísicas (por ejemplo, rendimiento de cultivos, índice de área foliar) o clasificar tipos de superficie terrestre. Se basan en observaciones de campo y pueden ser estadísticos o de aprendizaje automático.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — Satellite-derived models use satellite imagery as input to predict biophysical variables like crop yield or biomass.
    - [Satellite imagery](#satellite-imagery) — Satellite imagery provides the input data for training and applying satellite-derived models to estimate agricultural parameters.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite imagery → Satellite-derived models

<a id='soil-vegetation-index'></a>
### Soil Vegetation Index — Índice de vegetación de suelo
*index* · sources: uav_crop_growth#methods
- **EN.** A spectral index, such as OSAVI, that minimizes soil background effects to better estimate vegetation cover and vigor from remote sensing data.
- **ES.** Índice espectral, como el OSAVI, que minimiza los efectos del fondo del suelo para estimar mejor la cobertura y el vigor de la vegetación a partir de datos de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Soil](#soil) — This index adjusts for soil brightness to improve vegetation signal in areas with partial cover.
    - [Vegetation indices](#vegetation-indices) — A soil-vegetation index (e.g., OSAVI) minimizes soil background influence to better estimate vegetation cover.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cover → Vegetation → Vegetation indices → Soil Vegetation Index

<a id='space-agency'></a>
### Space agency — Agencia espacial
*organization* · sources: introduction · th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** A national or international organization responsible for space exploration, satellite development, and Earth observation programs.
- **ES.** Una organización nacional o internacional responsable de la exploración espacial, el desarrollo de satélites y los programas de observación de la Tierra.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — A space agency operates and launches satellites that provide Earth observation data.
    - [Sentinel Missions](#sentinel-missions) — Sentinel missions are operated by the European Space Agency (ESA) as part of the Copernicus program.
    - [NASA](#nasa) — Space agencies like NASA develop and manage satellite missions for remote sensing.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Landsat → Harmonized Landsat Sentinel → Sentinel Missions → Space agency

<a id='spatial-analysis'></a>
### Spatial Analysis — Análisis espacial
*method* · sources: uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** The process of examining locations, attributes, and relationships of features in spatial data. In this handbook, it includes operations like zonal statistics, buffering, and coordinate reference system harmonization.
- **ES.** El proceso de examinar ubicaciones, atributos y relaciones de características en datos espaciales. En este manual, incluye operaciones como estadísticas zonales, búfer y armonización del sistema de referencia de coordenadas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Geographic information systems](#geographic-information-systems) — Spatial analysis uses GIS tools to examine locations, patterns, and relationships in geographic data.
    - [Geospatial Data](#geospatial-data) — It operates on geospatial data, including satellite imagery and vector boundaries, to derive spatial statistics.
    - [Geospatial analysis](#geospatial-analysis) — Geospatial analysis applies spatial analysis techniques to geographic data like satellite imagery.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Geoinformatics → Geographic information systems → Spatial Analysis

<a id='spectral-bands'></a>
### Spectral bands — Bandas espectrales
*data* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** Discrete wavelength intervals in the electromagnetic spectrum recorded by a sensor, such as visible, near-infrared, or shortwave infrared bands, used to differentiate Earth surface materials.
- **ES.** Intervalos discretos de longitud de onda en el espectro electromagnético registrados por un sensor, como bandas visibles, infrarrojo cercano o infrarrojo de onda corta, utilizados para diferenciar materiales de la superficie terrestre.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Bands](#bands) — Bands are discrete spectral channels in satellite imagery that capture reflectance in specific wavelength ranges.
    - [Indices](#indices) — Indices are computed by mathematically combining two or more spectral bands.
    - [Satellite sensors](#satellite-sensors) — Satellite sensors capture data in distinct wavelength intervals known as spectral bands.
    - [Wavelength](#wavelength) — Each spectral band corresponds to a narrow range of wavelengths in the electromagnetic spectrum.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors → Spectral bands

<a id='statistical-methods'></a>
### Statistical methods — Métodos estadísticos
*method* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** Techniques for designing surveys, analyzing data, and drawing inferences. In remote sensing, they include sampling design, unbiased area estimation, accuracy assessment, and regression estimators.
- **ES.** Técnicas para diseñar encuestas, analizar datos y realizar inferencias. En teledetección, incluyen diseño muestral, estimación de área insesgada, evaluación de precisión y estimadores de regresión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Statistical methods provide techniques for estimating crop area, yield, and accuracy from sample data.
    - [Sampling](#sampling) — They rely on sampling theory to select representative units and draw inferences about the population.
    - [Statistical](#statistical) — The term 'statistical' refers to methods grounded in probability and inference, derived from statistical methods.
    - [Statistical survey](#statistical-survey) — A statistical survey applies statistical methods to collect and analyze data for official statistics.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling → Statistical methods

<a id='statistical-rigor'></a>
### Statistical rigor — Rigor estadístico
*metric* · sources: th_design_frames
- **EN.** The application of sound statistical principles, such as probability-based sampling and unbiased estimation, to ensure that remote sensing products meet standards for official statistics.
- **ES.** Aplicación de principios estadísticos sólidos, como el muestreo basado en probabilidad y la estimación insesgada, para garantizar que los productos de teledetección cumplan con los estándares de las estadísticas oficiales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — Statistics provide the foundation for rigorous methods in sampling and estimation.
    - [Estimator](#estimator) — Rigorous application of estimators ensures unbiased and precise statistical inference.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator → Statistical rigor

<a id='statistical-systems'></a>
### Statistical systems — Sistemas estadísticos
*other* · sources: introduction · th_design_frames
- **EN.** The institutional frameworks, methods, and data infrastructure used by national offices to produce official statistics, such as agricultural production estimates.
- **ES.** Los marcos institucionales, métodos e infraestructura de datos utilizados por las oficinas nacionales para producir estadísticas oficiales, como las estimaciones de producción agrícola.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [System](#system) — Statistical systems are the structured frameworks for producing official statistics.
    - [Statistics](#statistics) — They encompass methods, data, and institutions for generating reliable agricultural statistics.
    - [National statistical systems](#national-statistical-systems) — National statistical systems are the country-level implementations of statistical systems to produce official statistics.
    - [National Statistical Offices](#national-statistical-offices) — National Statistical Offices are government agencies within national statistical systems that produce official statistics.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Agricultural Statistics → Official agricultural statistics → National Statistical Offices → Statistical systems

<a id='survey-approach'></a>
### Survey approach — Enfoque de encuesta
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_ppi#mean-estimation
- **EN.** A statistical method that relies solely on a random sample of ground-truth data to estimate a quantity (e.g., mean yield) without using satellite map predictions.
- **ES.** Un método estadístico que se basa únicamente en una muestra aleatoria de datos de verdad terreno para estimar una cantidad (por ejemplo, rendimiento medio) sin utilizar predicciones de mapa satelital.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Estimation](#estimation) — The survey approach is a pure estimation method that does not incorporate satellite map predictions.
    - [Sampling](#sampling) — The survey approach uses a probability sample of ground observations to make unbiased population estimates.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling → Survey approach

<a id='synthetic-aperture-radar'></a>
### Synthetic Aperture Radar — Radar de Apertura Sintética
*sensor* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** A radar imaging technique that uses the motion of the satellite antenna to simulate a larger aperture, producing high-resolution images. It can penetrate clouds and operate day and night.
- **ES.** Una técnica de imágenes de radar que utiliza el movimiento de la antena del satélite para simular una apertura más grande, produciendo imágenes de alta resolución. Puede penetrar nubes y operar de día y de noche.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — A SAR satellite transmits radar pulses and records the echoes to create high-resolution images of the Earth.
    - [Radar](#radar) — Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) uses the motion of a satellite to simulate a larger antenna aperture.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Radar → Synthetic Aperture Radar

<a id='transferability'></a>
### Transferability — Transferibilidad
*method* · sources: ad_world_cereal
- **EN.** The ability of a machine learning model or classification system to maintain predictive performance when applied to new geographic regions, time periods, or conditions not seen during training.
- **ES.** Capacidad de un modelo de aprendizaje automático o sistema de clasificación para mantener el rendimiento predictivo al aplicarse a nuevas regiones geográficas, períodos de tiempo o condiciones no vistas durante el entrenamiento.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Model](#model) — Transferability is a model's ability to maintain predictive performance when applied to new regions or times.
    - [Transferable classification system](#transferable-classification-system) — A transferable classification system ensures transferability by maintaining accuracy across contexts.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Land cover classes → Classification Systems → Transferable classification system → Transferability

<a id='unbiased-area-estimates'></a>
### Unbiased area estimates — Estimaciones de área insesgadas
*statistic* · sources: th_validation · crop_statistics_area
- **EN.** Area estimates corrected for classification errors (omission and commission) using statistically rigorous methods such as stratified random sampling and the error-adjusted estimator. They provide accurate figures with confidence intervals.
- **ES.** Estimaciones de área corregidas por errores de clasificación (omisión y comisión) mediante métodos estadísticamente rigurosos, como el muestreo aleatorio estratificado y el estimador ajustado por error. Proporcionan cifras precisas con intervalos de confianza.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Area estimation](#area-estimation) — Unbiased area estimates correct for classification errors using statistically rigorous methods derived from area estimation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Area estimation → Unbiased area estimates

<a id='undersampling'></a>
### Undersampling — Submuestreo
*method* · sources: th_quality_control · th_quality_control
- **EN.** A technique that reduces the number of samples from overrepresented classes to balance the training dataset, often using Self-Organizing Maps (SOM).
- **ES.** Técnica que reduce el número de muestras de clases sobrerrepresentadas para equilibrar el conjunto de datos de entrenamiento, a menudo empleando Mapas Autoorganizados (SOM).
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Training dataset](#training-dataset) — Undersampling reduces the number of samples in overrepresented classes to balance the training dataset.
    - [Sample balancing](#sample-balancing) — It is a sample balancing technique that alleviates class imbalance by removing majority class samples.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Label → Training samples → Sample balancing → Undersampling

<a id='validation-datasets'></a>
### Validation datasets — Conjuntos de datos de validación
*data* · sources: th_validation · ct_zimbabwe
- **EN.** Labeled data independent from the training set used to assess the accuracy of a classification model. They enable unbiased evaluation metrics such as overall accuracy and F1-score.
- **ES.** Datos etiquetados independientes del conjunto de entrenamiento utilizados para evaluar la exactitud de un modelo de clasificación. Permiten métricas de evaluación no sesgadas como la precisión general y la puntuación F1.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Reference datasets](#reference-datasets) — Validation datasets are independent reference datasets used to assess the accuracy of a classification model.
    - [Accuracy assessment](#accuracy-assessment) — They enable accuracy assessment by providing ground truth for comparison with model predictions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Validation datasets

<a id='vector'></a>
### Vector — Vector
*data* · sources: uav_field_parcels
- **EN.** Geographic data represented by points, lines, and polygons, used to delineate features like field boundaries.
- **ES.** Datos geográficos representados por puntos, líneas y polígonos, utilizados para delinear atributos como los límites de los campos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Polygons](#polygons) — A vector object includes points, lines, and polygons; polygons represent field parcels in mapping.
    - [Points](#points) — A vector can represent a point, line, or polygon, enabling spatial analysis of discrete features.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Parcels → Polygons → Vector

<a id='vegetation-health'></a>
### Vegetation health — Salud de la vegetación
*phenomenon* · sources: uav_crop_growth · uav_crop_growth
- **EN.** A measure of the physiological condition and vitality of plants, often assessed using spectral indices like NDVI and GNDVI derived from satellite imagery.
- **ES.** Medida de la condición fisiológica y vitalidad de las plantas, a menudo evaluada mediante índices espectrales como NDVI y GNDVI derivados de imágenes satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Vegetation](#vegetation) — Vegetation health is assessed through remote sensing spectral indices that measure plant vigor.
    - [NDVI](#ndvi) — NDVI is a key indicator of vegetation health, correlating with green biomass.
    - [Chlorophyll](#chlorophyll) — Chlorophyll content is linked to vegetation health, as it drives photosynthesis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cover → Vegetation → NDVI → Vegetation health

<a id='zonal-statistics'></a>
### Zonal Statistics — Estadísticas Zonales
*method* · sources: uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** Statistical measures (e.g., mean, standard deviation) computed for each zone or polygon in a raster dataset, often used to summarize pixel values within field boundaries from remote sensing imagery.
- **ES.** Medidas estadísticas (ej. media, desviación estándar) calculadas para cada Zona o Polígono en un conjunto de datos ráster, a menudo utilizadas para resumir Valores de Píxeles dentro de límites de Campo a partir de Imágenes de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Polygons](#polygons) — Zonal statistics compute summary values (e.g., mean NDVI) for each polygon in a vector layer.
    - [Raster](#raster) — Zonal statistics summarize raster pixel values within each polygon zone to produce per-zone metrics.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Parcels → Polygons → Zonal Statistics


## Level 6

<a id='accuracy-metrics'></a>
### Accuracy metrics — Métricas de precisión
*metric* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** Quantitative measures used to evaluate the performance of a classification model, including overall accuracy, precision, recall, F1-score, and kappa coefficient.
- **ES.** Medidas cuantitativas utilizadas para evaluar el rendimiento de un modelo de clasificación, incluyendo la precisión general, la precisión, la exhaustividad, la puntuación F1 y el coeficiente Kappa.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Accuracy metrics are specific quantitative measures that evaluate how well a classification matches reality.
    - [Precision](#precision) — Precision is a classification metric derived from the confusion matrix.
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — From a confusion matrix, many accuracy metrics like producer's and user's accuracy are derived.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Accuracy metrics

<a id='area-weighted-error-matrices'></a>
### Area-Weighted Error Matrices — Matrices de error ponderadas por área
*metric* · sources: th_validation#accuracy-assessment-of-classified-images
- **EN.** An area-weighted error matrix adjusts the standard confusion matrix by weighting each cell by the proportion of area mapped as that class, providing unbiased accuracy and area estimates.
- **ES.** Una matriz de error ponderada por área ajusta la matriz de confusión estándar ponderando cada celda por la proporción de área mapeada como esa clase, proporcionando estimaciones de exactitud y área insesgadas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Area](#area) — Area weighting adjusts confusion matrices by the spatial extent of each class to reduce bias in accuracy metrics.
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — Area-weighted error matrices weight each cell by the proportion of area that cell represents in the map.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Area-Weighted Error Matrices

<a id='brazil-data-cube'></a>
### Brazil Data Cube — Brazil Data Cube
*data* · sources: th_data_sources · th_data_cubes
- **EN.** A cloud service providing open, regularized Earth observation data cubes from Sentinel-2, Landsat-8, CBERS-4/4A, and MODIS over Brazil. It provides ready-to-use data for machine learning classification.
- **ES.** Un servicio en la nube que proporciona cubos de datos de observación de la Tierra abiertos y regularizados a partir de Sentinel-2, Landsat-8, CBERS-4/4A y MODIS sobre Brasil. Proporciona datos listos para usar en clasificación por aprendizaje automático.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data cube](#data-cube) — The Brazil Data Cube is a cloud service providing open Earth observation data cubes from multiple satellite missions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite imagery → Data cube → Brazil Data Cube

<a id='chance-agreement'></a>
### Chance agreement — Acuerdo por azar
*metric* · sources: cy_colombia · cy_colombia
- **EN.** The proportion of classification agreement that would be expected by random chance, used as a baseline in metrics like Cohen’s Kappa.
- **ES.** La proporción de acuerdo en la clasificación que se esperaría por azar, utilizada como línea base en métricas como el Kappa de Cohen.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Overall accuracy](#overall-accuracy) — Chance agreement is a baseline that overall accuracy is compared against in Cohen's Kappa.
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — Chance agreement is the proportion of correct classifications expected by random labeling, derived from the confusion matrix.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Chance agreement

<a id='clustering'></a>
### Clustering — Agrupamiento
*method* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** A machine learning technique that groups a set of objects (e.g., satellite image pixels or time series) into clusters such that objects within the same cluster are more similar to each other than to those in other clusters. It is used for pattern discovery, data summarization, and sample quality control.
- **ES.** Una técnica de aprendizaje automático que agrupa un conjunto de objetos (por ejemplo, píxeles de imágenes satelitales o series temporales) en clústeres de modo que los objetos dentro del mismo clúster sean más similares entre sí que con los de otros clústeres. Se utiliza para descubrimiento de patrones, resumen de datos y control de calidad de muestras.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Cluster](#cluster) — Clustering is the process of partitioning data into clusters where points are similar to each other.
    - [Self-Organizing Maps](#self-organizing-maps) — Self-organizing maps are an unsupervised method that clusters high-dimensional data into a low-dimensional grid.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → Cluster → Clustering

<a id='clustering-algorithm'></a>
### Clustering Algorithm — Algoritmo de agrupamiento
*method* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** An unsupervised machine learning technique that groups similar data points (e.g., pixels or time series) into clusters based on feature similarity. Self-Organizing Maps (SOM) are a common clustering method for time series data.
- **ES.** Técnica de aprendizaje automático no supervisado que agrupa puntos de datos similares (por ejemplo, píxeles o series temporales) en clústeres basados en similitud de atributos. Los Mapas Autoorganizados (SOM) son un método común de agrupamiento para datos de series temporales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Algorithm](#algorithm) — Clustering algorithms are unsupervised methods that identify natural groupings in data without labels.
    - [Cluster](#cluster) — A clustering algorithm groups data points (e.g., pixels) into clusters based on feature similarity.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → Cluster → Clustering Algorithm

<a id='commission'></a>
### Commission — Comisión
*metric* · sources: th_validation#accuracy-assessment-of-classified-images
- **EN.** Commission error (false positive) occurs when a pixel or area is incorrectly assigned to a class in the map when it does not belong to that class in reality, leading to overestimation.
- **ES.** El error de comisión (falso positivo) ocurre cuando un píxel o área se asigna incorrectamente a una clase en el mapa cuando no pertenece a esa clase en la realidad, lo que lleva a una sobreestimación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Commission error occurs when a pixel is incorrectly labeled as a class it does not belong to.
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — In a confusion matrix, commission corresponds to false positives for a given class.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Commission

<a id='confusion-matrices'></a>
### Confusion matrices — Matrices de confusión
*metric* · sources: th_validation#accuracy-assessment-of-classified-images · ct_zimbabwe#accuracy-assessment
- **EN.** Synonym of confusion matrix. A cross-tabulation of predicted versus reference class labels used to assess classification accuracy.
- **ES.** Sinónimo de matriz de confusión. Tabulación cruzada de las etiquetas de clase predichas frente a las de referencia que se utiliza para evaluar la precisión de la clasificación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — Confusion matrices are the plural of confusion matrix; multiple confusion matrices can be used for different regions or classes.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Confusion matrices

<a id='crop-area'></a>
### Crop area — Área de cultivo
*statistic* · sources: th_validation#introduction
- **EN.** A fundamental agricultural statistic representing the total land extent cultivated with a specific crop, typically derived from classified satellite imagery and often corrected for map bias.
- **ES.** Una estadística agrícola fundamental que representa la extensión total de tierra cultivada con un cultivo específico, típicamente derivada de imágenes satelitales clasificadas y a menudo corregida por sesgo del mapa.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Area](#area) — Crop area is the spatial extent of land planted with a specific crop, often measured in hectares.
    - [Classification](#classification) — Crop area is estimated from classified satellite images by summing pixels per crop type.
    - [Estimation](#estimation) — Crop area estimation uses statistical methods to infer total planted area from samples.
    - [Acreage estimation](#acreage-estimation) — It aims to quantify the total land cultivated with a specific crop, i.e., crop area.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Area estimation → Acreage estimation → Crop area

<a id='crop-conditions'></a>
### Crop conditions — Condiciones de cultivo
*phenomenon* · sources: th_remote_sensing#introduction-to-remote-sensing-imagery
- **EN.** The state of agricultural vegetation, including health, vigor, and stress levels, as assessed through spectral and phenological indicators derived from satellite imagery.
- **ES.** El estado de la vegetación agrícola, incluyendo salud, vigor y niveles de estrés, evaluado mediante indicadores espectrales y fenológicos derivados de imágenes satelitales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Vegetation](#vegetation) — By analyzing spectral indices from satellite imagery, you assess crop conditions such as health and stress.
    - [Satellite vegetation indices](#satellite-vegetation-indices) — Satellite vegetation indices, like NDVI, quantify vegetation health and thus indicate crop conditions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Cover → Vegetation → Vegetation indices → Satellite vegetation indices → Crop conditions

<a id='crop-yield'></a>
### Crop yield — Rendimiento de cultivos
*statistic* · sources: cy_poland
- **EN.** The amount of a crop produced per unit of land area, typically expressed in kilograms per hectare or metric tons per hectare. It is a key agricultural statistic used for food security assessment, production forecasting, and policy planning.
- **ES.** La cantidad de un cultivo producida por unidad de área de tierra, típicamente expresada en kilogramos por hectárea o toneladas métricas por hectárea. Es una estadística agrícola clave utilizada para la evaluación de la seguridad alimentaria, el pronóstico de producción y la planificación de políticas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Crop](#crop) — Crop yield is the yield of a cultivated plant, measured per unit area for agricultural statistics.
    - [Yield](#yield) — Crop yield is the yield (mass per area) of a specific crop, estimated using remote sensing or surveys.
    - [Early season crop yield mapping](#early-season-crop-yield-mapping) — Crop yield is the target quantity estimated early in the season using satellite data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Mapping → Early season crop yield mapping → Crop yield

<a id='domain-shift'></a>
### Domain shift — Cambio de dominio
*phenomenon* · sources: th_parcel_extraction
- **EN.** A change in the statistical distribution of data between the source (training) domain and a target (application) domain, which can reduce the performance of a machine learning model applied to new conditions.
- **ES.** Cambio en la distribución estadística de los datos entre el dominio fuente (entrenamiento) y un dominio objetivo (aplicación), que puede reducir el rendimiento de un modelo de aprendizaje automático aplicado a nuevas condiciones.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Transferability](#transferability) — Domain shift, a change in data distribution between training and target domains, hinders model transferability.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Land cover classes → Classification Systems → Transferable classification system → Transferability → Domain shift

<a id='electromagnetic-spectrum'></a>
### Electromagnetic spectrum — Espectro electromagnético
*phenomenon* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The range of all types of electromagnetic radiation, from gamma rays to radio waves. Remote sensing uses specific portions of this spectrum, such as visible light, near-infrared, short-wave infrared, and microwaves, to collect information about Earth's surface features without physical contact.
- **ES.** El rango de todos los tipos de radiación electromagnética, desde rayos gamma hasta ondas de radio. La teledetección utiliza porciones específicas de este espectro, como luz visible, infrarrojo cercano, infrarrojo de onda corta y microondas, para recopilar información sobre las características de la superficie terrestre sin contacto físico.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Spectral reflectance](#spectral-reflectance) — It describes how surface materials reflect different portions of the electromagnetic spectrum.
    - [Optical](#optical) — Optical remote sensing uses visible and near-infrared portions of the electromagnetic spectrum.
    - [Electromagnetic radiation](#electromagnetic-radiation) — The electromagnetic spectrum is the full range of electromagnetic radiation wavelengths from gamma to radio.
    - [Spectral Range](#spectral-range) — Spectral range refers to a specific portion of the electromagnetic spectrum used for remote sensing.
    - [Wavelength](#wavelength) — The electromagnetic spectrum orders radiation by wavelength, from short to long waves.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors → Optical → Electromagnetic spectrum

<a id='foundation-model'></a>
### Foundation model — Modelo fundacional
*software* · sources: ad_world_cereal
- **EN.** A large pre-trained model that learns general representations from unlabeled data, such as satellite imagery, and can be fine-tuned for specific tasks like crop mapping with limited labeled samples.
- **ES.** Un modelo preentrenado grande que aprende representaciones generales a partir de datos no etiquetados, como imágenes satelitales, y puede ajustarse para tareas específicas como el mapeo de cultivos con muestras etiquetadas limitadas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Training](#training) — Foundation models are trained on massive unlabeled datasets and can be fine-tuned for specific tasks.
    - [Deep learning](#deep-learning) — A foundation model is a large pre-trained deep learning model that learns general representations from data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Neural networks → Deep learning → Foundation model

<a id='geographical-science'></a>
### Geographical Science — Ciencia geográfica
*other* · sources: about · th_lucc
- **EN.** The academic field that studies spatial relationships and patterns of physical and human phenomena on Earth's surface, using tools like GIS and remote sensing.
- **ES.** Campo académico que estudia las relaciones espaciales y los patrones de fenómenos físicos y humanos en la superficie de la Tierra, utilizando herramientas como SIG y teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Geoinformatics](#geoinformatics) — Geographical science provides the theoretical foundation for geoinformatics.
    - [Spatial Analysis](#spatial-analysis) — It studies spatial patterns and relationships, which spatial analysis applies.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Geoinformatics → Geographic information systems → Spatial Analysis → Geographical Science

<a id='geoprocessing'></a>
### Geoprocessing — Geoprocesamiento
*method* · sources: th_parcel_extraction
- **EN.** The manipulation and analysis of spatial data using specialized software to derive information, including operations like buffering, overlay, and spatial joins.
- **ES.** La manipulación y análisis de datos espaciales utilizando software especializado para derivar información, incluyendo operaciones como búfer, superposición y uniones espaciales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Geographic information systems](#geographic-information-systems) — Geoprocessing implements the analytical functions of a geographic information system.
    - [Spatial Analysis](#spatial-analysis) — Geoprocessing is a set of spatial analysis operations that manipulate geographic data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Geoinformatics → Geographic information systems → Spatial Analysis → Geoprocessing

<a id='ground-truth'></a>
### Ground-truth — Verdad terreno
*data* · sources: th_validation#introduction · th_quality_control#outline
- **EN.** Data collected by direct observation or measurement on the Earth's surface, used to calibrate and validate remote sensing analyses and classification models.
- **ES.** Datos recopilados mediante observación directa o medición en la superficie de la Tierra, utilizados para calibrar y validar análisis de teledetección y modelos de clasificación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Field](#field) — Field observations of real land cover conditions are directly used to create ground-truth data for training and validation.
