    - [Data collection](#data-collection) — Ground truth data collected via field surveys forms the basis for training and validation.
    - [Reference datasets](#reference-datasets) — Reference datasets are collections of ground-truth observations used to train and validate models.
    - [Survey approach](#survey-approach) — Ground-truth data from field surveys are the sole input for the survey approach's estimations.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling → Survey approach → Ground-truth

<a id='jupyter-notebook'></a>
### Jupyter Notebook — Jupyter Notebook
*software* · sources: howto · howto
- **EN.** An interactive web-based computing environment that supports R, Python, and other languages, used for reproducible data analysis and visualization.
- **ES.** Entorno informático interactivo basado en web que admite R, Python y otros lenguajes, utilizado para el análisis de datos reproducible y la visualización.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Reproducible code](#reproducible-code) — Jupyter Notebooks enable reproducible code by combining narrative text with executable code cells.
    - [JupyterLab](#jupyterlab) — A Jupyter Notebook runs within JupyterLab, providing an interactive computing environment for analysis.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Step → Process → Workflow → Reproducible code → Jupyter Notebook

<a id='kappa-coefficient'></a>
### Kappa Coefficient — Coeficiente Kappa
*metric* · sources: th_quality_control#validation
- **EN.** The Kappa coefficient is a statistical measure of agreement between classified map and reference data, accounting for chance agreement. Values range from -1 to 1, with higher values indicating better accuracy.
- **ES.** El Coeficiente Kappa es una medida estadística de concordancia entre un Mapa clasificado y datos de Referencia, que considera el acuerdo por azar. Los valores varían de -1 a 1, donde valores más altos indican mejor Exactitud.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Overall accuracy](#overall-accuracy) — Kappa coefficient goes beyond overall accuracy by accounting for chance agreement in classification.
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — Kappa coefficient measures agreement between classified map and reference data, adjusting for chance agreement.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Kappa Coefficient

<a id='omission'></a>
### Omission — Omisión
*metric* · sources: th_validation#accuracy-assessment-of-classified-images
- **EN.** Omission error (false negative) occurs when a pixel or area that belongs to a class in reality is not classified as that class by the map, leading to underestimation of that class's extent.
- **ES.** El error de omisión (falso negativo) ocurre cuando un píxel o área que pertenece a una clase en la realidad no es clasificado como esa clase por el mapa, lo que lleva a una subestimación de la extensión de esa clase.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification](#classification) — Omission error occurs when a pixel belonging to a class on the ground is missed in the classified map.
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — In a confusion matrix, omission corresponds to false negatives for a given class.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Omission

<a id='prediction-probabilities'></a>
### Prediction Probabilities — Probabilidades de predicción
*metric* · sources: th_uncertainty#measuring-uncertainty
- **EN.** Prediction probabilities are the output values from a classification model that represent the estimated likelihood that a pixel belongs to each possible class, typically ranging from 0 to 1.
- **ES.** Las probabilidades de predicción son los valores de salida de un modelo de clasificación que representan la probabilidad estimada de que un píxel pertenezca a cada clase posible, típicamente en un rango de 0 a 1.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Machine learning](#machine-learning) — Machine learning models often produce prediction probabilities for each class, indicating confidence.
    - [Classification algorithm](#classification-algorithm) — Classification algorithms output prediction probabilities representing the likelihood of a pixel belonging to each class.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → Classification algorithm → Prediction Probabilities

<a id='producer-s-accuracy'></a>
### Producer's accuracy — Precisión del productor
*metric* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** The probability that a pixel of a given class on the ground is correctly classified on the map, calculated as 1 minus the omission error rate. It measures how well the map represents that class.
- **ES.** La probabilidad de que un píxel de una clase dada en el terreno esté correctamente clasificado en el mapa, calculada como 1 menos la tasa de error de omisión. Mide qué tan bien el mapa representa esa clase.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Producer's accuracy is the probability that a ground truth pixel is correctly classified on the map.
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — From a confusion matrix, producer's accuracy is computed by dividing correct class pixels by the column total.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Producer's accuracy

<a id='recall'></a>
### Recall — Exhaustividad
*metric* · sources: th_validation · cy_colombia
- **EN.** The proportion of actual positive instances correctly identified by a classifier, also called Producer's Accuracy. It measures omission errors.
- **ES.** La proporción de instancias positivas reales identificadas correctamente por un clasificador, también llamada precisión del productor. Mide los errores de omisión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Accuracy](#accuracy) — Recall is derived from the confusion matrix as the true positives divided by the sum of true positives and false negatives.
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — In a confusion matrix, recall for a class is the proportion of actual positives correctly identified.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Recall

<a id='red-reflectance'></a>
### Red reflectance — Reflectancia roja
*data* · sources: th_remote_sensing#sentinel-2 · uav_wheat_growth#machine-learning-algorithms
- **EN.** The proportion of incident solar radiation reflected by a surface in the red portion of the visible spectrum (approximately 620–700 nm). It is inversely related to chlorophyll absorption and is used to compute vegetation indices.
- **ES.** La proporción de radiación solar incidente reflejada por una superficie en la porción roja del espectro visible (aproximadamente 620–700 nm). Es inversamente proporcional a la absorción de clorofila y se utiliza para calcular índices de vegetación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Spectral bands](#spectral-bands) — The red spectral band (around 600-700 nm) measures red reflectance from the Earth's surface.
    - [Reflectance](#reflectance) — Red reflectance is the portion of incident light reflected in the red spectral region, a key input for vegetation indices.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors → Spectral bands → Red reflectance

<a id='reproducibility'></a>
### Reproducibility — Reproducibilidad
*method* · sources: howto
- **EN.** The ability to obtain identical results from the same data and analysis methods, achieved through version control, content-hashed data snapshots, and containerized environments.
- **ES.** Capacidad de obtener resultados idénticos a partir de los mismos datos y métodos de análisis, lograda mediante el control de versiones, instantáneas de datos con hash de contenido y entornos contenerizados.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Reproducible analysis sessions](#reproducible-analysis-sessions) — Such sessions ensure reproducibility by encapsulating all software and data needed to re-run an analysis.
    - [Data code availability](#data-code-availability) — Data code availability enables reproducibility by sharing the data and code used in analysis.
    - [Software](#software) — Reproducibility relies on software containers or virtual environments that replicate the exact computational setup.
    - [Reproducible code](#reproducible-code) — Reproducibility in research is achieved by sharing the reproducible code along with data and environment specifications.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** System → Methods → Step → Process → Workflow → Reproducible code → Reproducibility

<a id='sample-design'></a>
### Sample design — Diseño muestral
*method* · sources: th_validation · crop_statistics_regression
- **EN.** The procedure for selecting a subset of units from a larger population to make inferences about that population, ensuring representativeness.
- **ES.** El procedimiento para seleccionar un subconjunto de unidades de una población más grande para hacer inferencias sobre esa población, asegurando la representatividad.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Sampling](#sampling) — Sample design is the detailed plan for how sampling is implemented, including selection methods.
    - [Design estimator](#design-estimator) — Sample design determines the inclusion probabilities that a design estimator uses.
    - [Statistical survey](#statistical-survey) — A statistical survey follows a sample design to select units and derive population estimates.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator → Design estimator → Sample design

<a id='sample-based-estimators'></a>
### Sample-based estimators — Estimadores basados en muestras
*statistic* · sources: crop_statistics_area#sec-methods · th_validation#sampling-design
- **EN.** Statistical methods that derive area or other population totals from a probability sample of reference units, often using a map for stratification. They provide unbiased, design-consistent estimates with quantifiable uncertainty.
- **ES.** Métodos estadísticos que derivan el área u otros totales poblacionales a partir de una muestra probabilística de unidades de referencia, utilizando a menudo un mapa para la estratificación. Proporcionan estimaciones insesgadas, consistentes con el diseño y con incertidumbre cuantificable.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Estimation](#estimation) — Sample-based estimators use data from a probability sample to estimate population parameters like total area.
    - [Sampling](#sampling) — The sampling design determines the properties of the sample-based estimator, such as unbiasedness and variance.
    - [Unbiased area estimates](#unbiased-area-estimates) — They rely on sample-based estimators that incorporate sampling design to remove bias from map predictions.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Area estimation → Unbiased area estimates → Sample-based estimators

<a id='sar-backscatter'></a>
### SAR backscatter — retrodispersión SAR
*phenomenon* · sources: th_remote_sensing · th_data_sources
- **EN.** The portion of the radar signal transmitted by a Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) that is reflected back to the sensor from the Earth's surface. Its intensity depends on surface properties like roughness, moisture, and structure.
- **ES.** La porción de la señal de radar transmitida por un Radar de Apertura Sintética que es reflejada de vuelta al sensor desde la superficie terrestre. Su intensidad depende de propiedades de la superficie como rugosidad, humedad y estructura.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Synthetic Aperture Radar](#synthetic-aperture-radar) — SAR backscatter measures the microwave energy returned from the ground, imaged by synthetic aperture radar.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Radar → Synthetic Aperture Radar → SAR backscatter

<a id='satellite-data-cube'></a>
### Satellite data cube — Cubo de datos satelitales
*data* · sources: th_data_cubes
- **EN.** A multi-dimensional array of satellite images organized by spatial coordinates and time, providing a consistent grid for time series analysis and machine learning.
- **ES.** Arreglo multidimensional de imágenes satelitales organizado por coordenadas espaciales y tiempo, que proporciona una cuadrícula consistente para el análisis de series temporales y el aprendizaje automático.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Satellite imagery](#satellite-imagery) — Satellite imagery is stacked along spatial and temporal dimensions to form a data cube.
    - [Data cube](#data-cube) — A data cube organizes satellite imagery into a regular spatiotemporal array.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite imagery → Data cube → Satellite data cube

<a id='soil-moisture'></a>
### Soil moisture — Humedad del suelo
*phenomenon* · sources: th_remote_sensing#sentinel-1
- **EN.** The water content held within the soil profile, a critical factor for crop growth that can be estimated from satellite data, particularly through Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) measurements.
- **ES.** El contenido de agua retenido en el perfil del suelo, un factor crítico para el crecimiento de los cultivos que puede estimarse a partir de datos satelitales, particularmente mediante mediciones de Radar de Apertura Sintética (SAR).
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Soil](#soil) — Soil moisture is the water content in the soil, affecting crop growth and remote sensing signals.
    - [Vegetation indices](#vegetation-indices) — Vegetation indices help infer soil moisture by monitoring plant water stress indirectly.
    - [Microwave](#microwave) — Microwave remote sensing can estimate soil moisture due to its sensitivity to water content.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Radar → Microwave → Soil moisture

<a id='spectral-channels'></a>
### Spectral channels — Canales espectrales
*sensor*
- **EN.** Discrete wavelength intervals in the electromagnetic spectrum that a remote sensing sensor records, each providing a separate image band. More channels provide richer spectral information for classification.
- **ES.** Intervalos discretos de longitud de onda en el espectro electromagnético que registra un sensor de teledetección, cada uno proporciona una banda de imagen separada. Más canales proporcionan información espectral más rica para la clasificación.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Sensors](#sensors) — Each spectral channel captures reflectance in a specific wavelength range determined by the sensor's filter.
    - [Spectral bands](#spectral-bands) — Spectral channels are the discrete wavelength intervals recorded by a sensor, also called bands.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors → Spectral bands → Spectral channels

<a id='spectral-index'></a>
### Spectral index — Índice espectral
*index* · sources: ct_chile#computing-vegetation-indexes · uav_crop_growth#methods
- **EN.** A mathematical combination of two or more spectral bands, designed to enhance a specific surface property (e.g., vegetation vigor). Common indices include NDVI and NDWI.
- **ES.** Una combinación matemática de dos o más bandas espectrales, diseñada para resaltar una propiedad específica de la superficie (por ejemplo, vigor de la vegetación). Los índices comunes incluyen NDVI y NDWI.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [NDVI](#ndvi) — NDVI is a specific spectral index calculated from near-infrared and red reflectance bands.
    - [Spectral bands](#spectral-bands) — Spectral index is a mathematical combination of two or more spectral bands to enhance a specific surface property.
    - [Reflectance](#reflectance) — Reflectance values from spectral bands are used to compute spectral indices that highlight vegetation or other features.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors → Spectral bands → Spectral index

<a id='spectral-indices'></a>
### Spectral Indices — Índices espectrales
*index* · sources: th_remote_sensing#introduction-to-remote-sensing-imagery
- **EN.** Spectral indices are mathematical combinations of two or more spectral bands designed to highlight specific surface properties, such as vegetation vigor (NDVI) or water content (NDWI).
- **ES.** Los índices espectrales son combinaciones matemáticas de dos o más bandas espectrales diseñadas para resaltar propiedades específicas de la superficie, como el vigor de la vegetación (NDVI) o el contenido de agua (NDWI).
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Vegetation indices](#vegetation-indices) — Vegetation indices are spectral indices designed to highlight vegetation health and cover.
    - [Spectral bands](#spectral-bands) — Spectral indices are mathematical combinations of two or more spectral bands to highlight specific surface properties.
    - [Reflectance](#reflectance) — Spectral indices use surface reflectance values from different bands, such as NDVI from red and NIR bands.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors → Spectral bands → Spectral Indices

<a id='statistical-analysis'></a>
### Statistical analysis — Análisis estadístico
*method* · sources: index
- **EN.** The process of collecting, exploring, and presenting large quantities of data to discover underlying patterns and trends. In this handbook, it refers to generating official agricultural statistics from EO data.
- **ES.** El proceso de recolectar, explorar y presentar grandes cantidades de datos para descubrir patrones y tendencias subyacentes. En este manual, se refiere a la generación de estadísticas agrícolas oficiales a partir de datos EO.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data Analysis](#data-analysis) — Statistical analysis applies data analysis techniques to estimate quantities and test hypotheses using models.
    - [Statistical methods](#statistical-methods) — It employs statistical methods to ensure estimates are valid, unbiased, and accompanied by uncertainty measures.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling → Statistical methods → Statistical analysis

<a id='survey-vector'></a>
### Survey vector — Vector de encuesta
*data* · sources: crop_statistics_calibration
- **EN.** A vector representing the crop type observed at a pixel, with element 1 for the observed crop and 0 for others. It follows a multinomial distribution and is used in design-based estimators for crop area.
- **ES.** Un vector que representa el tipo de cultivo observado en un píxel, con el elemento 1 para el cultivo observado y 0 para los demás. Sigue una distribución multinomial y se utiliza en estimadores basados en diseño para la estimación de áreas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Survey](#survey) — A survey vector represents the crop type observed at a pixel, with element 1 for the observed crop and 0 for others.
    - [Vector](#vector) — Survey vectors encode ground observations as binary vectors for integration with satellite-derived probability vectors.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Area → Land → Field → Parcels → Polygons → Vector → Survey vector

<a id='uav-imagery'></a>
### UAV imagery — imágenes de UAV
*data* · sources: uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** Images captured from Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (drones) at low altitudes, providing very high spatial resolution (centimeter-level) for detailed agricultural monitoring, plot delineation, and crop health assessment.
- **ES.** Imágenes capturadas desde vehículos aéreos no tripulados (drones) a bajas altitudes, que proporcionan una resolución espacial muy alta (nivel centimétrico) para el monitoreo agrícola detallado, la delimitación de parcelas y la evaluación de la salud de los cultivos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [UHR CFP dataset](#uhr-cfp-dataset) — The UHR CFP dataset consists of ultra-high resolution imagery from UAVs showing cultivation parcels.
    - [CGI algorithm](#cgi-algorithm) — The CGI algorithm processes multispectral UAV imagery to compute vegetation indices for crop monitoring.
    - [DCP MTL model](#dcp-mtl-model) — It is designed for processing UAV imagery with very high spatial resolution to delineate individual fields.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → CGI algorithm → UAV imagery

<a id='un-statistical-commission'></a>
### UN Statistical Commission — Comisión de Estadística de las Naciones Unidas
*organization* · sources: introduction
- **EN.** The highest body of the global statistical system, overseeing the work of the UN Statistical Division and its expert groups. It receives reports from the UN Committee of Experts on Big Data and Data Science.
- **ES.** El órgano más alto del sistema estadístico global, que supervisa el trabajo de la División de Estadística de la ONU y sus grupos de expertos. Recibe informes del Comité de Expertos de la ONU sobre Macrodatos y Ciencia de Datos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Statistical systems](#statistical-systems) — The UN Statistical Commission oversees global statistical systems, including those for agricultural statistics.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Agricultural Statistics → Official agricultural statistics → National Statistical Offices → Statistical systems → UN Statistical Commission

<a id='utm-zone'></a>
### UTM zone — zona UTM
*data* · sources: th_data_sources · uav_agriculture_cook_islands
- **EN.** A 6-degree-wide longitudinal division of the Universal Transverse Mercator coordinate system used for accurate spatial measurements.
- **ES.** Una división longitudinal de 6 grados de ancho del sistema de coordenadas Universal Transversal de Mercator, utilizada para mediciones espaciales precisas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Military Grid Reference System](#military-grid-reference-system) — The Military Grid Reference System extends UTM zones by adding a grid of 100 km squares for precise location.
    - [Tiling system](#tiling-system) — UTM zones partition the Earth into zones for consistent mapping and tile organization.
    - [Coordinate system](#coordinate-system) — A UTM zone is a 6-degree longitudinal division of the Universal Transverse Mercator coordinate system.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Map → Basemap → Coordinate system → UTM zone


## Level 7

<a id='chlorophyll-absorption'></a>
### Chlorophyll absorption — Absorción de clorofila
*phenomenon*
- **EN.** The process by which plant chlorophyll takes in light energy, predominantly in the blue and red spectral bands, used to assess vegetation health via remote sensing.
- **ES.** El proceso por el cual la clorofila vegetal absorbe energía lumínica, predominantemente en las bandas espectrales azul y roja, utilizado para evaluar la salud de la vegetación mediante teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Spectral reflectance](#spectral-reflectance) — Chlorophyll absorption causes specific troughs in the spectral reflectance curve of vegetation.
    - [Red reflectance](#red-reflectance) — Chlorophyll strongly absorbs red reflectance, making red bands sensitive to chlorophyll content.
    - [Chlorophyll](#chlorophyll) — Chlorophyll absorption refers to the uptake of light energy by plant chlorophyll molecules.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors → Spectral bands → Red reflectance → Chlorophyll absorption

<a id='cohen-s-kappa'></a>
### Cohen's Kappa — Kappa de Cohen
*metric* · sources: cy_colombia · th_validation
- **EN.** A statistical measure of inter-rater agreement for categorical items. It quantifies the agreement between two raters (e.g., a classified map and reference data) while accounting for the agreement that would occur by chance alone.
- **ES.** Una medida estadística de acuerdo entre evaluadores para elementos categóricos. Cuantifica el acuerdo entre dos evaluadores (por ejemplo, un mapa clasificado y datos de referencia) teniendo en cuenta el acuerdo que ocurriría solo por azar.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — Cohen's Kappa quantifies agreement between two raters balancing chance, based on the confusion matrix.
    - [Chance agreement](#chance-agreement) — Cohen's Kappa corrects observed agreement for chance agreement, giving a reliability measure.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Chance agreement → Cohen's Kappa

<a id='drone'></a>
### Drone — Dron
*platform* · sources: uav_wheat_growth · uav_crop_growth
- **EN.** An unmanned aerial vehicle used for capturing very-high-resolution imagery and crop growth data over small areas.
- **ES.** Un vehículo aéreo no tripulado utilizado para capturar imágenes de muy alta resolución y datos de crecimiento de cultivos en áreas pequeñas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [UAV imagery](#uav-imagery) — Drone imagery provides ultra-high spatial resolution data for detailed crop monitoring.
    - [Unmanned aerial vehicle](#unmanned-aerial-vehicle) — A drone is another term for an unmanned aerial vehicle that captures high-resolution imagery over fields.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → CGI algorithm → UAV imagery → Drone

<a id='f1-score'></a>
### F1-score — puntuación F1
*metric* · sources: th_validation#accuracy-assessment-of-classified-images · ct_zimbabwe#accuracy-assessment
- **EN.** The harmonic mean of precision and recall, providing a single measure of a classification model's performance for a given class. F1 balances commission and omission errors.
- **ES.** Media armónica de la precisión y la exhaustividad, que proporciona una medida única del rendimiento de un modelo de clasificación para una clase determinada. La puntuación F1 equilibra los errores de comisión y omisión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Precision](#precision) — F1-score is the harmonic mean of precision and recall, providing a balanced measure of classification performance.
    - [Recall](#recall) — Recall, together with precision, forms the basis for computing the F1-score in classification evaluation.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Recall → F1-score

<a id='false-negative'></a>
### False negative — Falso negativo
*metric* · sources: th_validation · dis_china_floods
- **EN.** A pixel or sample incorrectly classified as not belonging to a class (e.g., crop or flood) when it actually does, representing an omission error.
- **ES.** Píxel o muestra clasificado incorrectamente como no perteneciente a una clase (p. ej., cultivo o inundación) cuando en realidad sí pertenece, representando un error de omisión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — A false negative occurs when a pixel truly belonging to a class is predicted as another in the confusion matrix.
    - [Omission](#omission) — False negatives correspond to omission errors, where true class pixels are missed in the map.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Omission → False negative

<a id='false-positive'></a>
### False positive — Falso positivo
*metric* · sources: th_validation · dis_china_floods
- **EN.** A pixel or sample incorrectly classified as belonging to a class (e.g., crop or flood) when it actually does not, representing a commission error.
- **ES.** Píxel o muestra clasificado incorrectamente como perteneciente a una clase (p. ej., cultivo o inundación) cuando en realidad no pertenece, representando un error de comisión.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Confusion matrix](#confusion-matrix) — A false positive occurs when a pixel predicted as a class actually belongs to another in the confusion matrix.
    - [Commission](#commission) — False positives correspond to commission errors, where pixels are incorrectly assigned to a class.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Accuracy → Validation → Accuracy assessment → Confusion matrix → Commission → False positive

<a id='ground-truth-data'></a>
### Ground-truth data — Datos de verdad terreno
*data* · sources: th_validation#introduction · crop_statistics_area#sec-introduction
- **EN.** Synonym of ground-truth. Information collected on the Earth's surface through field visits, surveys, or high-resolution image interpretation, used to calibrate and validate satellite-based classifications and models.
- **ES.** Sinónimo de verdad terreno. Información recopilada en la superficie de la Tierra mediante visitas de campo, encuestas o interpretación de imágenes de alta resolución, utilizada para calibrar y validar clasificaciones y modelos basados en satélites.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Ground-truth](#ground-truth) — Ground-truth data is the set of observations collected on the Earth's surface, used to calibrate and validate remote sensing results.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling → Survey approach → Ground-truth → Ground-truth data

<a id='leaf-area-index'></a>
### Leaf area index — Índice de área foliar
*index* · sources: uav_wheat_growth · th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The total leaf area per unit ground surface area, a key crop parameter governing photosynthesis and transpiration, estimated from remote sensing data.
- **ES.** Área foliar total por unidad de superficie del suelo, un parámetro clave del cultivo que regula la fotosíntesis y la transpiración, estimado a partir de datos de teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Vegetation](#vegetation) — Leaf area index measures the leaf area per ground unit, a key biophysical parameter of vegetation.
    - [Spectral Indices](#spectral-indices) — Leaf area index is often estimated from spectral indices like NDVI that relate to canopy density.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors → Spectral bands → Spectral Indices → Leaf area index

<a id='radar-signal'></a>
### Radar signal — Señal de radar
*phenomenon* · sources: th_remote_sensing
- **EN.** The microwave pulse transmitted by a radar satellite and the echo reflected back from the Earth's surface. Its intensity and polarization carry information about ground properties.
- **ES.** El pulso de microondas transmitido por un satélite radar y el eco reflejado desde la superficie terrestre. Su intensidad y polarización contienen información sobre las propiedades del terreno.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Microwave](#microwave) — A radar signal is a microwave pulse transmitted and received by radar satellites like Sentinel-1.
    - [SAR backscatter](#sar-backscatter) — SAR backscatter is the portion of the radar signal reflected back to the satellite sensor.
    - [Echo](#echo) — A radar signal is the transmitted pulse, and the echo is its reflection from the ground.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Radar → Synthetic Aperture Radar → SAR backscatter → Radar signal

<a id='reference-samples'></a>
### Reference samples — Muestras de referencia
*data* · sources: th_quality_control#outline · th_validation#sampling-design
- **EN.** Subset of ground observations used to train a classification model or validate its output. They must be representative, well-labeled, and independent of the model's training data for unbiased accuracy assessment.
- **ES.** Subconjunto de observaciones de campo utilizado para entrenar un modelo de clasificación o validar su resultado. Deben ser representativas, estar bien etiquetadas y ser independientes de los datos de entrenamiento del modelo para una evaluación de precisión insesgada.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Samples](#samples) — Reference samples are a subset of samples with known ground truth labels used for training or validating models.
    - [Ground-truth](#ground-truth) — Reference samples come from ground-truth data and are used to assess classification accuracy.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling → Survey approach → Ground-truth → Reference samples

<a id='sampling-frame'></a>
### Sampling frame — Marco de muestreo
*method* · sources: th_design_frames#outline
- **EN.** An ordered list or spatial structure from which a statistical sample is selected; for agricultural surveys, an area frame or list frame is used, and can be improved with Earth Observation data.
- **ES.** Una lista ordenada o estructura espacial de la cual se selecciona una muestra estadística; para encuestas agrícolas, se utiliza un marco de área o un marco de lista, y puede mejorarse con datos de observación de la Tierra.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Sampling](#sampling) — A sampling frame is the list or spatial structure from which a sample is selected.
    - [Sample design](#sample-design) — Sample design requires a sampling frame from which units are selected following a defined procedure.
    - [Robust sampling frame](#robust-sampling-frame) — A robust sampling frame is a sampling frame that is complete, accurate, and up-to-date.
    - [Population](#population) — The sampling frame must represent the entire target population for valid inference.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator → Design estimator → Sample design → Sampling frame

<a id='satellite-data'></a>
### Satellite data — Datos satelitales
*data*
- **EN.** Information collected by sensors aboard satellites orbiting Earth, including imagery and measurements of electromagnetic radiation. It is used for monitoring land, atmosphere, and oceans.
- **ES.** Información recolectada por sensores a bordo de satélites que orbitan la Tierra, incluyendo imágenes y mediciones de radiación electromagnética. Se utiliza para monitorear tierra, atmósfera y océanos.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Data](#data) — Satellite data include imagery and other measurements used as input for Earth observation analysis.
    - [Satellite](#satellite) — Satellite data are the measurements collected by sensors aboard satellites orbiting Earth.
    - [EarthData](#earthdata) — It provides access to satellite data, including Landsat and MODIS, for research and applications.
    - [Brazil Data Cube](#brazil-data-cube) — It organizes satellite data into a regular spatiotemporal array for easier analysis and time series processing.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite imagery → Data cube → Brazil Data Cube → Satellite data

<a id='som'></a>
### SOM — SOM
*method* · sources: th_quality_control
- **EN.** Self-Organizing Map: an unsupervised neural network that reduces high-dimensional data (e.g., satellite image time series) to a two-dimensional grid while preserving topological relationships. It is used for clustering, visualizing data patterns, and detecting noisy or mislabeled training samples.
- **ES.** Mapa autoorganizado: una red neuronal no supervisada que reduce datos de alta dimensión (por ejemplo, series temporales de imágenes satelitales) a una cuadrícula bidimensional preservando relaciones topológicas. Se utiliza para agrupamiento, visualización de patrones de datos y detección de muestras de entrenamiento ruidosas o mal etiquetadas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time series](#time-series) — SOM organizes input time series into clusters, preserving topological relationships for pattern discovery.
    - [Clustering Algorithm](#clustering-algorithm) — SOM is an unsupervised clustering algorithm that maps high-dimensional time series to a 2D grid.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → Cluster → Clustering Algorithm → SOM

<a id='spatiotemporal-array'></a>
### Spatiotemporal array — Arreglo espacio-temporal
*data* · sources: th_data_cubes
- **EN.** A three-dimensional array of Earth observation data with two spatial dimensions and one temporal dimension, where each cell has a fixed spatial resolution, temporal duration, and set of spectral attributes.
- **ES.** Arreglo tridimensional de datos de observación de la Tierra con dos dimensiones espaciales y una dimensión temporal, donde cada celda tiene una resolución espacial fija, una duración temporal y un conjunto de atributos espectrales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time](#time) — A spatiotemporal array organizes satellite imagery along both spatial coordinates and a time dimension, enabling analysis of change.
    - [Satellite data cube](#satellite-data-cube) — A spatiotemporal array is a data cube where layers represent time slices of registered satellite images.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite imagery → Data cube → Satellite data cube → Spatiotemporal array

<a id='spectral-temporal-signatures'></a>
### Spectral-Temporal Signatures — Firmas espectro-temporales
*phenomenon* · sources: th_lucc#the-key-role-of-time-series
- **EN.** Spectral-temporal signatures are the unique patterns of reflectance values over time for a given land cover type, capturing phenological changes and enabling classification from time series.
- **ES.** Las firmas espectro-temporales son los patrones únicos de valores de reflectancia a lo largo del tiempo para un tipo de cobertura del suelo dado, capturando cambios fenológicos y permitiendo la clasificación a partir de series temporales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Time series](#time-series) — Spectral-temporal signatures are the unique patterns of spectral indices over time for a given land cover.
    - [Spectral Indices](#spectral-indices) — Spectral-temporal signatures combine spectral indices like NDVI with time to form characteristic curves.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Images → Satellite → Remote sensing → Sensors → Satellite sensors → Spectral bands → Spectral Indices → Spectral-Temporal Signatures

<a id='statistics-production'></a>
### Statistics production — Producción de estadísticas
*method* · sources: th_alignment
- **EN.** The end-to-end process of generating official statistics, from data collection and processing to analysis, validation, and dissemination. It includes the integration of EO data into official statistical workflows.
- **ES.** El proceso integral de generar estadísticas oficiales, desde la recopilación y el procesamiento de datos hasta el análisis, la validación y la difusión. Incluye la integración de datos de observación de la Tierra en los flujos de trabajo estadísticos oficiales.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Estimation](#estimation) — Statistics production generates official estimates of crop area and yield using rigorous estimation methods.
    - [Validation](#validation) — It includes validation steps to ensure the accuracy and reliability of the produced statistics.
    - [Statistical analysis](#statistical-analysis) — It encompasses the full pipeline from data collection through analysis to dissemination of statistics.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling → Statistical methods → Statistical analysis → Statistics production

<a id='stratified-random-sampling'></a>
### Stratified random sampling — Muestreo aleatorio estratificado
*method* · sources: th_validation
- **EN.** A method dividing the population into homogeneous subgroups (strata) and then randomly sampling within each stratum. It is recommended for selecting reference data for map validation to produce unbiased estimates.
- **ES.** Método que divide la población en subgrupos homogéneos (estratos) y luego muestrea aleatoriamente dentro de cada estrato. Se recomienda para seleccionar datos de referencia para la validación de mapas con el fin de producir estimaciones insesgadas.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Sampling](#sampling) — Stratified random sampling extends simple random sampling by partitioning the population into homogeneous subgroups.
    - [Sample design](#sample-design) — Sample design often uses stratified random sampling to increase precision of estimates.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator → Design estimator → Sample design → Stratified random sampling

<a id='uncertainty'></a>
### Uncertainty — Incertidumbre
*metric* · sources: th_uncertainty · th_uncertainty
- **EN.** The degree of doubt or ambiguity in classification results, caused by classification errors, data limitations, or landscape variability.
- **ES.** El grado de duda o ambigüedad en los resultados de clasificación, causado por errores de clasificación, limitaciones de datos o variabilidad del paisaje.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classification accuracy](#classification-accuracy) — Uncertainty in classification arises from imperfect accuracy; it is quantified by metrics like confidence intervals.
    - [Prediction Probabilities](#prediction-probabilities) — Uncertainty can be expressed through prediction probabilities, which indicate how confident the model is.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Training → Machine learning → Algorithm → Classification algorithm → Prediction Probabilities → Uncertainty


## Level 8

<a id='agricultural-statistical-production'></a>
### Agricultural statistical production — Producción estadística agrícola
*method* · sources: th_design_frames · ct_chile
- **EN.** The process of generating official quantitative information on agricultural activities, including crop area, yield, and production, using surveys, administrative data, and remote sensing.
- **ES.** El proceso de generar información cuantitativa oficial sobre actividades agrícolas, incluyendo área de cultivo, rendimiento y producción, utilizando encuestas, datos administrativos y teledetección.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Agricultural Statistics](#agricultural-statistics) — Agricultural statistical production is the process of generating official agricultural statistics.
    - [Statistics production](#statistics-production) — It applies the principles of statistics production to the agricultural domain.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Samples → Classification → Design → Sampling → Statistical methods → Statistical analysis → Statistics production → Agricultural statistical production

<a id='area-frame'></a>
### Area frame — Marco de área
*statistic* · sources: crop_statistics_regression
- **EN.** A sampling method based on dividing the land surface into contiguous, exhaustive area units (such as grid cells or segments), from which a probability sample is selected. It is used to estimate land cover proportions and crop areas without relying on pre-existing farmer lists.
- **ES.** Método de muestreo que divide la superficie terrestre en unidades de área exhaustivas y contiguas (como celdas de cuadrícula o segmentos), de las cuales se selecciona una muestra probabilística. Se utiliza para estimar proporciones de cobertura del suelo y áreas de cultivo sin depender de listas preexistentes de agricultores.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Grid](#grid) — Area frames use a grid to partition the land into contiguous cells for random sampling.
    - [Sampling frame](#sampling-frame) — An area frame is a sampling frame based on exhaustive area units like grid cells.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator → Design estimator → Sample design → Sampling frame → Area frame

<a id='list-frame'></a>
### List frame — Marco de lista
*method* · sources: crop_statistics_calibration
- **EN.** A sampling method where the population of agricultural holdings or parcels is enumerated in a list (often from a census), and a sample is selected from that list. It typically provides one georeferenced centroid per parcel without direct area measurement.
- **ES.** Un método de muestreo donde la población de explotaciones agrícolas o parcelas se enumera en una lista (a menudo de un censo) y se selecciona una muestra de esa lista. Por lo general, proporciona un centroide georreferenciado por parcela sin medición directa del área.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Sampling frame](#sampling-frame) — A list frame is a sampling frame that enumerates all agricultural holdings or parcels in a list.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator → Design estimator → Sample design → Sampling frame → List frame

<a id='sampling-strategies'></a>
### Sampling strategies — Estrategias de muestreo
*method* · sources: th_validation#sampling-design
- **EN.** Plans for selecting a subset of units from a population to make inferences; common designs include stratified random sampling to ensure representative coverage of all classes.
- **ES.** Planes para seleccionar un subconjunto de unidades de una población para hacer inferencias; los diseños comunes incluyen el muestreo aleatorio estratificado para asegurar una cobertura representativa de todas las clases.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Design](#design) — They include design-based approaches like stratified random sampling to reduce bias.
    - [Sampling](#sampling) — Sampling strategies are plans for selecting units from a population to estimate characteristics.
    - [Stratified random sampling](#stratified-random-sampling) — Stratified random sampling is a common strategy that divides the population into homogeneous strata.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator → Design estimator → Sample design → Stratified random sampling → Sampling strategies

<a id='strata'></a>
### Strata — Estratos
*statistic* · sources: th_validation · crop_statistics_area
- **EN.** Homogeneous subgroups of a population created for sampling, within which random samples are drawn to increase estimate precision and reduce variance.
- **ES.** Subgrupos homogéneos de una población creados para el muestreo, dentro de los cuales se extraen muestras aleatorias para aumentar la precisión de la estimación y reducir la varianza.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Classes](#classes) — Strata are often defined by land cover classes to improve sampling efficiency.
    - [Stratified random sampling](#stratified-random-sampling) — Strata are homogeneous subgroups created for stratified random sampling.
    - [Population](#population) — Strata partition the population into distinct, non-overlapping groups.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator → Design estimator → Sample design → Stratified random sampling → Strata


## Level 9

<a id='agricultural-holding'></a>
### Agricultural holding — Explotación agrícola
*statistic* · sources: crop_statistics_calibration · th_alignment
- **EN.** An economic unit of agricultural production under single management, comprising all livestock and all land used wholly or partly for agricultural purposes, regardless of tenure or size.
- **ES.** Unidad económica de producción agrícola bajo una sola dirección, que comprende todo el ganado y todas las tierras utilizadas total o parcialmente para la agricultura, independientemente de la tenencia o el tamaño.
- **Prerequisites / Prerrequisitos:**
    - [Parcels](#parcels) — An agricultural holding may consist of multiple parcels, all under unified economic management.
    - [Agriculture](#agriculture) — An agricultural holding is a single management unit engaged in agricultural production.
    - [List frame](#list-frame) — List frames rely on a list of agricultural holdings from administrative registers or census data.
- **Lineage / Linaje:** Data → Statistics → Estimates → Estimation → Estimator → Design estimator → Sample design → Sampling frame → List frame → Agricultural holding
